Ka nak nad', Beṉ' Bseḻ' Chioza' Yell-lioni, wit beṉ' nad' ka na Cho'a Xtill' Chioza'. Per nyesh'laz gak c̱he beena' gone' nad' lo na' beṉ'ka'. Naklan wen sheḻ'ka' bi golje'.
Na' shlak chaogake', bex̱' Jesúza' yetxtila' na' bi'e Chioza' yeḻ' chox̱ken, na' bxoxje'n na' bi'en ḻegake', chi'e: ―Ḻi gao dga. Ḻennan' kwerp c̱ha'ni.
Na' bex̱ee kopa', na' bi'e Chioza' yeḻ' chox̱ken na' bdie'n lawe'ka' na' yog'ḻoḻgake' weejgake' daa yollan.
Na' chi'e ḻegake': ―Ḻennan' xc̱hen'na' daa gon ka gak ḻi dii koba' bc̱heb Chioza' gone'. Na' ḻaljan kwenc̱he gaklenan beṉ' zan.
Dii ḻi nia' le', bichga yeej' x̱is uvana' ax̱t ki illin lla yeeja'n gana' chṉabia' Chioza'.
Na' ka biyoll beḻgake' be'la'ogake' Chioza', na'ch wyajgake' lo Yaa Olívoza'.
Na' che' Jesúza' ḻegake': ―Yog'le le' kwej yic̱hjle nad'. Ḻa' Cho'a Xtill' Chioza' nan: “Wit' beena' chap xil'ka', na' guesles xil'ka' chape'.”
Per kat' ba biban' ladj beṉ' wetka', na' yiyaa Galileana' lljalez' le'.
Na' che' Pédrona'ne': ―Ḻa'kzi yog' beṉ'ki c̱hooṉlall'gake' li', nad' bi gon' ka'.
Na' che' Jesúza'ne': ―Dii ḻi nia' li', ṉaanyel ka zi' kwell teza' de wchop shii, shoṉ shii wi'o dill' nan bi nombi'o nad'.
Na' zeyid Pédrona' chi'ene': ―Ḻa' guetlentia' li', biga iṉia' bi nombi'a li'. Na' yog'zgake' che'gake'ne' ka'.
Na' wyajgake' to latj gana' le Getsemaní, na' che' Jesúza' beṉ'ka' nakgake'ne' txen: ―Nizə ḻi kwe' shlak llje'ḻwill' Chioza'.
Na' bc̱hi'e Pédrona', Jacóbona', na'ch Juanna', na' wzoloe' chakyeshile' na'ch chakchgaile' dii wal inlleb.
Na' chi'e ḻegake': ―Ax̱t chaklikazid' lii guettia' daa ḻe chakyeshii yic̱hjlall'dawaani. Ḻi igaaṉ nizə na' bi guesle.
Na' wzee zi lat' kwite'ka', na' bc̱hek' xibe'na' lo yona' na' be'ḻwille' Chioza' chi'ene' shi wak ten ka'zə daa wtiḻe'.
Na' chi'e: ―X̱adawaa, aga bi dii lallj c̱ho' li' de. Bislagach nad' lawi dga ba zoa idiḻ illag'. Per aga gak ka cheenid', san gak ka cheenilo' li'.
Na' biyaje' gana' lle'gake' na' ble'ile' ba chesgake'. Na' chi'e Pédrona': ―Simón, ¿Aba cheson'? ¿Abikzə bchejlat'gailo' ḻa'c̱h' tgor bi gueso'?
Bi guesle, ḻi we'ḻwill Chioza' kwenc̱he bi we'zle latj gon beli chenna' le' gan. Aga ki cheeni yic̱hjlall'do'chona' gonchon per beli chenna' bi chizoin.
Na' wyaje' sto shii jeḻwille' Chioza', na' toz ka golle'ne'.
Na' ka billine' gana' lle'gake', na' bizle'ile' chizesgake', ḻa' jalawe'ka' bi chizoyin bishgala'. Na' bibi billelgakile' ye'gake'ne'.
Na' ka billine' de wyoṉ shii, chi'e ḻegake': ―¿Ani cheskzle? Ba gok. Ba bllin gor nad', Beṉ' Bseḻ' Chioza' Yell-lioni, gak' lo na' beṉ' saaxyaka'.
Ḻi c̱has. Ḻi sho'. Ba za' beena' gone' nad' lo na'gake'.
Ni choe'te Jesúza' dill' ka bllin Juda', beena' wlen beṉ'ka' shlliṉ, lene' beṉ' zan beṉ'ka' bseḻ' bx̱ozka' chṉabia' len beṉ'ka' chli' chsedi leya' na'ch beṉ' golka' chṉabia', nox̱'gake' spad, na' no yag.
Na' Juda', beena' bene'ne' lo na' beṉ'ka', ba be'le' dill', chi'e: ―Beena' wnop', ḻen' gox̱'le, na' wc̱he'lene'.
Na' ka bllingake', jabiguee lao Jesúza' na' chi'ene': ―¡Maestro! Na'ch bnope'ne'.
Na' lii bex̱'tegake' Jesúza' bc̱he'gake'ne'.
Na' to beena' len na' wleje' spad c̱he'na' bc̱hogue' shḻaa nag xmos bx̱oz choo bx̱oz xenna'.
Na' che' Jesúza' ḻegake': ―¿Berac̱he za'zle nox̱'le no spad no yag kwenc̱he gox̱'le nad' ka to no beṉ' wban?
Yog' lla wzoa' ladjlena' bli' bsedid' ḻoo yoodo'na', na' biga bex̱'le nad'. Per chonan byen gak ka na Cho'a Xtill' Chioza'.
Na' yog'ḻoḻ beṉ'ka' ben Jesúza' txen wchooṉlall'gake'ne' na' bxoṉjgake'.
Na' to bi' xkwid' nob' ḻe' ndobb' to lech'. Na' ka bex̱'gake'b'
bsam' lechaa ndobb' na' bxoṉjb' gaḻ'yidzb'.
Na' jwa'gake' Jesúza' lao bx̱oz choo bx̱oz xenna', na' bdi'a yog'ḻoḻ bx̱ozka' chṉabia' na' beṉ' golka' chṉabia' na'ch beṉ'ka' chli' chsedi leya'.
Na' zit' zit'lə jano Pédrona'ne' bllintie' lesh' lill bx̱oz choo bx̱oz xenna'. Na' wche'lene' beṉ'ka' chap yoodo'na' chbillgake' cho'a yi'na'.
Na' bx̱ozka' chṉabia' na' yog'ḻoḻ beṉ'ka' chṉabia' beṉ' Israelka' lle' na' chiyiljyollgake' ga si' sengake' kwenc̱he wc̱hoglogake' c̱he Jesúza' guete', per bi bllel dii gao xya c̱he'.
Ḻa'kzi beṉ' zan chiya de wxiye' che'gake' c̱he', bi bidiḻi cho'a dillaa choe'gake'.
Baḻgake' wzolla'gake' chziye'gake' na' chaogake' xya c̱he', che'gake':
―Neto' ba beninto' ne': “Nad' wc̱hiṉj yoodo'ni dga ben beṉ' yell-lioki. Na' ka gak shoṉ lla yiḻis' ston na' aga beṉ' yell-lionichan gone'n.”
Na' ḻa'kzi wxiye'gake', bi bidiḻi cho'a xtilleeka'.
Na' bx̱oz choo bx̱oz xenna' wzollee ladj beṉ'ka' na' chi'e Jesúza': ―¿Abikz bi iṉo' c̱heyi dga na beṉ'ki c̱ho'?
Na' Jesúza' wzie' lliz bibi gollkze'. Na' bx̱oz choo bx̱oz xenna' chizi'ene': ―¿Alin' Crístona', Xiiṉ Chioza'?
Na' che' Jesúza'ne': ―Awe, nadaan. Na' ile'ile nad', Beṉ' Bseḻ' Chioza' Yell-lioni, chi'a de shḻi c̱he Chioza', beṉ' yeḻ' wak choo beṉ' yeḻ' wak xenna', na' ḻekzka' ile'ile' zizaa ladj bejka' ze xan yabana'.
Na' bx̱oz choo bx̱oz xenna' bsho' bc̱hez' xe'na' kwenc̱he chli'n nan ḻe chllee. Na' chi'e: ―Bich chyalljicho beṉ' gawe' xya c̱he beeni.
Kwinle ba benile ka chṉie' c̱he Chioza'. ¿Nakra gonchon? Na' yog'ḻoḻgake' bc̱hoglogake' c̱he' nan chiyaḻ' guete'.
Na' baḻgake' wzologake' chlla'gake'ne' x̱eneeka'. Na' bsejgake' jalawe'na' na'ch chgap' chball'gake'ne', na' che'gake'ne': ―Wnashki, non bet li'. Na' beṉ'ka' chap yoodo'na' wdap'gake' x̱ague'na'.
Na' Pédrona' zie' lesh' chyoona' de lli'lə ka bllin to noolə, beṉ' nak xmos bx̱oz choo bx̱oz xenna'.
Na' ka ble'ile' Pédrona' chbille' cho'a yi'na', na' wzie' chwie'ne' chi'e: ―Lenon' nako' txen Jesús, beṉ' Nazareta'.
Na' bi bc̱heb Pédrona', san chi'e: ―Bi nombi'a beena', ni bi ṉezid' bi dillaan choo. Na' bicheje' na' jazie' cho'a leeja'. Na' wchell to tez.
Na' ble'i noola'ne' sto shii, na' golle' beṉ'ka' sto: ―Beenin lene' beṉ'ka' nak Jesúza' txen.
Na' sto shii bi bc̱hebe' nake'ne' txen. Na' ka gok zi shloll, beṉ'ka' lle' na' gollgake'ne' sto shii: ―Dii ḻi lenon' nako'ne' txen, ḻa' nakbia' nako' beṉ' Galilea.
Na' Pédrona' wzoloe' chone' zṉia, chi'e: ―Chioza' gone' yeḻ' zi' c̱ha' shi chziye'zan nia' bi nombi'ane'.
Na' katena' lii wchellte teza' de wchop shii. Na' jadini Pédrona' daa goll Jesúza'ne': “Ka zi' kwell teza' de wchop shii, na' gak shoṉ shii bi wc̱hebo' shi nombi'o nad'.” Na' wzoloe' chbelle'.
Na' ka wyeeni' bidi'a bx̱ozka' chṉabia' len beṉ' golka' chṉabia', na' beṉ'ka' chli' chsedi leya' na'ch yog'ḻoḻ beṉ'ka' chṉabia'gake' yell Israela'. Na' bc̱hejgake' Jesúza' jwa'gake'ne' lao Pilátona'.
Na' wṉabi Pilátona'ne', chi'e: ―¿Alin' nako' beṉ' wṉabia' c̱he beṉ' Israelka'? Na' che' Jesúza'ne': ―Kan' ba wno'.
Na' bx̱ozka' chṉabia' dii zan dii chaogake' xya c̱he'.
Na' che' Pilátona'ne' sto shii: ―¿Abibi iṉakzo'? Bwialat', dii zan dii chaogake' xya c̱ho'.
Na' bibi goll Jesúza'ne'. Na' bibani Pilátona' daa bibi golle'ne'.
Na' kat' chaḻ' lṉina', Pilátona' chisane' to beṉ'ka' nseje' lillyana', beena' iṉab beṉ' yellka' wsane'.
To beṉ' le Barrabás die' lillyana' len beṉ'ka' benlene' xyana' daa bx̱egake' wdiḻa'.
Na' bdi'a bllag beṉ' yellka', na' che'gake' Pilátona' gone' ka chonkze' yog' yiz.
Na' che' Pilátona' ḻegake': ― ¿Acheenile yisan' beṉ' wṉabia' c̱heleni, le' nakle beṉ' Israel?
Ḻa' chakbe'ile' nan bx̱ozka' chṉabia' daa chakxe'zgakile'nen' jwa'gake'ne' lawe'na'.
Na' bx̱ozka' chṉabia' bta bṉegake' beṉ'ka' lle' na' kwenc̱he iṉabgake' yisane' Barrabáza'.
Na' che' Pilátona' ḻegake': ―Na' bera cheenile' gonid' beena' nale nake' beṉ' wṉabia' c̱hele, le' beṉ' Israel.
Na' besyaagake' che'gake': ―¡Bdee ḻee yag cruza'!
Na' che' Pilátona' ḻegake': ―¿Bera dii malan' bene'? Na' zizikli besyaagake' che'gake': ―¡Bdee ḻee yag cruza'!
Na' daa goklall' Pilátona' yigaaṉe' wen lao beṉ'ka' lle' na', bisane' Barrabáza'. Na' bene' mandad wit c̱hingake' Jesúza', na'tech bene'ne' lo na' beṉ'ka' wda'gake'ne' ḻee yag cruza'.
Na' bc̱he' soldadka' Jesúza' lesh' chyoona' gana' chon Pilátona' yeḻ' josc̱hisa', na' biti'a bishaggake' yog' soldadka' lle' na'.
Na' bwakwgake'ne' to lech' xṉa, na' bengake' to bxooṉ de xis yesh' na' bllingake'n yic̱hje'na' ka to corona.
Na' wzologake' chosyaagake' nagake': ―¡Soashga beṉ' wṉabia' c̱he beṉ' Israelka' mbalaz!
Na' wdingake' xisa' yic̱hje'na', na' bllaa x̱eneeka' ḻe', na' bc̱hek' xibe'ka' lawe'na' bengake' ka beṉ' chgwee balaaṉ.
Ka biyoll btitjgakile'ne', bikwasgake' lech' xṉana' daa bx̱oagake' kolleena' na' biwakwgake'ne' xe'na'kzə. Na' wlejgake'ne' kwenc̱he lljada'gake'ne' ḻee yag cruza'.
To beṉ' yell Cirene lie' Simón, x̱a Alejándrona' na' Rúfona', zizee lyix̱aa. Na' ka billague' ḻegake', bengake' byen bi'e yag cruz c̱he Jesúza'.
Na' bc̱he'gake' Jesúza' latja' le Gólgota, na' zejin: Latj c̱he llit yic̱hj beṉ' wet.
Na' bshabgakile'ne' vino daa nc̱hix̱ə mírrana', per bi weeje'n.
Na' bda'gake'ne' ḻee yag cruza'. Na' soldadka' bengake' to wyitj kwenc̱he yiḻaagake' xe'na' na' ikaagake' daa yidoḻ' to togake'.
Na' chida ga kana' bda'gake'ne' ḻee yag cruza'.
Na' yic̱hj yag cruz c̱he'na' bda'gake' to dii cho'en dill' bic̱he nda'gake'ne' ḻee yag cruza', nan: “Beenin beṉ' wṉabia' c̱he beṉ' Israelka'.”
Na' bda'lengake'ne' c̱hop beṉ' wban, toe' wda' kwite' de shḻina', na' stoe' kwite' de robesa'.
Na' billinin ka na Cho'a Xtill' Chioza' daa nan: “Ble'gakilene' ka to beṉ' mal.”
Na' beṉ'ka' chde na', chṉeḻegakile'ne', na' chta yic̱hje'ka' che'gake': ―¡Lin' wnazo' yic̱hiṉjo' yoodo'na' na' lo shoṉ llazə yiyono'n,
bislashki kwino' na' biyetj ḻee yag cruza'!
Na' ḻekzka' chon bx̱ozka' chṉabia' len beṉ'ka' chli' chsedi leya', chṉeḻegakile'ne', che'gake': ―Beṉ' yoblə gok bisle', na' bi chak yisla kwine'.
Shi leile' ḻen' Crístona', beṉ' wṉabia' c̱hechona', cho' beṉ' Israel, yiyetjshkile' ḻee yag cruza' ṉaa kwenc̱he ile'teicho na' shajḻe'cho c̱he'. Na' ax̱t len beṉ'ka' da'lene' ḻee yag cruza' chṉeḻegakile'ne'.
Ka bllin gobill, doxen yell-liona' bic̱hoḻ, bllinte chida shoṉ.
Na' chida shoṉ besyaa Jesúza' zillj, chi'e: ―Eloí, Eloí, ¿lama sabactani? ―na' zejin: Chios c̱ha', Chios c̱ha', ¿bic̱he ba wlej yic̱hjzo' nad'?
Na' baḻ beṉ'ka' lle' na' bengakile' daa wne' na' che'gake': ―Ḻi wzenag, ba chaxe' Elíaza'.
Na' zejdo toe' na' bḻeeje' to dii chzi' nisa' gana' yollə vino daa zic̱hj zḻa' na' bzoe'n to lo xis kwenc̱he bzoe'n cho'ena' x̱ope'n, na' chi'e: ―Jwayishkile'na', wwiashkicho shi wid Elíaza' yiḻetje'ne'.
Na' besyaadia Jesúza', na'ch wite'.
Na' ka wite', lechaa ze ḻoo yoodo'na' bcheza'n gokan c̱hoplə.
Na' beena' chṉabia' soldadka' zie' lao Jesúza', ka benile' besyee na' ble'ile' ka gok wite', na' chi'e: ―Dii ḻi beenin Xiiṉ Chioza'.
Ḻekzka' zi baḻ noolka' lle'gake' de zit'lə chwiagake'. Na' ladje'ka' len María beṉ' Magdálana', na' Saloména', na'ch María, beena' nak x̱na' Joséna' len Jacóbona', beṉ' neshaa.
Noolkin wnogake' Jesúza' na' goklengake'ne' kana' zoe' gana' mbani Galileana'. Na' ḻekzka' len zanch noolka' beṉ'ka' wyajlengake'ne' Jerusalénna'.
Na' llana' gok ka' nakan llana' chsini'a beṉ' Israelka' c̱he llana' chombaaṉgake'. Na' ka goḻ,
bllin José beṉ' Arimatéana', beena' nak txen beṉ'ka' chṉabia' beṉ' Israelka', na' lene' none' lez beena' wseḻ' Chioza' iṉabi'e. Na' biyaxjile' wyaje' lao Pilátona' jaṉabe' lsens yiḻetje' kwerp c̱he Jesúza'.
Na' bibani Pilátona' daa ba wite'. Na' goxe' beena' chṉabia' soldadka' kwenc̱he iṉabilene' shi dii ḻikzan ba witen'.
Na' ka che' beena' chṉabia' soldadka' ba wite' na' wxenlallee, na' bi'e lsens biḻetj Joséna' kwerp c̱he'na'.
Na' wxi' Joséna' to lech' de lino na' biḻetje' kwerp c̱he Jesúza' na' bitobe'ne' lechaa. Na' jḻo'ene' to ḻoo blej, na' bisejile'n to yaj xen.
Na' María beṉ' yell Magdálana', na' María, xṉa' Joséna', chwiayeṉ'gake' gana' jḻo'ene'.
Na' ka wde lla sabda', llana' chombaaṉ beṉ' Israelka', María beṉ' Magdálana' len Saloména', na'ch María, x̱na' Jacóbona', wxi'gake' diika' chḻa' zix̱ kwenc̱he wlla'gake'n kwerp c̱he Jesúza'.
Na' lla nech c̱he xmanna', shinzə chla' wbilldo'na', wyajgake' cho'a ba c̱he'na'.
Na' ka zejgake' che' ljwellgake': ―¿Nora gaklen cho' wkwase' yaja' daa chi' cho'a ba c̱he'na', lla?
Per ka bllingake', ble'gakile' bich chi' yaj xenna' cho'a bana'.
Na' ka wyoogake' ḻoo bana', ble'gakile' chi' to beṉ' xkwid' de shḻi c̱he bana' nakwe' to lech' llyish dii toṉ. Na' ḻe blleb noolka'.
Na' chi'e ḻegake': ―Bi illeble. Le' chiyiljle Jesús, beṉ' Nazareta', beena' bda'gake' ḻee yag cruza'. Ba biban beena', bich zoe' ni. Ḻi wwiakachi gana' wdix̱jgake'ne'.
Ḻi yiyaj lao beṉ'ka' nakgake'ne' txen na' len lao Pédrona', na' ḻi lljayellgake': “Ba ziyaje' zjaleze' le' Galileana', na' na' yile'ile'ne' sto shii, kon ka wne' le'.”
Na'ch bichej noolka' ḻoo bana' ziyajdogake' ax̱t chxiztitgake' daa ḻe chllebgake'. Na' kono bi gollgake' daa ḻe bllebgake'.
Na' ka biban Jesúza' ladj beṉ' wetka' lla nech c̱he xmanna' shzildo', zigaate bli'lawe' María beṉ' yell Magdálana', beena' bibej Jesúza' gall dii x̱iw'ka'.
Na' Maríana' wyaje' lao beṉ'ka' wdalen Jesúza' txen. Na' ka blline' lawe'ka' ḻe chakyesh'gakile' na' chbellgake', na' golle' ḻegake' ba biban Jesúza'.
Na' ka beni beṉ'ki mban Jesúza' na' ba ble'teyi Maríana'ne', bi wyajḻe'gake'.
Ka biyoll gok ka', c̱hop beṉ'ka' nak Jesúza' txen ngoogake' nez zejgake' lyix̱aa, na' bli'lawe' ḻegake' na' nake' nlla'lə.
Na' biyajgake' gana' lle' beṉ'ka' sto, jayellgake' ḻegake' ba ble'gakile'ne', na' ni c̱hegake' bi wyajḻe'gake'.
Na' wdetech, bli'lao Jesúza' beṉ'ka' shnej shlak chi'gake' chaogake'. Na' bsheshlene' ḻegake' daa bi chajḻe'gake' na' daa nakgake' lall'do' c̱hec̱h, ḻa' bi wyajḻe'gake' c̱he beṉ'ka' ble'gakile'ne' ka wde bibane'.
Na' chi'e ḻegake': ―Ḻi shaj doxen yell-lioni, ḻi lljtix̱je'i yog'ḻoḻ beṉ' dill' wen dill' kob c̱ha'na'.
Beena' shajḻe' na' c̱hoe' nisa', gat' yeḻ' mban c̱he' zejḻi kaṉi, san beena' bi shajḻe', c̱hogbi'a kwiayee.
Na' diikin gon beṉ'ka' nonḻilall' nad': wc̱hingake' lia'na' yibejgake' dii x̱iwaa yoo beṉ'; na' iṉegake' dill' kob dii bi nombia'gake';
na' shi gonzin gox̱'gake' no beḻ wa yeejgake' dii nak yierb, aga bi gakgakile'. Na' ḻekzka' wx̱oa neeka' yic̱hj beṉ' we'ka' na' yiyakgakile'.
Ka biyoll bshaljlene' ḻegake', X̱ancho Jesúza' biyepe' yabana' na' jachi'e kwit Chioza' shḻaa de shḻina'.
Na' beṉ'ka' nakgake'ne' txen wyajgake' doxen jtix̱je'gake' cho'a xtilleena' na' X̱ancho Jesúza' goklene' ḻegake' bengake' yeḻ' wakka' kwenc̱he wyajḻe' beṉ' dillaa be'gake' nakan dii ḻi.
Beṉ' zan ba goklall'gake' wzejgake' to to diika' ba gok ladjnto'ni
kon ka wna beṉ'ka' bli' bsedi neto', beṉ'ka' ble'gakile' daa gok dezd nech na' gok lo na'gake' be'gake'n dill'.
Na' ka'kz nad', ba wṉabyoll' nakyeṉ'an gok dezd nech. Na' chakid' nakan wen wzej' li', Teófilo, kon ka gok to to diiki,
kwenc̱he iṉezilo' daa ba bli' bsedgakile' li' nakan dowalj dii ḻi.
Kana' chṉabia' rey Heródeza' gana' mbani Judeana' wzoa to beṉ' wlie' Zacarías, goke' toz bx̱ozka' nonlen dii Abíaza'. Na' xoole', Elizabeta', ḻekzka' goke' xiiṉ dia c̱he dii bx̱oz Aarónna'.
Na' c̱hop xooltie' chongake' wen lao Chioza', na' chongake' yog'ḻoḻte daa nllie' bia'.
Na' aga no xiiṉgake' wzoa daa nak Elizabeta' nool will; na' ba naktegake' beṉ' gol.
Na' to shii ka bidoḻ' bx̱ozka' nak Zacaríaza' txen gongake' xshin Chioza' daa nak lo na'gake',
bengake' to wyitj, ka yoologake' chongake', kwenc̱he got'bia' noe' yidoḻ' lljḻo' llen yala' ḻoo lill xḻatj X̱ancho Chioza'. Na' bidoḻ' Zacaríaza' gone'n.
Na' shlak chgwee llen yala' ḻoo yoodo'na', beṉ' zan bgaaṉ chyoolə choe'ḻwillgake' Chioza'.
Na' bli'lao to anjl c̱he X̱ancho Chioza' Zacaríaza', na' anjla' zie' shḻaa de shḻina' gana' chzeygake' yala'.
Ka ble'i Zacaríaza' anjla', bikzə bi billel-lallee gone' daa ḻe bllebe'.
Na' anjla' chi'ene': ―Bi illebo' Zacarías, ḻa' Chioza' ba bzenague' daa chṉabilo'ne', na' xoolo' Elizabeta' sane' to xiiṉo' na' wsi'ob' Juan.
Na' yibachgailo' kat' galjb', na' ḻekzka' beṉ' zan yibayi,
ḻa' xiiṉo'na' gakb' to beṉ' zakii lao Chioza'. Bi chiyaḻ' wnix̱b' vino wa bichlə dii gonan ka sollib', na' Espíritu Sántona' soloe' iṉabi'e yic̱hjlall'do'baa ka zi' galjləb'.
Na' yigoob' beṉ' zan xiiṉ dia c̱he Israela' lo xṉez Chioza', beena' nak X̱angake'.
Na' kwialob' lao X̱anchona', na' soalen Espíritu c̱he Chioza' ḻeb' ka wzoalene' Elíaza', na' gapb' yeḻ' wak ka daa wdape'. Na' ye'b' beṉ'ka' bi zoalen xiiṉe'ka' wen, yizoagake' mbalaz. Na' gom' ka wzenag beṉ'ka' bi cheeni wzenaggake' dill' sin' c̱he beṉ'ka' zej shḻi lao Chioza'. Na' diikin gom' kwenc̱he kat' za' X̱anchona' na' gonḻilall'gake'ne'.
Na'ch che' Zacaríaza' anjla': ―¿Nakra gak iṉezid' shi lekzilo'n?, ḻa' ba nak' beṉ' gol na' ḻekzka' nool c̱ha'na'.
Na'ch che' anjla'ne': ―Nadaan anjl Gabriela', na' chon' xshin Chioza', na' kwine' bseḻee nad' kwenc̱he zaa zidnia' li' dill' wenni.
Na' daa bi wyajḻi'o daa wnia' li', idap shi'ona'. Bich gak iṉio' ax̱t kat'ch illin lla gak yog' dga ba wnia' li'.
Na' beṉ'ka' lle' chyoolə chbezgake' yichej Zacaríaza', gokllejgakile' daa wllaile' ḻoo yoodo'na'.
Na' ka bicheje' bich chak iṉie', seṉzə chone', na' gokbe'gakile' nan nochodan' bli'lao ḻe' ḻoo yoodo'na'.
Na' ka biyoll ben Zacaríaza' daa llia bia' gone' yoodo'na', na'ch biyaje' lille'na'.
Na' ka wde gok diiki, na' bia' xoole', Elizabeta'. Na' lao gay' beo' bichkzə ga bcheje', na' wne':
“X̱ancho Chioza' ba goklene' nad' kwenc̱he bich sia' yeḻ' zto' lao beṉ'.”
Na' ka gok x̱op beo' noa' Elizabeta', bseḻ' Chioza' anjla' le Gabriel yella' le Nazaret daa llia gana' mbani Galileana',
gana' zoa to nool wew' lie' María. Na' Maríana' ba nakan wshagna'lene' to beṉ' le José, na' Joséna' nake' xiiṉ dia c̱he dii rey Davina'.
Na' wyoo anjla' gana' zoa Maríana' na' chi'ene': ―¡Chwap' li' chiox, nool, beṉ' ba goklen Chioza' kwenc̱he gak dii wen c̱ho'! X̱anchona' zoalene' li', na' ba benḻeeyche' li' aga ka yog'ḻoḻte nool.
Na' Maríana' bibanile' daa golle'ne' ka', na' gokile' berac̱he naz beeni nad' ka'.
Na' che' anjla' ḻe': ―Bi illebo' María, ḻa' Chioza' ba wleje' li' kwenc̱he gone' to dii wen c̱ho'.
Na' ṉaa woo to bdo' na' kat' galjb' na' wsi'ob' Jesús.
Na' gakb' to beṉ' zakii na' ye'gake'b' Xiiṉ Chios, beena' nak ḻiizelozi beṉ' choo beṉ' xen. Na' X̱ancho Chioza' gone'b' to beṉ' wṉabia' ka dii x̱ozxto'b' Davina'
kwenc̱he toshiizi iṉabia'b' le' beṉ' Israel, le' nakle xiiṉ dia c̱he dii Jacoba', na' yeḻ' wṉabia' c̱he'baa bi yiyoll yidon.
Na'ch wṉabi Maríana' anjla', chi'ene': ―¿Nakra gakz wa', lla?, ḻa' aga no beṉ' byo zoalen'.
Na'ch che' anjla' ḻe': ―Espíritu Sántona' yidsoalene' li', na' yeḻ' wak c̱he Chioza', beena' nak ḻiizelozi beṉ' choo beṉ' xen, soalenan li'. Na' bi'do'na' galj gakb' lall' na' Chioza' na' ye'gake'b' Xiiṉ Chios.
Ḻekzka' dialla c̱ho' Elizabeta' ba no'e, ḻa'kzi ba nake' beṉ' gol. Na' ḻa'kzi chaki beṉ' nake' nool will, ba gok x̱op beo' no'e.
Aga bi de dii bi chak gon Chioza'.
Na'ch che' Maríana' anjla': ―Xmos X̱ancho Chiozan' nak', na' wak gone' c̱ha' kon ka ba wno'. Na' biza' anjla' gana' zoa Maríana'.
Na' lii wza'te Maríana' wyaje' to yell dii llia yaa yao c̱he Judeana'.
Na' blline' lill Zacaríaza' na' bwape' Elizabeta' chiox.
Na' ka bwap Maríana' ḻe' chiox, gokbe'i Elizabeta' bxit' bdo'na' ḻoo ḻi'ena'. Na' wzolo wṉabia' Espíritu Sántona' ḻoo yic̱hjlall'do'ena',
na' wṉie' zillj, chi'ene': ―Chioza' ba benḻeeyche' li' ladj yog'ḻoḻ nool, na' ḻekzka' bdo' c̱ho'na'.
¿Nora nak' nad' zidwia'zə xṉa' X̱an'na' nad', lla?
Ḻa' kon ka bwapo' nad' chiox, lii bxit'te bdo' c̱ha'ni ḻoo ḻi'ani daa chibaib'.
Chakomba li' wyajḻi'o ka wna anjla', ḻa' yog' daa wna X̱anchona', aga wde bi gakan.
Na'ch wna Maríana': Do yic̱hj do lallaa choe'lawaa X̱ancho Chioza'.
Chibayi yic̱hjlall'dawaani lao Chioza', beena' chisla nad'.
Ba biyesh'lallile' nad' nak' xmose', ṉaa solo yog' beṉ' iṉe' nad': “Chakomba li'.”
Ḻa' Chioza', beena' nap yeḻ' wak choo yeḻ' wak xen, ba bene' dii wen inlleb c̱ha'. Nake' ḻiizelozi beṉ' ḻi beṉ' shao',
na' chiyesh'lallile' yog'te beṉ'ka' chall chllebgake'ne'.
Dii zakii nlleb ba benlene' yeḻ' wak c̱he'na'. Ba bc̱hiṉj bselle' yog'ḻoḻ daa nan gon beṉ'ka' chep cha'lall'.
Ba bikwase' yeḻ' wṉabia' c̱he beṉ' wṉabia'ka', na' beṉ'ka' ble'gakile' nakzi, Chioza' ba bene' ḻegake' beṉ' zakii.
Na' beṉ'ka' chbiḻ chdon, ba bzesh bzeljile' ḻegake' kon dii wen dii shao' c̱he'na', na' bilague' beṉ' wni'aka' to ka cha'gake'.
Ba goklene' cho' beṉ' Israel, cho' nakcho xmose', na' toshiizi chiyesh'lallile' cho',
kon ka bc̱hebe' gone' c̱he dii x̱ozxto'cho Abrahama' na' yog' beṉ' zizaak lo dia c̱he'na'.
Na' Maríana' bgaaṉe' ka do shoṉ beo' lill Elizabeta', na'ch bizee ziyaje' lille'na'.
Na' ka bllin lla wxan Elizabeta', wxane' to bi' byodo'.
Na'ch ka wṉezi beṉ' wlill c̱he'ka' na' beṉ' dialla c̱he'ka', wyajgake' bibalengakile'ne' daa ba biyeshii X̱ancho Chioza' ḻe'.
Na' ka gokib' to xman, jḻoogake'b' seṉ daa ne' circuncisión, na' goklall'gake' wsi'gake'b' Zacarías ka le x̱abaa.
Na' che' xṉa'baa: ―¡Bi gakan! Juanan chiyaḻ' wsi'nto'b'.
Na' gollgake'ne': ―¿Bic̱he wsi'zo'b' ka'? Ḻa' aga no dialla c̱ho' le ka'.
Na'ch bengake' seṉ kwenc̱he wṉabgakile' x̱abaa bi cheenile' wsi'e bdo'na'.
Na'ch wṉabe' to yagla'do' kwenc̱he bzeje'n, na' daa bzeje' nan: “Juanan wsi'nto'b'.” Na' yog' beṉ'ka' bibani.
Na' lii gokte biṉe Zacaríaza', na'ch wzoloe' choe'lawee Chioza'.
Na' beṉ' wlill c̱he'ka' bllebgake' ka nak daa gok, na' yog' yellka' lle' ladj yaa yao c̱he Judeana' wze dill' ka gok.
Na' yog' beṉ'ka' beni ka gok, gokgakile': ―¿Noran gak bi'do'ni, lla? Wnagake' ka', ḻa' nakbia' zoalen X̱ancho Chioza' ḻeb'.
Na' Espíritu Sántona' wṉabi'e yic̱hjlall'do' x̱ab' Zacaríaza' na' bi'e cho'a xtill' Chioza', wne':
Choe'lawaa X̱anchona', beena' nak Chios c̱hecho, cho' beṉ' Israel, ḻa' ba bide' ladjchoni, cho' nakcho beṉ' yell c̱he', kwenc̱he yisle' cho' lawi dii mala'.
Na' ba bseḻee to beṉ' nap yeḻ' wak xen yisle' cho', na' zee lo dia c̱he dii Davina', beena' gok xmose'.
Ba chak ka bc̱hebe' gone' kani'yi daa golle' dii beṉ'ka' wdix̱jee cho'a xtilleena', beṉ'ka' gok lall' nee.
Bc̱hebe' yisle' cho' lao beṉ'ka' bi chle'shii cho', na' lao yog' beṉ'ka' chakzi' chakzbani cho'.
Na' golle' dii x̱ozxto'choka' yiyeshile' ḻegake', na' bi gaḻ-lallee ka nak diika' bc̱hebe' gone'.
Ki nak daa bc̱heb Chioza' gone' c̱he dii x̱ozxto'cho Abrahama':
Bc̱hebe' yisle' cho' lao beṉ'ka' bi chle'shii cho' kwenc̱he we'la'ochone' na' bibi wwall wsheban cho',
na' gon kwincho lall' nee na' goncho ka yiyoolallile' shlak mbancho.
Na'ch Zacaríaza' chi'e bdo' c̱he'na': Na' li', xiiṉdawaa, iṉa beṉ' li' beṉ' chyix̱jee daa na Chioza', beena' nak ḻiizelozi beṉ' choo beṉ' xen. Na' kwialozego' lao X̱anchona' kwenc̱he wzenaggake' c̱he' kat' zee.
Wzenilo' beṉ' wlall c̱hechoka' daa chiyaḻ' gongake' kwenc̱he yizi'xen Chioza' saaxya c̱he'ka' na' yisle' ḻegake' bi tegake' lo yeḻ' zak'zi'na'.
Ḻa' Chios c̱hechona' chakile' cho' na' chiyesh'lallile' cho', na' wseḻee to beṉ' za' yabana' nsee to beeni' c̱he yic̱hjlall'do' beṉ' yell-lioni
kwenc̱he sho' beeni'na' ḻoo yic̱hjlall'do' beṉ'ka' chda gani nak shgasj shc̱hoḻ ni che dii mala' daa nsa' yeḻ' wit, na' wliile' cho' nez ḻi c̱he'na' na' soacho mbalaz.
Shlak bgol Juanna', ben Chioza'ne' beṉ' wal. Na' wzoe' to latj gana' bibi chashj chḻeb ax̱t ka bllin lla wzoloe' be'lene' beṉ' Israelka' cho'a xtill' Chioza'.
Kana' chṉabia' César Augústona', bene' byen ibab baḻ beṉ' lle' to to yell doxen yell-liona' gana' chṉabi'e.
Na' ka wbabgake' dii nech, beena' le Cirenio nake' gobernador c̱he Síriana'.
Na' benan byen biyaj yog' beṉ' yell c̱he c̱hegake' kwenc̱he jada' lie'ka'.
Na' daa nak Joséna' xiiṉ dia c̱he dii Davina', bizee yell Nazareta' daa llia gana' mbani Galileana', na' biyaje' yell Belénna' gana' golj dii Davina', daa llia gana' mbani Judeana'.
Na' kwenc̱he ibabgake' biyaje' yell Belénna' len Maríana', beena' ba nakan ikee. Na' Maríana' ba no'e.
Na' shlak zoagake' Belénna', bllin lla sane'.
Na' wxane' to bi' byodo' nakb' bi' nech, na' btobe'b' lechaa na' wdix̱je'b' gana' chao bayix̱'ka', ḻa' bich bi latj bllel gana' chigaaṉ beṉ'.
Na' lle'na' goljb', gaozə yell Belénna' lle' x̱oṉj beṉ' chapgake' xil' c̱he'ka'.
Na' gokx̱e to anjl c̱he X̱ancho Chioza', na' yeḻ' chey cheeni' c̱he X̱anchona' bzeeni'n gana' lle'gake', na' ḻe bllebgake'.
Na' che' anjla' ḻegake': ―Bi illeble, ḻa' zidtix̱je'id' le' dill' wen dill' koba' daa gonan ka yibachgayi yog' beṉ'.
Ḻa' ṉaa yell c̱he dii Davina' ba golj beena' yisla le' lao dii mala'. Na' ḻen' X̱ancho Crístona', beena' chbezle wseḻ' Chioza'.
Na' kwenc̱he yillelileb', ki nak gana' deb': deb' gana' chao bayix̱'ka' na' ndobb' lech'.
Na' ka biyoll goll anjla' ka', lii bllinte anjl zanch kwite'na', na' choe'la'ogake' Chioza', nagake':
¡We'la'ocho Chioza' zoa yabana'! Mbalaz beṉ'ka' zoa yell-lioni, beṉ'ka' ba bli'yi Chioza' yeḻ' goklen c̱he'na'.
Na' ka biza' anjlka' ziyajgake' yabana', na'ch che' ljwell beṉ'ka' chap xil'ka': ―Ḻi yidoshki Belénna', ḻi sho' diwiashki daa ba gok, daa ba wdix̱je'i anjl c̱he X̱anchona' cho'.
Na'ch ziyajdogake' Belénna' na' bllingake' gana' zoa Maríana' len Joséna', na' bdo'na' deb' gana' chao bayix̱'ka'.
Na' ka biyoll ble'gakile'b', na' be'gake' dill' lao beṉ' wlall c̱he'ka' daa goll anjla' ḻegake' c̱he bdo'na'.
Na' yog' beṉ'ka' beni ka wna wap xil'ka' bibangakile' ka dillaa be'gake'.
Na' Maríana' kon ka biyoll bzenague' dill'ka' na' bgaaṉan ḻoo yic̱hjlall'do'ena', na' gokile' bera zejin dga.
Na'ch ziyaj wap xil'ka' choe'la'ogake' Chioza' daa ba ben ble'gakile' yog' daa goll anjla' ḻegake'.
Na' ka gokib' to xman, wloogake'b' seṉ daa le circuncisión, na' bsi'gake'b' Jesús kon ka goll anjla' Maríana' kana' zi' weeb'.
Na' kon ka na ley c̱he dii Moiséza' gongake', wlezgake' ka bzaa llaka' bixi biyech Maríana' len bdo' c̱he'na', na'ch wyajlengake'b' Jerusalénna' kwenc̱he jengake'b' lo na' X̱ancho Chioza'.
Bengake' ka', ḻa' ley c̱he X̱anchona' nan: “Bi' byo nech c̱he yog'ḻoḻ beṉ', chiyaḻ' gongake'b' lo na' Chioza'.”
Na' jaake' je'la'ogake' X̱ancho Chioza' jengake' ka na leya' daa nan chiyaḻ' witgake' c̱hop ngolbex wa c̱hop palom.
Na' kana' jwa'gake' Jesúza' yoodo'na', zoa to beṉ' le Simeón Jerusalénna'. Nake' to beṉ' chon dii wen dii shao' na' choe'lawee Chioza', na' chbeze' batan wseḻ' Chioza' beena' gaklene' beṉ' Israelka'. Na' zoalen Espíritu Santo c̱he Chioza' ḻe'.
Na' Espíritu Sántona' ba bzenile'ne' nan aga wete' shi biṉ' ile'ile' Crístona', beena' chbezgake' wseḻ' X̱ancho Chioza' kwenc̱he iṉabi'e.
Na' Espíritu Sántona'kz bseḻeene' yoodo'na', na' na' zie' ka bllinlen x̱axṉa' Jesúza' ḻeb' kwenc̱he gongakile'b' ka na leya'.
Na'ch bḻen Simeónna' ḻeb' na' be'lawee Chioza', chi'e:
Chios c̱ha', be' latj guet' mbalaz ṉaa, ḻa' ba beno' daa bc̱hebo' gono' c̱ha', nad' nak' xmoso'.
Ḻa' ba ble'id' beena' yisla neto',
beena' ba bseḻoo lao yog'ḻoḻ beṉ' yell-lioki.
Ḻen' kwee beeni'na' ḻoo yic̱hjlall'do' beṉ'ka' bi nakgake' beṉ' Israel. Na' gone' ka neto' beṉ' Israel sho'nto' balaaṉ, neto' naknto' yell c̱ho'.
Na'ch Joséna' len xṉa'ba bibangakile' ka nak daa wna Simeónna' c̱heb'.
Na'ch wṉabi Simeónna' Chioza' gaklene' ḻegake', na' chi'e Maríana', xṉa' Jesúza': ―Ba nc̱hogbi'a Chioza' c̱he bi'do'ni gom' kwenc̱he zan beṉ' Israelka' kwiayi'gake' na' ḻekzka' zane' yila. Na' wliib' beṉ' ka nak yeḻ' wak c̱he Chioza', na' beṉ' zan iṉegake' zban c̱heb' na' bi shajḻe'gake' c̱heb',
na'ch gakbia' ka chza'lall' beṉ' ḻoo yic̱hjlall'do'eka'. Na' ka nako' li', ḻoo yic̱hjlall'do'na' gakan ka'kzə ga chaz to spad ka ile'ilo' daa illaglob'.
Na' ḻekzka' yoodo'na' zoa to nool goldo', beṉ' chyix̱jee daa che' Chioza'ne', na' lie' Ana. Nake' xiiṉ dii Fanuela' na' xiiṉ dia c̱he dii Asera'. Beṉ' xkwid'ze' bshagnee, na' gall yizchga wzoalene' beṉ' c̱he'na' ka wite'.
Nake' noolə wizeb na' ba gokile' taplaḻj tap yiz. Na' toshiizi zoe' yoodo'na', na' ka waḻ ka tella zoe' choe'lawee Chioza', na' tlizi chzoe' wbas' na' choe'ḻwille'ne'.
Na' ḻekzka' wbiguee kwite'ka' na' bi'e Chioza' yeḻ' chox̱ken daa ba bseḻee beena' gaklene' beṉ' Israelka'. Na' bi'e dill' c̱he Jesúza' lao beṉ' Jerusalénka', beṉ'ka' chbez wseḻ' Chioza' beena' yisla ḻegake' lao dii mala'.
Na' ka biyoll bengake' yog' daa nllia ley c̱he X̱ancho Chioza' bia', na'ch biyajgake' lalle'ka' daa le Nazaret daa llia gana' mbani Galileana'.
Na' Jesúza' bgolb' na' zejch gokb' bi' wal na' bi' sin', na' ḻe goklen Chioza' ḻeb'.
X̱axṉa' Jesúza' chajgake' Jerusalénna' yog' yiz kat' chaḻ' lṉi Paskwa'.
Na' ka goki Jesúza' shlliṉ yiz, wyajlengake'b' lṉina' kon ka yoologake'.
Na' ka wde lṉina' biza' x̱axṉa'baa, na' bi gokbe'gakile' bigaaṉ Jesúza' Jerusalénna'.
Gokgakile' do ladj beṉ'ka' ziyajlengake' zilem', na' kon bigootezgake' nez do lla. Na' ka biyiljgake'b' ladj beṉ' dialla c̱he'ka' na' beṉ'ka' nombia'gake'
aga billelgakile'b'. Na' bibiigake' jadiljgake'b' Jerusalénna'.
Na' ka gok shoṉə lla billelgakile'b' yoodo'na', chi'b' ladj beṉ'ka' chli' chsedi leya' chzenagb' xtilleeka' na' chṉabib' ḻegake' c̱he daa choe'gake' dill'.
Na' yog' beṉ'ka' chzenag xtill'baa chibangakile' yeḻ' chajnii c̱he'baa na' ka chilliib' xtill' beṉ'ka' chli' chsedi leya'.
Na' ka ble'i x̱axṉa'baab' bibangakile'. Na'ch che' xṉa'baa: ―Xiiṉdawaa, ¿bic̱he benzilo' neto' ka'? X̱o'ni na' nad' ba gokshejlall'chgainto' biyiljnto' li'.
Na'ch che' Jesúza' ḻegake': ―¿Bic̱he chiyiljzle nad'? ¿Abi ṉezile chiyaḻ' soa' lill X̱a'na'?
Na' aga wyajni'gakile' bi zejin daa gollb' ḻegake'.
Na'ch Jesúza' biyajlem' ḻegake' Nazareta' na' bzenagb' c̱hegake' toshiizi. Na' xṉa'baa aga goḻ-lallee diika' gok.
Na' Jesúza' zejch bgolb' na' wdapchb' yeḻ' sin', na' Chioza' bibachile'b', na' ḻekzka' bibayi beṉ' ḻeb'.
Na' ka gok shin' yiz chṉabia' César Tibériona', na' Poncio Pilátona' chṉabi'e gana' mbani Judéana', na' Heródeza' chṉabi'e gana' mbani Galileana', na' beṉ' bishee Felípena' chṉabi'e gana' mbani Ituréana' len Traconítena', na' Lisániaza' chṉabi'e gana' mbani Abilíniana',
na' Anáza' len Caifáza' nakgake' bx̱oz choo bx̱oz xen c̱he beṉ' Israelka'. Na' kana'yeṉ' wṉe Chioza' Juanna', xiiṉ Zacaríaza', kana' zoe' to latj gana' bibi chashj chḻeb.
Na'ch wyaj Juanna' jte' doxen yell-liona' de cho'a yao Jordánna' na' wdix̱je'ile' beṉ' chiyaḻ' yiyaj yilengakile' na' c̱hoagake' nis kwenc̱he yizi'xen Chioza' c̱hegake'.
Bene' kon ka bzej dii Isaíaza' gana' nan: To beṉ' gosyee latja' gana' bibi chashj chḻeb, na' iṉe': “Ḻi se kwas wzenagle c̱he X̱anchona' na' wsalj yic̱hjlall'do'leka' kat' zee.
Ḻa' ḻe' gone' ka chon beṉ' chillee ga nak xitj yao, na' ka beṉ' chc̱hiṉj yaa kwenc̱he chiḻeshe'n. Na' chiḻie' yog'ḻoḻ nez dii nyok nḻew, na' chillee xitjka' chi' lo neza'.
Na' yog'ḻoḻ beṉ' ile'gakile' ka gon Chioza' yisle' beṉ' lawi dii mala'.”
Na' beṉ' zan chllin lao Juanna' kwenc̱he wchoe' ḻegake' nisa', na'ch kat' chllingake' lawe'na', chi'e ḻegake': ―¡Le' naklikzle ka beḻ zṉia! ¿Achakile wak wxoṉjile' yeḻ' zak'zi' daa wseḻ' Chioza'?
Ḻi gon ka gakbe'i beṉ' nan dii ḻi ba biyaj bilenile'. Na' bi gakzile bibi yeḻ' zak'zi' ile'ile daa iṉazle: “Neto' naknto' xiiṉ dia c̱he dii Abrahama'.” Ni iṉia' le' ax̱t yajki wak gon Chioza' xiiṉ dia c̱he dii Abrahama'.
Yog'ḻoḻ-le shi bi chonle ka chiyoolallii Chioza' na' gak c̱hele ka chak c̱he to yag dii choe' dii zix̱ dii bi nak wen, na' lii chc̱hogtegake'n na' chzaḻ'gake'n lo yi'na'.
Na' beṉ'ka' chzenag xtill' Juanna' che'gake'ne': ―¿Beran chiyaḻ' gonnto', shka'?
Na'ch che' Juanna' ḻegake': ―Beena' de c̱hop kwe' xe', chiyaḻ' wi'e shkwe' c̱he beena' bi de c̱he'. Na' beena' de dii cheej chawe', chiyaḻ' gaolene'n beena' bi de c̱heyin.
Na' ḻekzka' bllin baḻ beṉ' wic̱hixjka' kwenc̱he wchoa Juanna' ḻegake' nisa', na' wṉabgakile'ne': ―Maestro, ¿beran chiyaḻ' gonnto', shka'?
Na'ch che' Juanna' ḻegake': ―Bi wc̱hixjle dii xenchlə ka to daa chiyaḻ' wc̱hixjle.
Na' ḻekzka' baḻ beṉ'ka' nak soldad wṉabgakile'ne': ―¿Shera neto', beran chiyaḻ' gonnto' shka'? Na'ch che' Juanna' ḻegake': ―Bi wwall wsheble beṉ' kwenc̱he ikaazle bi de c̱he', ni bi wtobilene' dii bi nak ka'. Ḻi gon banez laxjlena'.
Na' beṉ' zan yoo yic̱hjgake' ila' Crístona', beena' wseḻ' Chioza' kwenc̱he iṉabi'e, na' yog'ze' gokgakile' Juanna'ljan Crístona'.
Na' Juanna' golle' ḻegake': ―Zi' za' beena' napch yeḻ' wak xench ka nad'. Na' nad' ni bi zakaa gak' xmose' kwenc̱he wḻec̱hj' xele'na'. Nad' chchoa' le' nis daa chiyaj chilenile, san ḻen' gone' ka yidsoa Espíritu Sántona' ḻoo yic̱hjlall'do'lena', na' beṉ'ka' bi chiyaj chileni, wseḻee ḻegake' lo yi' gabiḻa'.
Na' daa gon Crístona' c̱he beṉ' chzaklebin ka daa chon beena' nox̱' yag xoz' daa chpa'ile' trígona', na' yitope' trígona' kooshaween na' wzeye' beb c̱heyinna' lo yi'na' daa biga yiyolkzə.
Kan' nak diika' bzajnii Juanna' beṉ'ka', na' dii zanch dill' dii be'lene' ḻegake' kana' bi'e dill' wen dill' kob c̱he Chioza'.
Na' Juanna' ḻekzka' bsheshlene' Heródeza', beena' wṉabia' Galileana', daa bikee Herodíaza', xool beṉ' bishee Felípena', na' c̱he bichlə dii malka' ba bene'.
Na'ch Heródeza' benche' bish' ljwell dii malka' ba bene' daa wlo'e Juanna' lillyana'.
Kana' chchoa Juanna' beṉ' nisa', len Jesúza' bchoe'n. Na' shlak choe'ḻwill Jesúza' Chioza', byalj yabana'
na' betj Espíritu Sántona' jsoalene'ne', na' ble'gakile' Espírituna' ka to palom. Na' bengakile' shii Chioza' za'n yabana', chi'e: ―Lin' nako' Xiiṉ', chakchgaid' li' na' ḻe chibaid' li'.
Na' do shichoa yizi Jesúza' ka wzoloe' bene' yog' daa llia bia' gone'. Na' yog' beṉ' wnagake' xiiṉ Josénan'. Na' Joséna' goke' xiiṉ Elína',
Elína' goke' xiiṉ Matata', Matata' goke' xiiṉ Levína', Levína' goke' xiiṉ Mélquina', Mélquina' goke' xiiṉ Jánana', Jánana' goke' xiiṉ Joséna'.
Joséna' goke' xiiṉ Matatíaza', Matatíaza' goke' xiiṉ Amóza', Amóza' goke' xiiṉ Nahuma', Nahuma' goke' xiiṉ Éslina', Éslina' goke' xiiṉ Nagaina'.
Nagaina' goke' xiiṉ Maata', Maata' goke' xiiṉ Matatíaza', Matatíaza' goke' xiiṉ Semeina', Semeina' goke' xiiṉ Joséna', Joséna' goke' xiiṉ Judána'.
Judána' goke' xiiṉ Joánana', Joánana' goke' xiiṉ Résana', Résana' goke' xiiṉ Zorobabela', Zorobabela' goke' xiiṉ Salatiela', Salatiela' goke' xiiṉ Nérina'.
Nérina' goke' xiiṉ Mélquina', Mélquina' goke' xiiṉ Ádina', Ádina' goke' xiiṉ Cosama', Cosama' goke' xiiṉ Elmodama', Elmodama' goke' xiiṉ Era'.
Era' goke' xiiṉ Josuéna', Josuéna' goke' xiiṉ Eliezera', Eliezera' goke' xiiṉ Jorima', Jorima' goke' xiiṉ Matata'.
Matata' goke' xiiṉ Levína', Levína' goke' xiiṉ Simeónna', Simeónna' goke' xiiṉ Judána', Judána' goke' xiiṉ Joséna', Joséna' goke' xiiṉ Jonánna', Jonánna' goke' xiiṉ Eliaquima'.
Eliaquima' goke' xiiṉ Meleana', Meleana' goke' xiiṉ Mainána', Mainána' goke' xiiṉ Matátana', na' Matátana' goke' xiiṉ Natánna'.
Natánna' goke' xiiṉ Davina', Davina' goke' xiiṉ Isaína', Isaína' goke' xiiṉ Obeda', Obeda' goke' xiiṉ Booza', na' Booza' goke' xiiṉ Salmónna', Salmónna' goke' xiiṉ Naasónna'.
Naasónna' goke' xiiṉ Aminadaba', Aminadaba' goke' xiiṉ Arama', Arama' goke' xiiṉ Ezroma', Ezroma' goke' xiiṉ Fáreza', Fáreza' goke' xiiṉ Judána'.
Judána' goke' xiiṉ Jacoba', Jacoba' goke' xiiṉ Isaaca', Isaaca' goke' xiiṉ Abrahama', Abrahama' goke' xiiṉ Taréna', Taréna' goke' xiiṉ Nacora'.
Nacora' goke' xiiṉ Seruga', Seruga' goke' xiiṉ Ragauna', Ragauna' goke' xiiṉ Pelega', Pelega' goke' xiiṉ Hebera', Hebera' goke' xiiṉ Sálana'.
Sálana' goke' xiiṉ Cainánna', Cainánna' goke' xiiṉ Arfaxada', Arfaxada' goke' xiiṉ Sema', Sema' goke' xiiṉ Noéna', Noéna' goke' xiiṉ Lameca'.
Lameca' goke' xiiṉ Matusalénna', Matusalénna' goke' xiiṉ Enoca', Enoca' goke' xiiṉ Jareda', Jareda' goke' xiiṉ Mahalaleela', Mahalaleela' goke' xiiṉ Cainánna'.
Cainánna' goke' xiiṉ Enóza', Enóza' goke' xiiṉ Seta', Seta' goke' xiiṉ Adánna', na' Adánna' goke' xiiṉ Chioza'.
Ka biza' Jesúza' cho'a yao Jordanna', Espíritu Sántona', beena' chṉabia' ḻoo yic̱hjlall'do'ena', bc̱hi'ene' latja' gana' bibi chashj chḻeb.
Na' na' wzoe' c̱hoa lla, na' dii x̱iwaa goklalliin kooyeḻa'n ḻe' gone' ka cheenin. Na' shlak wzoe' na' ni lat' bibi wdawe', na' ka gok c̱hoa lla, wdone'.
Na'ch che' dii x̱iwaane': ―Shi leilo' nako' Xiiṉ Chios, goll yaji yiyakan yetxtil.
Na'ch che' Jesúza': ―Cho'a Xtill' Chioza' nan: “Aga toz yeḻ' wawa' choe'n yeḻ' mban c̱he beṉec̱ha', san ḻekzka' Cho'a Xtill' Chioza' choe'n yeḻ' mban c̱hegake'.”
Na'ch ka wde, bc̱he' dii x̱iwaa Jesúza' to lo yaa sib wal, na' tolbe'do' bliin ḻe' yog' yellka' llia yell-lioni.
Na'ch che'n ḻe': ―Goṉ' li' doxen yeḻ' wṉabia'na' na' yeḻ' zakiina' daa de c̱he yog' yellki, ḻa' ba nakin c̱ha' na' wak wi'an kon no cheenid'.
Na' goṉa'n li' shi wc̱hek' xibo'na' we'lawoo nad'.
Na' che' Jesúza': ―Cho'a Xtill' Chioza' nan: “Be'la'o toz X̱ano' Chioza' na' kon daa iṉe', ḻennan' gono'.”
Na'ch ka wde, bizc̱he' dii x̱iwaa Jesúza' Jerusalénna' na' bḻepan ḻe' yic̱hj yoodo'na' gana' nakch sib wal, na' gollan ḻe': ―Shi leilo' nako' Xiiṉ Chios, lla bxit'shki ni.
Ḻa' Cho'a Xtill' Chioza' nan: Chioza' wseḻee anjl c̱he'ka' gap wwiagake' li',
na' gox̱'gake' li' kwenc̱he ki koo wc̱hewo' yajka'.
Na'ch che' Jesúza': ―Ḻekzka' na Cho'a Xtill' Chioza': “Bi wzo' Chioza' gone' daa nazan c̱ho' kwenc̱he x̱enlalloo shi gone' ka ba wne'.”
Na' ka bi gok kooyeḻ' dii x̱iwaa Jesúza' gone' ka cheenin, na'ch bkwasan kwite'na' shloll.
Jesúza' billine' gana' mbani Galileana' ziyoochgue' yeḻ' wak c̱he Espíritu Sántona', na' doxenzə na' wze dill' daa chone'.
Na' chjali' chjasedile' beṉ' Israelka' gana' chdop chllaggake' choe'ḻwillgake' Chioza', na' yog' beṉ' nagake' ḻe xochi cho'e dill'.
Na'ch biyaje' Nazareta', yella' gana' bgole'. Na' ka bllin lla sabda', llana' chombaaṉ beṉ' Israelka', wyaje' gana' chdop chllaggake' choe'ḻwillgake' Chioza' kon ka yooloe' chone'. Na'ch wzollee lawe'ka' kwenc̱he blabe' Cho'a Xtill' Chioza'.
Na' be'gake'ne' yisha' daa bzej dii Isaíaza', beena' wdix̱jee daa goll Chioza'ne', na' ka bzeshe'n blabe' gana' na:
Espíritu c̱he X̱ancho Chioza' zoalene' nad', na' Chioza' ba bzoe' nad' zidye'len' beṉ' yesh'ka' dill' wen dill' kob c̱he'na'. Ba bseḻee nad' kwenc̱he zidtip' lall' beṉ'ka' chakyeshii yic̱hjlall'do'eka', na' zidtix̱je'id' beṉ' wak yisell yiḻaagake', na' gon' ka ile'i beṉ' lc̱hoḻka', na' gaklen' beṉ'ka' chc̱hi' chsak' beṉ' ḻegake',
na' wi'a dill' ba bllin lla gaklen X̱anchona' beṉ' yell-lioki.
Ka biyoll blabe' yisha' na'ch bitobe'n na' biyo'en beena' ngoo lall' neen, na' bibi'e. Na' yog' beṉ'ka' lle' na' shin chizozgakile' chwiagake'ne'.
Na' wzoloe' cho'e dill', chi'e: ―Ṉaa billinin ka na Cho'a Xtill' Chioza' dga ba benile.
Na' yog' beṉ'ka' lle' na' che' ljwellgake' ḻe chon beeni, na' chibangakile' ka xochi cho'e dill'. Na' che' ljwellgake': ―¿Aaga beenin xiiṉ Joséna'?
Na'ch che' Jesúza' ḻegake': ―Wnaljale c̱ha' ka dillaa de: “Wen rmech, biyon kwino'.” Na' ḻekzka' wnaljale nad': “Daa beninto' beno' Capernaúma' ḻekzka' benshkin lallchoni.”
Na' be'che' dill' chi'e ḻegake': ―Dii ḻi nia' le', to beṉ' chyix̱jee daa che' Chioza'ne' aga no shajḻe' c̱he' yell c̱he'na'.
Na' nia' le', zan nool wizeb wlle' gani mbani Israeli kana' wzoa Elíaza', beena' wdix̱jee daa goll Chioza'ne', kana' aga bi yej gok shoṉ yiz yoo gashjə na' wche'chga wbinna' doxen gani mbani Israeli.
Na' bi bseḻ' Chioza' Elíaza' kwenc̱he gaklene' nool wizebka' lle' ni, san bseḻeene' to yell zit' daa le Sarepta, daa llia gaozə yell Sidónna', gana' goklene' to nool wizeb zoa na'.
Na' ḻekzka' gok kana' wzoa dii Elisewa', beena' wdix̱jee daa goll Chioza'ne'. Beṉ' zan beṉ' Israelka' che'gakile' yillwe' daa le lepra, per ni toe' bi biyone'. Toz beṉ' Síriana' biyone', beena' le Naamán.
Na' yog' beṉ'ka' lle' gana' chdop chllaggake' ḻe bllaagake' daa wna Jesúza' ka'.
Na' lii wzolla'tegake' bibejgake' Jesúza' yella', na' bc̱he'gake'ne' to ga ze bdiṉj xen wal, goklall'gake' lljachix̱gake'ne'.
Per Jesúza' bicheje' ladje'ka' na' ziyaje'.
Jesúza' wyaje' Capernaúma', sto yell daa llia gana' mbani Galileana', na' bli' bsedile' beṉ'ka' lla sabda', llana' chombaaṉ beṉ' Israelka'.
Na' bibangakile' ka chli' chsedi Jesúza', ḻa' bli' bsedile' ḻegake' ḻega beṉ' nap yeḻ' wṉabia'.
Na' gana' chdop chllaggake', len to beṉ' yoo dii x̱iwaa na' bgosyaan ḻe' zillj wal, chi'e:
―¡Jwayi neto', Jesús, beṉ' Nazaret! ¿Abido' kwenc̱he wlliayoo neton'? Nad' nombi'a li', na' ṉezid' nako' ḻiizelozi beṉ' ḻi beṉ' shao' c̱he Chios.
Na'ch bsheshlen Jesúza' dii x̱iwaa, golle'n: ―¡Llizə wzoa! ¡Bichej! Na' chwiate beṉ'ka' bchix̱ btoḻ dii x̱iwaa beena', na' bichejan na' bikzə gayile' bi goki.
Na' yog' beṉ'ka' lle' na' bibangakile', na' che' ljwellgake': ―¿Naktekan nak cho'a xtill' beeni, lla? Ka chṉeze' chillesh dii x̱iw'ka' yoo beṉ' daa napchgue' yeḻ' wṉabia' na' yeḻ' wak.
Na' doxen na' wze dill' ka nak daa chon Jesúza'.
Na' biza' Jesúza' gana' chdop chllaggake' na' biyaje' lill Simónna'. Na' tobiiṉ c̱he Simónna' bi shawee, yoochgue' dii ḻana', na' wṉabgakile' Jesúza' gaklene'ne'.
Na'ch wbig' Jesúza' kwite'na' gana' die' na' bsheshlene' dii ḻana' na' bichejan. Na' lii biyaste noola' wzoloe' bene' dii weej wdaogake'.
Na' ka ba chxoa wbilla', beṉ'ka' lle' na' jwa'gake' lao Jesúza' beṉ'ka' chak wde wdeli yillwe'. Na' bx̱oa neena' to togake' na' biyakgakile'.
Na' bibeje' dii x̱iwaa yoo beṉ' zan, na' ka bichejgakan chosyaagakan zillj inlleb, che'gakan: ―Lin' nako' Xiiṉ Chioza'. Na'ch bsheshlen Jesúza' ḻegakan. Bi bi'e latj iṉegakan ḻa' ṉezgakin ḻen' nake' Crístona', beena' chbez beṉ' Israelka' wseḻ' Chioza' iṉabi'e.
Ka wyeeni', bchej Jesúza' yella' na' wyaje' ga kono lle'. Per beṉ' yellka' biyiljgake'ne', na' ka bllingake' kwite'na', goklall'gake' wzag'gake'ne' kwenc̱he yigaaṉlene' ḻegake'.
Na'ch goll Jesúza' ḻegake': ―Ḻekzka' chiyaḻ' c̱hix̱je'id' beṉ'ka' lle' yell yoblə ka nak yeḻ' wṉabia' c̱he Chioza', ḻa' daan bseḻee nad'.
Na' wda Jesúza' wdix̱ji'e cho'a xtill' Chioza' to to gana' chdop chllag beṉ' Israelka' choe'ḻwillgake' Chioza'.
To shii bllin Jesúza' cho'a nisdo' c̱he Genesareta' na' bllin beṉ' zan wal ax̱t bdakwyillgake'ne', daa cheengakile' wzenaggake' cho'a xtill' Chioza'.
Na' ble'i Jesúza' c̱hop barkw chi'gakan cho'a nisdo'na'. Ba bichej beṉ' wxen beḻka' na' ba chiyibgake' yix̱j c̱he'ka'.
Na'ch wyoo Jesúza' ḻoo barkw c̱he Simónna', na' wṉabile'ne' wllig' zilateen ḻoo nisdo'na'. Na' wche' Jesúza' ḻoo barkwa' na' wzoloe' bli' bsedile' beṉ'ka'.
Na' ka biyoll bli' bsedile' ḻegake', na'ch chi'e Simónna': ―Wyajlen barkwi gana' zitj na' wzaḻ'le yix̱j c̱helena' kwenc̱he senle beḻka'.
Na'ch che' Simónna': ―Maestro, do yel ba bennto' llinna' na' ni tlish'b bi bdoḻinto', per shi kan' no', wzaḻ'chnto' yix̱jki.
Na' ka bzaḻ'gake' yix̱j c̱he'ka', wxenan beḻ zan inlleb. Na' ka nan yibejgake' yix̱ja' wzolo chcheza'n.
Na' blaa neeka' beṉ'ka' lle' ḻoo barkwa' sto kwenc̱he jaklengake' ḻegake'. Na' ka bllin beṉ'ka', na'ch bissha'chagake' c̱hopte barkwka' ax̱t ba chakgakan ka dii kwe' yel.
Ka ble'i Simón Pédrona' ka gok, bc̱hek' xibe'na' lao Jesúza' na' chi'ene': ―Bikwasgach kwitii X̱an', ḻa' beṉ' saaxyaz nad'.
Golle'ne' ka' daa bibanile', na' ka'kzə beṉ'ka' lene' bibangakile' daa bdoḻ' beḻ zan inlleb.
Na' ḻekzka' bibani Jacóbona' len Juanna' xiiṉ Zebedewa', ḻa' lengaken' nakgake' txen Simónna'. Na' che' Jesúza' Simónna': ―Bi illebo'. Kon ka chono' ṉaa chbejo' beḻki ḻoo nisi, ka'kzan gono' yibejo' beṉ' lao dii mala'.
Na' ka billinlengake' barkwka' cho'a nisdo'na', na'zə bkwaaṉgake'n len xshinḻaze'ka' na'ch janogake' Jesúza'.
Na' shlak zoa Jesúza' to yell, bllin to beṉ' lawe'na' chak doxen kwerp c̱he'na' yillwe' daa le lepra. Na' ka ble'ile' Jesúza', bc̱hek' xibe'na' lawe'na' na' bc̱hek' yic̱hje'na' ax̱t lo yona' na' got'yoile'ne', chi'ene': ―X̱an', ṉezid' wak yikwaso' yillwe'ni chak' shi cheenilo'.
Na'ch Jesúza' bx̱oa neena' yic̱hj beena', na' chi'ene': ―Cheenid'x. Na' ṉaate yikwasa'n. Na' kon ka golle' ka' lii biyakteyi beena'.
Na'ch che' Jesúza'ne': ―Kono yoo ka ba ben' c̱ho'. Ḻete wyaj lao bx̱oza' kwenc̱he ile'ile' ba biyakilo', na' jwa' daa chiyaḻ' lljoo c̱he Chioza' daa nllia dii Moiséza' bia' kwenc̱he iṉezi beṉ' ba biyakilo'.
Na' ḻa'kzi golle'ne' ka', zizikchli wzeyi c̱he', na' beṉ' zan bdop bllaggake' kwenc̱he bzenaggake' cho'a xtilleena' na' kwenc̱he biyone' bittezə yillwe' dii chakgake'.
Per Jesúza' yooloe' chaje' ga kono beṉ' chak kwenc̱he chjeḻwille' Chioza'.
To lla ka chli' chsedi Jesúza', x̱oṉj fariseoka' na' beṉ'ka' chli' chsedi leya', na' beṉ'ka' za' yog' yellka' daa mbani Galileana' na'ch daa mbani Judeana' na' ḻekzka' beṉ' za' yell Jerusalénna', chi'gake' chzenaggake' dill' daa cho'e. Na' yeḻ' wak c̱he Chioza' wzoalenan Jesúza' kwenc̱he gok biyone' beṉ'ka' bi shao'.
Na'ch bllin to c̱hop beṉ' nḻengake' to beṉ' net ṉi'a neena' nx̱oagake'ne' to lo daa. Goklall'gake' sho'lengake'ne' ḻoo yoona' kwenc̱he lljwa'gake'ne' lao Jesúza',
per bi gok sho'lengake'ne' daa nyichachga beṉ'ka' ḻoo yoona'. Na'ch wyepgake' koll' yoona'lə na' bkwasgake' dexka' kwenc̱he gok bḻetjgake'ne' do daa c̱he'na' ladj beṉ'ka' lle' na' kwenc̱he blline' lao Jesúza'.
Na' ble'i Jesúza' ḻe nx̱enilall'gake'ne', na'ch chi'e beṉ' we'na': ―Bish'dawaa, ba biyakxen saaxya c̱ho'ka'.
Na'ch beṉ'ka' chli' chsedi leya' na' fariseoka' wza'lall'gake', chakgakile': “¿Nora beeni chonz kwine' ka Chioza'? ¡Ḻa' toz Chiozan' chak chizi'xene' saaxya c̱he beṉ'!”
Na' gokbe'i Jesúza' daa wza'lall'gake', na'ch golle' ḻegake': ―¿Berac̱he chza'lall'zle ka'?
¿Achakile chyalljchid' yeḻ' wak xench yep' beeni: “Ba bizi'xen' saaxya c̱ho'na'”, ka daa yepee: “Biyas na' bigoo nez”?
Na' wliid' le', nad', Beṉ' Bseḻ' Chioza', nap' yeḻ' wṉabia' yell-lioni kwenc̱he yizi'xen' saaxya c̱he beṉ'. Na'ch golle' beena' net ṉi'a neena': ―Ṉaa nia' li', biyas, bitob daa c̱ho'na' na' biyaj lillo'na'.
Na' lii biyaste beena' chwiate beṉ'ka' lle' na', bitobe' daa c̱he'na' bizee ziyaje' lill-le' choe'lawee Chioza'.
Na' yog'ḻoḻ beṉ'ka' bibangakile' na' be'la'ogake' Chioza', na' do chllebzgake' che'gake': ―Ṉaanlla ba ble'icho dga chonan ka chibanicho.
Ka biza' Jesúza', na' ble'ile' to beṉ' wic̱hixj lie' Leví, chi'e gana' chc̱hixjgake'. Na' chi'ene': ―Da, dino nad'.
Na'ch lii wzolla'te Levína', wlej yic̱hje' xshine'na' na' janoe' Jesúza'.
Na' Levína' bene' to lṉi xen c̱he Jesúza' lille'na'. Na' wyaj beṉ' zan beṉ' wic̱hixjka' na' zi baḻ beṉ' yoblə wdaogake' txen.
Na' fariseoka' na' beṉ'ka' chli' chsedi leya' wzologake' chakdiḻ-lengake' beṉ'ka' nak Jesúza' txen, che'gake': ―¿Berac̱he cheej chaolenle beṉ' wic̱hixjka' na' beṉ' malka'?
Na'ch che' Jesúza' ḻegake': ―Beena' zoa shi'a shao' aga no wen rmech chyalljile', san beena' bi shawaan chyalljile'ne'.
Aga bid' ni c̱he beṉ'ka' nak beṉ' ḻi beṉ' shao', san bid' kwenc̱he yep' beṉ' saaxyaka' chiyaḻ' yiyaj yilengakile'.
Na' wṉabgakile' Jesúza', che'gake'ne': ―Beṉ'ka' nak Juanna' txen na' beṉ'ka' nak fariseoka' txen zekizezi chzoagake' wbas' na' choe'ḻwillgake' Chioza'. Na' ¿berac̱he beṉ'ki nakgake' li' txen bi chzoagake' wbas'?
Na' chi'e ḻegake': ―Kat' de to yeḻ' wishagna', aga wak gonle byen beṉ'ka' chdop chllag soagake' wbasaa shlak zoalengake' bi'na' chshagna'. Na' ka'kzan beṉ'ki nakgake' nad' txen, cheej chaogake' ṉaa zoalen' ḻegake'.
Per wllin lla wkwas beṉ' nad' ladje'ka', kana'chan soagake' wbasaa.
Na' ḻekzka' bzoe' sto jempl, chi'e ḻegake': ―Ni to beṉ' bi chc̱hogue' xa kobe'na' na' chideen ḻee xe' dii gola'. Ḻa' shi gone'n ka', na' wlliayee dii koba', na' dii gola' aga wṉelebin lech' koba'.
Na' ni kono chgaa vinona' daa zi' chchejte to ḻoo yid golə. Ḻa' shi no gon ka', vino koba' wc̱hezaan yid gola' na' c̱hopten kwiayi'.
San vino koba' chiyaḻ' shollan ḻoo yid koba'.
Na' ḻekzka' to beṉ' ba yooloe' cheeje' vino gola' aga weenile' yeeje' dii koba', daa chziachile' dii gola'.
To lla sabd, llana' chombaaṉ beṉ' Israelka', wdelen Jesúza' beṉ'ka' nakgake'ne' txen to ga naz beṉ' trígona', na' beṉ'ka' zejlengake'ne' wzolo wdishjgake' trígona' na' wxobgake'n wdaogake'n.
Na' baḻ fariseoka' gollgake' ḻegake': ―¿Bic̱he chonzle daa bi chiyaḻ' goncho llani chombaaṉcho?
Na'ch che' Jesúza' ḻegake': ―¿Abiṉ' wlable gana' cho'en dill' ka ben dii Davina' len beṉ'ka' nakgake'ne' txen ka wdongake'?
Wyo'e ḻoo lill xḻatj Chioza' na' wdoyoe' yetxtilka' daa naki c̱he Chioza' daa toz bx̱ozka' de lsens gaogake'. Na' ḻekzka' bi'en beṉ'ka' nakgake'ne' txen.
Na' ḻekzka' chi'e fariseoka': ―Nad', Beṉ' Bseḻ' Chioza' Yell-lioni, chṉabi'a lao llani chombaaṉcho.
Na' sto lla sabd, llana' chombaaṉ beṉ' Israelka', wyaj Jesúza' gana' chdop chllaggake' choe'ḻwillgake' Chioza' na' wzoloe' chli' chsedile' ḻegake'. Na' ladj beṉ'ka' len to beṉ' net nee de shḻina'.
Na' fariseoka' na' beṉ'ka' chli' chsedi leya' lle'gake' chwiayeṉ'gake' shi wiyon Jesúza' beena' llana' chombaaṉgake', kwenc̱he gaogake' xya c̱he'.
Na' gokbe'i Jesúza' daa chza'lall'gake', na'ch golle' beena' net tḻaa neena': ―Wzolla' na' wze gchoḻa'. Na'ch wzolla' beena', wzie' gchoḻa'.
Na'ch goll Jesúza' beṉ'ka': ―Ni iṉabid' le': ¿Beran na leya' chiyaḻ' goncho lla sabdka'? ¿Agoncho dii wenna' anti goncho dii mala'? ¿Ayislacho beṉ' anti witchone'?
Na'ch bwia Jesúza' ḻegake', na' chi'e beena' net tḻaa neena': ―Bḻi noona'. Na'ch bḻi neena' na' biyakin.
Na' fariseoka' na' beṉ'ka' chli' chsedi leya' ḻe bllaagake' na' choe'gake' dill' nak ka gongake' c̱he Jesúza'.
Na' wyaj Jesúza' to lo yaa kwenc̱he jeḻwille' Chioza', na' do yel be'ḻwille'ne'.
Ka wyeeni', goxe' beṉ'ka' nakgake'ne' txen na' ladj beṉ'ka' wleje' beṉ'ki shlliṉ na' bsi'e ḻegake' postl:
Simónna' beena' bsi'e Pedro, len beṉ' bishee Andréza', na' Jacóbona', Juanna', Felípena', Bartoloména',
Matewa', Tomáza', Jacobo xiiṉ Alfewa', Simónna', beena' bsi'gake' Zelote,
Judas, beṉ' bish' Jacóbona' na' Jud Scariota', beena' bene' Jesúza' lo na' beṉ' malka'.
Na'ch biyetjlen Jesúza' ḻegake' lo yaana' na' billingake' to ga nak lesh'. Na' na' lle' beṉ' zan inlleb, beṉ' zaak doxen gana' mbani Judeana' na' yell Jerusalénna', na' beṉ' zaak cho'a nisdo'na' gana' mbani yell Tírona' na' yell Sidónna'.
Wyajgake' kwit Jesúza' kwenc̱he wzenaggake' xtilleena' na' yiyakgakile' bi yillwe' dii chakgake'. Na' ḻekzka' biyaki beṉ'ka' chsak'zi' dii x̱iw'ka' ḻegake'.
Yog'z beṉ' goklall'gake' idi'gake' Jesúza' daa ba ṉezgakile' chchej yeḻ' wak c̱he'na' na' chiyaki yog' beṉ'.
Na'ch bwia Jesúza' beṉ'ka' nakgake'ne' txen, na' chi'e ḻegake': ―Chakomba le' nakle beṉ' yesh' daa chleble yeḻ' wṉabia' c̱he Chioza'.
’Chakomba le' chbiḻ chdonle ṉaa; wllin lla yesh yeljile. ’Chakomba le' chbell-le ṉaa; wllin lla yixill-le.
’Chakomba le' shi chakzbani beṉ' le', shi bi chongake' le' txen, shi biya dii nagake' le', na' shi chongakile' le' nakzi ka chongakile' to beṉ' wen dii mal ni c̱ha', nad', Beṉ' Bseḻ' Chioza' Yell-lioni.
Ḻi yibayi, na' ḻi soa mbalaz kat' ba chongakile' le' ka', ḻa' yabana' gaple to dii wen dii shao'. Ḻa' ka'kzə beni dii x̱ozxtoe'ka' beṉ'ka' wdix̱jee daa goll Chioza' ḻegake' kani'yi.
’Nyesh'laz gak c̱hele, le' nakle beṉ' wni'a, ḻa'kzi ḻe wen chak c̱hele ṉaa.
’Nyesh'laz gak c̱hele, le' de dii cheej chaole ṉaa, ḻa' wllin lla ibiḻ idonle. ’Nyesh'laz gak c̱hele, le' chyitj chxill-le ṉaa; wllin lla kwellyesh'le.
’Nyesh'laz gak c̱hele, le' choe'la'o yog' beṉ' le', ḻa' ka'kzə be'la'o dii x̱ozxto'leka' dii beṉ'ka' benzə ka chyix̱jee daa che' Chioza' ḻegake'.
’Le' chzenagle ṉaa, nia' le', ḻi gaki beṉ'ka' chakzbani le'. Ḻi gonigake' wen.
Ḻi iṉabi Chioza' gone' ka gak wen c̱he beṉ'ka' chyishj bia' blag' c̱hele. Ḻi iṉabi Chioza' gaklene' beṉ'ka' chiya dii nagake' c̱hele.
Shi no kap' x̱ag'lena' tḻaa, ḻi wze daa zi shḻaa. Na' shi no koyo xachel-lena', ḻi we'tega len xkamislena'.
Nottezə beṉ' shi bi iṉabe' c̱hele, ḻi we'n. Na' ka', shi no ikaa bi de c̱hele, bi yiṉabzilene'n.
Ḻi goni beṉ' kon ka cheenile gongakile' le'.
’Shi to beṉ'ka' nllagzile chakile, ¿garan de dii wenna' daa chonle? Ḻa' ka'klen chon beṉ' saaxyaka'.
Ḻekzka' shi to beṉ'ka' chonzi le' wen chiyonile wen, ¿garan de dii wenna' chonle? Ḻa' ka'klen chon beṉ' saaxyaka'.
Na' shi choe'le bi choe'le beṉ' daa ṉezile yigwee wzonna', ¿garan de dii wenna' daa chonle? Ḻa' ka'klen chon beṉ' ssaxyaka', choe'gake' bi choe'gake' daa nongake' lez wigoogake' wzon c̱he'ka'.
Na' le', ṉaalla, chiyaḻ' gakile beṉ'ka' chakzbani le', na' gonle wen c̱hegake'. Na' shi we'le dii we'le ḻegake', bi gonle lez yiyoṉgake'n. Shi ka' gonle, Chioza' yiyoṉe' dii xench c̱hele, na' iṉezi beṉ' nakle xiiṉ Chios, beena' nak beṉ' choo beṉ' xen, ḻa' ḻe' chone' wen c̱he beṉ'ka' bi choe' ḻe' yeḻ' chox̱ken na' beṉ' wen dii malka'.
Chiyaḻ' yiyeshii ljwell-le ka chiyeshii X̱acho Chioza' yog' beṉ'.
’Bi wwia wyile bi chon beṉ', kwenc̱he bi gon Chioza' xya c̱hele. Bibi wtobile' beṉ', kwenc̱he bi gaple doḻ' lao Chioza'. Ḻi si'xen c̱he ljwell-le, na' Chioza' si'xene' c̱hele.
Ḻi we' beṉ' bi chyalljile' na' Chioza' yiyoṉe'n. Na' yiyoṉchle' dii xench, ka chon beṉ' chzanile' do yic̱hj do lallee kat' bi wi'e, chzoayaa chzoalline'n. Ḻa' kon ka chonle chzanile' we'le beṉ' bi de c̱hele, ka'kzan goni Chioza' le'.
Na' bzoa Jesúza' to jempl, chi'e ḻegake': ―Ṉezicho bi gak to beṉ' lc̱hoḻ wc̱hi'e sto beṉ' lc̱hoḻ, ḻa' c̱hoptegake' lljabix̱gake' to ḻoo yech.
Na' beena' chsed bi gak iṉe': “Chonch' ka beena' chli' chsedile' nad'.” Kat'ch yiyoll yido wsede', kana'chan gake' ka beena' bli' bsedile'ne'.
’¿Bic̱he chwiazo' bic̱ha' yoo ḻoo jalao bish' ljwello'na' na' bi chile'ilo' kwagaa yoo ḻoo jalawo'na'?
Shi bi chle'ilo' kwagaa yoo ḻoo jalawo'na', ¿nakra gono' yoo bish' ljwello'na': “Beṉshki yibej' bic̱ha' yoo ḻoo jalawo'na'”? ¡Beṉ' wxiye'! Zigaate bwia c̱ho'na' na' tech wwio' c̱he' bish' ljwello'na'.
’Biga zoa to yag wen na' kwiazan dii bi nak wen, ni biga zoa to yag dii bi nak wen kwiazan dii nak wen.
Ka ile'icho daa chbia to yag, na' chṉezicho bi yag daa. Yag yeshaa aga wbian yix̱wewa', na' ḻekzka' yag bisgaana' aga wbian uvana'.
Ka'kzan beena' nak beṉ' wen, choe' dill' wen, ḻa' ḻoo yic̱hjlall'do'enan' yoo dii wenna'. Na' beena' nak beṉ' mal, cho'e dill' dii nak mal, ḻa' ḻoo yic̱hjlall'do'enan' yoo dii mala', ḻa' yog' daa chṉecho chchejan ḻoo yic̱hjlall'do'chona'.
’¿Berac̱he nazle nad' “X̱an', X̱an'”, na' bi chonle daa nia' le'?
Ni iṉia' le' no zaklebi beena' chone' nad' txen na' chzenague' c̱ha' na' chone' ka nia'.
Zaklebile' beena' ben to yoo. Zigaate wdene' zitj wal na' wleke' leninna' lo yaja'. Ka wde yawa' na' wyoon ḻe'inna', aga bizoyin yisheen daa, ḻa' chi'cha leninna' lo yaja'.
Na' beena' cheni cho'a xtillaana' na' bi chone' ka nia', zaklebile' beena' ben lille'na' lo yona' na' bibi lenin wleke'. Na' ka wde yawa' wyoon ḻe'inna', lii billeeten na' wlliayi'tekkzan.
Ka biyoll be'len Jesúza' beṉ'ka' dill', biyaje' Capernaúma'.
Na' yella' zoa to beṉ' Roma beṉ' chṉabi'e to guiyoa soldad, na' zoa to xmose' lille'na', beena' ḻe chakile', na' chake' to yillwe' dii chonan ka witan ḻe'.
Na' ka beni x̱an soldadka' choe'gake' xtill' Jesúza', na'ch bseḻee baḻ beṉ' golka' chṉabia' Israela' kwenc̱he lljet'yogakile'ne' lljayene' beena' bi shao'.
Na' ka bllin beṉ' golka' kwit Jesúza', got'yogakile'ne', che'gake': ―X̱an soldadka' chidoḻee gakleno'ne',
ḻa' ḻe chakile' cho' beṉ' Israel na' ḻen' bene' yoona' gana' chdi'anto' choe'ḻwillnto' Chioza'.
Na'ch wyajlen Jesúza' ḻegake'. Na' ka ba zoa yillingake' lille'na', x̱an soldadka' bseḻee baḻ beṉ' nllaguile' kwenc̱he jellgake' Jesúza' dill'ki: ―X̱an', bi sio' wṉeyi yido', ḻa' bi chidoḻaa shoo ḻoo lillii.
Daan bi biyaxjid' yid' kwin' yidtiḻ' li'. Ḻa'c̱h' to c̱hop cho'a dill' sheḻ' iṉo' na' yiyakile'.
Ḻa' zoa no chṉabia' nad', na' ḻekzka' chṉabi'a soldad c̱ha'ka'. Na' kat' chep' toe': “Wyaj ni”, na' chaje'. Na' kat' chep' stoe': “Da ni”, na' chide'. Na' kat' chep' xmosaa: “Ben dga”, na' chone'n.
Na' ka beni Jesúza' xtill' beena' na' bibanile', na' biyec̱hje' bwie' beṉ'ka' zjanogake'ne', na' chi'e ḻegake': ―Dii ḻi, ni to beṉ' Israel biṉ' illag' beṉ' gonḻilall'ḻikze' nad' ka chonḻilall' beeni nad'.
Na'ch ziyaj beṉ'ka' bseḻ' x̱an soldadka', na' ka billingake' lille'na' ble'gakile' ba biyaki xmose'na'.
Ka wde, na' wyaj Jesúza' sto yell dii le Naín kon beṉ'ka' nakgake'ne' txen na' lench zan beṉ' yoblə.
Na' ka bllingake' cho'a yella', ble'gakile' zjakwash' beṉ'ka' to bi' wet. Na' bi'na' wit nakb' bi' tlish', na' xṉa'baa nake' noolə wizeb. Na' beṉ' zan beṉ' yellka' zjakwash'gake'b'.
Na' ka ble'i X̱ancho Jesúza' noola', na' biyeshile'ne', chi'ene': ―Bi kwello'.
Na'ch jabiguee bex̱ee gana' xoa bi' weta', na' wlez beṉ'ka' nḻengake'b'. Na' golle' bi' weta': ―Bi' xkwid', nia' li', ¡biyas!
Na' bi' weta' lii bibanteb' na' bibe'b' na' wzolo chiṉeb', na' biyon Jesúza'b' lo na' xṉa'baa.
Na' ka ble'i beṉ'ka' daa bene', yog'ḻoḻze' blleb na' wzologake' choe'la'ogake' Chioza', nagake': ―Ladjchoni ba bla' to beṉ' zakii beṉ' chyix̱jee daa che' Chioza'ne'. Na' ḻekzka' nagake': ―Chiozan' ba blee kwenc̱he gaklene' cho' nakcho yell c̱he'.
Na' doxen gana' mbani Judeana' na' yellka' llia gaozə wṉezgakile' daa ben Jesúza'.
Na' beṉ'ka' nongake' Juanna' txen jayellgake'ne' yog' diika' chon Jesúza'. Na'ch Juanna' wṉie' c̱hope'
na' bseḻee ḻegake' gana' zoa Jesúza' kwenc̱he jaṉabgakile'ne' shi ḻeyeṉ'en' beena' llia bia' yid wa shi chiyaḻ' kwezgake' sto beṉ' yoblə.
Na' ka bllin beṉ'ka' bseḻ' Juanna' kwit Jesúza', che'gake'ne': ―Juanna', beena' chchoa beṉ' nisa', bseḻee neto' kwenc̱he zidṉabinto' li' shi li'yeṉ'kzan nako' Crístona', beena' chbeznto' wseḻ' Chioza' kwenc̱he iṉabi'e, wa shi chiyaḻ' kweznto' stoe'.
Na' shlak zegake' na', biyon Jesúza' beṉ' zan beṉ' chak yillwe', na' ḻekzka' bibeje' dii x̱iw'ka' yoo beṉ', na' bene' ka ble'i beṉ' zan beṉ' lc̱hoḻka'.
Na'ch che' Jesúza' beṉ'ka' bseḻ' Juanna': ―Ḻi yiyaj na' ḻi lljayell Juanna' daa ba ben ble'ile. Ḻi lljayelle' beṉ' lc̱hoḻka' chle'gakile', na' beṉ'ka' bi chak sa' chza'gake', na' beṉ'ka' chak yillwe'na' daa le lepra chiyakgakile', na' beṉ' kwellka' chengakile', na' chiban beṉ' wetka', na' chyix̱je'id' beṉ' yesh'ka' dill' wen dill' kob c̱he Chioza'.
Chakomba beena' chajḻe' c̱ha' na' bi chakc̱hoplallee.
Na' ka biza' beṉ'ka' bseḻ' Juanna', Jesúza' bi'e xtill' Juanna' lao beṉ'ka' lle' na', chi'e: ―¿Nakra nak beena' jawiale latja' gana' bibi chashj chḻeb? ¿Anake' to beṉ' chakc̱hoplallii c̱he dill'ka' cho'e?
Na' shi bi nake' ka', ¿nakran nak beena' jawiale, shka'? ¿Ato beṉ' nakwe' lech' dii zakii? Ḻa' ṉezkzile beṉ'ka' nakw lech' dii zakii, na' naptegake' bittezə dii chzelall'gake', zoagake' lill beṉ' wṉabia'ka', aga zoagake' latja' gana' bibi chashj chḻeb.
Na' ¿nakran nak beena' jawiale, shka'? ¿Ato beṉ' chyix̱jee daa che' Chioza'ne'? Dii ḻi kan' chone', na' chontechle' ka to beṉ' chyix̱jee daa che' Chioza'ne'.
Ḻa' c̱he beenin cho'e Cho'a Xtill' Chioza' dill' gana' nan: Wseḻaa beena' kwialo lawo'na', na' c̱hix̱ji'e xtilloona' kwenc̱he soa beṉ' wzenaggake' c̱ho' kat' illino'.
Na' nia' le', lao yog'ḻoḻte beṉ' yell-lioni, ni to konoṉ' ichej beṉ' zak'teche' ka Juanna'. Per nottezə beena' choe' latj iṉabia' Chioza' ḻoo yic̱hjlall'do'ena', zak'teche' ka Juanna'.
Na' yog'ḻoḻ beṉ'ka' bchoa Juanna' nisa', no beṉ' wic̱hixjka' na' zan beṉ' yoblə, ka bengakile' daa wna Jesúza', gokbe'gakile' dill' ḻi dill' shao' nak cho'a xtill' Chioza'.
Na' fariseoka' na' beṉ'ka' chli' chsedi leya' bi goongakile' wchoa Juanna' ḻegake' nisa', ni bi goklall'gake' gon Chioza' dii wenna' cheenile' gone' c̱hegake'.
Na'ch goll X̱ancho Jesúza' ḻegake': ―¿Bi ka wsaklebid' le' mbanle ṉaa? ¿No ka iṉia' nakle?
Nakle ka bi'do'ka' chbe' gana' chak yaana' na' chosyaagakb' che' ljwellb': “Bkwellnto' blleja' na' bi byaale, na' beḻnto' dii chon nyesh', na' ni bi wchell-le.”
Ḻa' bid Juan wichoa nisa', na' bi chawe' yetxtil ni bi cheeje' vino, na' nale c̱he': “Dii x̱iwaan yo'e.”
Na'ch bid' nad', Beṉ' Bseḻ' Chioza' Yell-lioni, na' chle'ile cheej chaw', na' nale c̱ha': “Ḻe beṉ' waox̱at nak beeni na' cheejtie', na' nllagteile' beṉ' saaxyaka' na' beṉ' wic̱hixjka'.”
Per yeḻ' sin' c̱he Chioza' chli'lawin ka nsa' c̱he beṉ'ka' chzenaggake' c̱heyin.
To fariseo wṉie' Jesúza' kwenc̱he gaogake' lille'na'. Ka blline' na' wchi'e cho'a mesa'.
Na' to noolə wda zoa yella', ka wṉezile' zjtao Jesúza' lill farisewa', na'ch wyaje' nox̱ee to lmet de yaj xochi na' yollan set zix̱.
De chbellzile' jabiguee xṉi'a Jesúza' na' bisbisile' ṉi'ena' nis xc̱hell c̱he'na'. Na' bisbillile'n yish' yic̱hje'na', na' bnope'n na' bwazje'n set zix̱a'.
Na' farisewa', beena' wṉie' Jesúza' lille'na', ka ble'ile' ka chon noola', na' gokile': “Sheḻ'ka' dii ḻi nak beeni to beṉ' chyix̱jee daa che' Chioza'ne', wakbe'ile' nan nooli chox̱' ṉi'ena' nake' beṉ' saaxya.”
Na'ch che' Jesúza' farisewa': ―Simón, de to dii cheenid' iṉia' li'. Na' che' Simónna': ―Wna, Maestro.
Na'ch che' Jesúza': ―C̱hop beṉ' chbag'gake' mech c̱he to beṉ' chon yic̱hjin. Toe' chbaguee gay' guiyoa mech plat, na' stoe' chbaguee shiyonan.
Na' ni toe' bi bllelgakile'n yiyixjgake'n. Na'ch x̱an mecha' benxenlallee daa chaḻ'gake' c̱he'. Wnashki nad', ¿no beṉ'ka' c̱hop gakchile'ne'?
Na'ch che' Simónna': ―Chakid' beena' chbag' dii xench. Na' che' Jesúza'ne': ―Lekzilo', kan' nakan.
Na'ch bwia Jesúza' noola' na' chi'e Simónna': ―Bwiakachi nooli. Ka wyo'a ḻoo lillo'ni bi beṉo' nisa' kwenc̱he c̱hib ṉi'ani, per nooli ba wdibile' nis xc̱hell c̱he'na' ṉi'ani na' bisbillile'n yish' yic̱hje'na'.
Bi bnopo' nad', per nooli kon ka wyo'a chnoptezi chnope' ṉi'ani.
Bi wdebo' yic̱hjii set, per nooli ba bwazje' set zix̱a' ṉi'ani.
Daan nia' li', ḻa'kzi dii zan saaxya ba ben nooli, ba biyakxengakan daa ḻe chakchgaile' nad'. Na' beena' lat'zə biyakxen c̱he', ḻekzka' lat'chga chakile' nad'.
Na'ch golle' noola': ―Ba biyakxen saaxya c̱ho'ka'.
Na' beṉ'ka' chi'lengake' Jesúza' txen wzologake' che' ljwellgake': ―¿Nora beeni, lla, ax̱t saaxyaka' chizi'xene'?
Na' Jesúza' chi'e noola': ―Daa chonḻilalloo nad', ba bilo' lao yeḻ' zak'zi'na'. Biyaj mbalaz.
Ka wde dga, wda Jesúza' zan yell xen na' zan yelldo', chyix̱ji'e dill' koba' nan Chioza' chṉabi'e ḻoo yic̱hjlall'do' beṉ'ka' chzenag c̱he'. Na' postl c̱he'ka' shlliṉ chdalengake'ne' txen.
Na' ḻekzka' len baḻ noolka' ba biyone'. Baḻe' bibeje' dii x̱iw'ka' wyoogake', na' zi baḻe' gokgake' yillwe' na' biyone' ḻegake'. Na' ladje'ka' len Maríana', noola' nsi'gake' Magdalena, beena' bibej Jesúza' gall dii x̱iw'ka'.
Na' ḻekzka' len noola' le Juana, xool Chúzana', beena' ngoo lo nee chap chwie' lill Heródeza'. Na' len Susánana', na' zanch noolka' beṉ'ka' jano Jesúza' na' bc̱hingake' dii de c̱hegake' kwenc̱he goklengake'ne'.
Beṉ' zan bllesh to to yell jawiagake' Jesúza', na' ka bdop beṉ' zan wal na'ch bseesile' ḻegake' to jempl, chi'e:
―To beṉ' goz gooṉ wzee zeje' goza'. Na' ka zej chzaḻee biṉna', baḻan bxop cho'a neza' na' blej bshoshj beṉ' ḻen, na' bllin byiṉka' wdaogakban.
Na' zi baḻan bxop ladj yajka' gana' bitek chi' yona', na' ka bla'gakan to wbillzgakan, ḻa' aga bi gop' de gana' bxopan.
Na' zi baḻan bxop ladj yag yesh'ka', na' ka bla'gakan aga be' yag yesh'ka' latj igolgakan.
Na' zi baḻan bxop lo yo wenna', na' ḻe bgolgakan na' ax̱t do to guiyoa wej wllia to ton. Na' ka biyoll bseesee jempla', na'ch wṉie' zilljə chi'e: ―Le' chenile dga nia', ḻi sen wṉeyi.
Na'ch wṉab beṉ'ka' nakgake'ne' txen bi zejin jempla' daa bseesee.
Na' che' Jesúza' ḻegake': ―Chioza' cho'e latj iṉezile daa kono ṉezkzi, ka chṉabi'e ḻoo yic̱hjlall'do' beṉ'ka' chzenaggake' c̱he'. Na' beṉ'ka' sto chseesid' ḻegake' shgaḻ' jempl, ḻa' ḻa'kzi chle'gakile' bin chon', kon chongake' ka beṉ' bi chle'i. Na' ḻa'kzi chengakile' bin nia', aga chajni'gakile'n.
’Kin zeji jempl c̱he beṉ goz gooṉa': cho'a xtill' Chioza' nakan ka biṉna' daa goze'.
Na' zoa beṉ' chzenaggake' cho'a xtill' Chioza', na' lii ze'te dii x̱iwaa chikwasan daa kwenc̱he bi shajḻe'gake' na' kwiayi'gake'. Chak c̱hegake' ka gok c̱he biṉna' daa bxop cho'a neza'.
Na' zoa beṉ' chibagakile' chzenaggake' cho'a xtill' Chioza' na' chlebgake'n, per kat' chak bi chak c̱hegake' na' chbej yic̱hjgake'n. Chak c̱hegake' ka gok c̱he biṉna' bi bde loinna' daa bxopan lo yaja'.
Na' zoa beṉ' chzenague' cho'a xtill' Chioza', per chi'ch yic̱hjgake' daa chak c̱hegake' na' c̱he yeḻ' wni'ana', na' c̱he bichlə dii chzelall'gake', na' bi chakchagake' lo xṉez Chioza'. Chak c̱hegake' ka gok c̱he biṉna' bxop ladj yag yesh'ka'.
Na' zoa beṉ' chzenaggake' cho'a xtill' Chioza' do yic̱hj do lall'gake' na' chongake' ka nan, na' chzo chzakgakile' bittezə dii chak c̱hegake'. Beṉ'kin chak c̱hegake' ka gok c̱he biṉna' bxop lo yo wenna' daa ḻe wllia.
’Biga zoa to beṉ' chxene' kandila' na' chdose'n to dii wkwashaan daa wa chzoe'n xan xḻague'na', san chzoe'n sibə kwenc̱he ile'i beṉ'ka' sho' ḻoo yoona'.
Na' ḻekzka' yog'ḻoḻte dii ngash' ṉaa, wllin lla yila' lawin, na' daa kono ṉezi ṉaa, wllin lla iṉezi beṉaan.
’Ḻi wzenag dga nia' le' ṉaa. Beena' chzenag zizikchli shajni'chile', na' beena' bi chzenag, daa ba bzenague' lat', yog'ḻoḻan yiyaḻ-lallee.
Na'ch bllin xṉa' Jesúza' len beṉ' bisheeka' gana' zoe', na' bi gok ibig'gake' kwite'na' daa lle' beṉ' zan.
Na' wbig' to beṉ' golle' Jesúza': ―Xṉoona' len beṉ' bishooka' lle'gake' lesh' chyoona' na' cheengakile' wshaljlengake' li'.
Na' goll Jesúza': ―Beṉ'ka' chzenaggake' cho'a xtill' Chioza' na' chongake' ka nan, ḻegaken' nakgake' xṉa' na' beṉ' bishaa.
To lla wyoo Jesúza' to ḻoo barkw len beṉ'ka' nakgake'ne' txen na' golle' ḻegake': ―Techo shḻaalə nisdo'ni. Na'ch wza'gake'.
Na' shlak ngoo barkwa' nez, wtes Jesúza'. Na'ch wze to be' wal lo nisdo'na' na' wzolo chas chat' nisa' na' biyollan ḻoo barkwa', na' zi lat'zə nan kwe'n yel.
Na' jasbangake' Jesúza', che'gake'ne': ―¡Maestro! ¡Maestro! ¡Ba chbe'cho yel! Na' wyas Jesúza' na' bsheshlene' be'na' len nisdo'na'. Na' wlezgakan, bich bi gok.
Na'ch golle' ḻegake': ―¿Abi chonḻilall'kzle nad'? Na' ḻegake' ḻe chllebgake' na' ḻe chibangakile' na' che' ljwellgake': ―¿Nora beeni lla?, ax̱t be'na' na' nisdo'na' chzenaggakan c̱he'.
Na'ch bllingake' yell-lio c̱he beṉ' Gadáraka', daa llia shḻaa nisdo'na' ndiḻ yell-lio c̱he Galileana'.
Ka bichej Jesúza' ḻoo barkwa' jabig' to beṉ' Gadara kwite'na'. Ba wlla yo'e dii x̱iw'ka', na' bich bi xalaane' nakw, ni bich zoe' lille', san kapsanta' noni lille'.
Na' ka ble'ile' Jesúza', besyee na' jac̱hek' xibe' lawe'na', na' zillj inlleb chi'e: ―Jwayiz nad', Jesús Xiiṉ Chios, beṉ' nak ḻiizelozi beṉ' choo beṉ' xen. Ben goklen bi wsak'zi'o nad'.
Gollan ka' daa ba chon Jesúza' byen yichejan. Ba wlla chṉabi'an ḻe' na' ḻa'kzi chc̱hejgake' ṉi'a neena' gdenna', ḻobe' chc̱hogue'n. Na' dii x̱iwaa chtadon ḻe' na' chjsoe' ga kono beṉ' lle'.
Na' che' Jesúza': ―¿Bin lio'? Na' chi'e: ―Legiónan lia'. Golle' ka', ḻa' zanannan' yo'e.
Na' got'yogakin Jesúza' bi wseḻeegakan gana' kwiayi'gakan.
Na' gaozə zoa to yaa gana' lle' kush zan chaogakb. Na' dii x̱iw'ka' wzeyidgakan wṉabgakin Jesúza' wi'e latj yiyoogakan kushka', na' bi'e latj.
Na'ch bichej dii x̱iw'ka' yoo beena' na' biyoogakan kushka'. Na' lii goklleshtegakib na' jabix̱gakb to cho'a bdiṉj na' jshoogakb ḻoo nisa' na' witgakb.
Na' beṉ'ka' chap kushka' ka ble'gakile' daa gok, biyajdogake' jazengakile'n beṉ'ka' lle' yella' na' beṉ'ka' lle' lyix̱aa.
Na'ch bllesh beṉ'ka' jawiagake' daa gok. Na' ka bllingake' kwit Jesúza', na' chi' beena' wyoo dii x̱iw'ka' kwite'na'. Ba biyakw xalaane'na' na' ba biyeeṉ biyeeniile'. Na' bllebgake'.
Na' beṉ'ka' ble'gakile' daa gok, gollgake' beṉ'ka' zi' bllin nakan gok biyaki beena' wyoo dii x̱iw'ka'.
Na' yog'ḻoḻ beṉ' Gadáraka' got'yogakile' Jesúza' yizee lalle'ka' daa ḻe chllebgake' ka bene'. Na' biyo'e ḻoo barkwa' ziyaje'.
Na' beena' bichej dii x̱iw'ka' got'yoile' Jesúza' wi'e latj shajlene'ne'. Per Jesúza' chi'ene':
―Biyaj lillo'na' na' jaye' dill' ka nak dii wen dii shawaa daa ba ben Chioza' c̱ho'. Na'ch biyaj beena' jayee dill' doxen yella' ka nak dii wen dii shawaa daa ben Jesúza' c̱he'.
Ka billin Jesúza' shḻaa nisdo'na', ḻe chiba chizaki beṉ'ka' lle' na', ḻa' yog'zgake'n chbezgake' ḻe'.
Na'ch bllin to beṉ' le Jairo, nake' to beṉ'ka' chgoo xṉezi c̱heyi diika' chon beṉ' Israelka' gana' chdop chllaggake' choe'ḻwillgake' Chioza'. Na' bc̱hek' xibe'na' lao Jesúza' na' got'yoile'ne' shaje' lille'na',
daa ba chakshwet bi' nool c̱he'na'. Nakb' to bi' tlish' tyaj, na' ka do shlliṉ yizib'. Na' shlak zej Jesúza' beṉ' zan janogake'ne' ax̱t bdakwyillgake'ne'.
Na' ladj beṉ'ka' zjano Jesúza' len to noolə ba gok shlliṉ yiz chzoe' wbaana'. Na' ba blliayee yog' dii de c̱he' daa chajtezi chaje' lao beṉ' wen rmechka', na' ni to kono gok yiyon ḻe'.
Na'ch wbiguee koll' Jesúza' bex̱ee xe'na', na' katena' lii biyakteile'.
Na'ch goll Jesúza' beṉ'ka' zjano ḻe': ―¿No beena' ba bex̱' nad'? Na' ni to kono bc̱heb. Na'ch goll Pédrona'ne': ―Maestro, beṉ'kin chdakwyillgake' li' na' chllig'gake' li' to ki to ka'lə. ¿Bic̱he nazo': “Non ba bex̱' nad'”?
Na' che' Jesúza' ḻegake': ―Nochodan' ba bex̱' nad', ḻa' gokbe'teid' bchej yeḻ' wak c̱ha'na'.
Na' noola', ka gokbe'ile' aga wak wkwashee, do chllebze' jac̱hek' xibe'na' lao Jesúza'. Na' lao yog'ḻoḻ beṉ'ka' lle' na', golle' bic̱he bex̱'ze' xe'na' na' daa bex̱een lii biyakteile'.
Na'ch goll Jesúza'ne': ―Xiiṉ', daa chonḻilalloo nadaan biyakilo'. Biyaj mbalaz.
Ni choe'telə Jesúza' dill' ka bllin to beṉ' wzee lill Jairona', na' jelle'ne': ―Ba wit bi' c̱ho'na'. Bich gonilo' Maestroni zed.
Na' ka beni Jesúza', na' golle' Jairona': ―Bi illebo'. Wyajḻe' c̱ha', na' wiyakkzi bi' c̱ho'na'.
Na' ka bllingake' lille'na', aga be' Jesúza' latj sho' beṉ' yoblə, ḻete Pédrona', Jacóbona', Juanna' na' x̱axṉa' bi' weta'zə.
Yog'ḻoḻ beṉ'ka' lle' lill Jairona' chbellgake' daa ba wit bi'do'na'. Na' goll Jesúza' ḻegake': ―Bi kwell-le, aga witbaan, cheszbaan.
Na' bxill-ləgake' c̱he', ḻa' ṉezgakile' ba witbaan.
Na'ch bex̱' Jesúza' na' bi' wetdo'na' na' wṉie' zilljə, chi'e: ―Biyas, bi'do'.
Na'ch bibam' na' lii biyasteb'. Na' goll Jesúza' ḻegake' we'gake' dii gaob'.
Na' x̱axṉa'baa ḻe bibangakile', na' che' Jesúza' ḻegake' ni to kono ye'gake' daa gok.
Na' bitop Jesúza' beṉ'ka' shlliṉ, na' bi'e ḻegake' yeḻ' wak na' yeḻ' wṉabia' kwenc̱he yibejgake' yog'ḻoḻ dii x̱iw'ka' yoo beṉ' na' yiyongake' beṉ' che'i yillwe'.
Na' bseḻee ḻegake' kwenc̱he llje'gake' dill' ka nak yeḻ' wṉabia' c̱he Chioza', na' yiyongake' beṉ'ka' bi shao'.
Na' chi'e ḻegake': ―To ka chazlen ḻi shaj. Bi gox̱'le yag bar, bi wa'zle yix̱j ga koo xshinḻazle, bi wa'le dii gaole, ni mech, na' ni zi shkwe' xale.
Na' yoona' gana' illinle, na'tezə soale ax̱t ka illinch lla yiza'le.
Na' yella' gana' bi wlebgake' le', kat' yiza'le, yishible bishtena' llia ṉi'aleka' kwenc̱he gakbe'gakile' aga wenan chongake' bi chlebgake' cho'a xtill' Chioza'.
Na'ch wza' beṉ'ka' nakgake'ne' txen na' wyajgake' to to yell wdix̱je'gake' dill' wen dill' kob c̱he Chioza' na' biyongake' beṉ'ka' bi shao'.
Heródeza', beena' wṉabia' gana' mbani Galileana', benile' yog' daa chon Jesúza'. Na' chakile' nora beena', ḻa' baḻ beṉ' nagake' dii Juan wichoa nisan' ba bibane' dii yoblə.
Na' zi baḻe' nagake' Elíazan' ba bila' dii yoblə. Na' zi baḻe' nagake' nochod' dii beṉ'ka' wdix̱jee daa goll Chioza' ḻegake' kani'yin ba biban ladj beṉ' wetka'.
Na' Heródeza' wne': ―Nad' ben' mandad wchog yen dii Juanna'. ¿Noraz beena' chenzid' nagake' chiya dii chone', lla? Na' ḻe goklall' Heródeza' ile'ile' Jesúza'.
Na' ka billin postlka' shlliṉ, na' gollgake' Jesúza' yog'ḻoḻ diika' jengake'. Na'ch bc̱hi'e to ḻezgake' yella' le Betsaida.
Na' ka wṉezi beṉ'ka' ba zej Jesúza', na'ch wloogake' nez zjanogake'ne' na' ka bllingake' lawe'na', blebe' ḻegake' na' bzajniile' ḻegake' ka nak yeḻ' wṉabia' c̱he Chioza', na' biyone' beṉ'ka' bi shao'.
Na' ka ba wlle', beṉ'ka' shlliṉ jabig'gake' kwit Jesúza' na' gollgake'ne': ―Goll beṉ'ki yiyajgake' yellka' wa no ranshdo'ka' llia gaozə lljadiljgake' dii gaogake' na' ga guesgake', ḻa' ga ni zoacho bikzə bi de.
Na' che' Jesúza' ḻegake': ―Len', ḻi we' dii gaogake'. Na'ch che'gake'ne': ―Gay'lish'tgui yetxtilki napcho na' zi c̱hopchga beḻ, ḻechozə shi willjx̱i'chnto' c̱he yoguee.
Gollgake'ne' ka' ḻa' ka do gayaa mil beṉ' byoka' lle' na'. Na'ch che' Jesúza' beṉ'ka' shlliṉ: ―Ḻi ye'gake' kwe' shiyon wejgake'.
Na' bzoagake' xtillee na' wlekgake' beṉ'ka'.
Na'ch bex̱' Jesúza' yetxtilka' gay' na' beḻka' c̱hop. Na' bḻis jalawe'na' yabana' bi'e Chioza' yeḻ' chox̱ken, na' bxoxje'n na' bi'en beṉ'ka' nakgake'ne' txen na'ch be'gake' c̱he c̱he beṉ'ka'.
Na' yog'gake' wdao ka beljgakile', na' diika' bichooṉan bitopgake'n biyakten shlliṉ xet'.
To shii ka choe'ḻwill Jesúza' Chioza', na' lle' beṉ'ka' nakgake'ne' txen, na' wṉabile' ḻegake': ―¿Non na beṉ'ka' nak'?
Na' che'gake'ne': ―Baḻe' nagake' nako' dii Juan wichoa nisa', na' zi baḻe' nagake' nako' Elíaza', na' zi baḻe' nagake' nako' to beṉ' wdix̱jee daa goll Chioza'ne' kani'yi, na' ba bibane' ladj beṉ' wetka'.
Na'ch chi'e ḻegake': ―Shera le', ¿nora nale nak'? Na'ch che' Pédrona'ne': ―Lin' Crístona', beena' nc̱heb Chioza' wseḻee.
Na'ch goll Jesúza' ḻegake' ni to kono ye'gake' ka'.
Na' chi'e ḻegake': ―Kon ka nchogbia' c̱ha', nad', Beṉ' Bseḻ' Chioza' Yell-lioni, biya dii wc̱hi' wsak'gake' nad'. Na' beṉ' golka' chṉabia' wzoagake' nad' ka'lə na' ka'kzə bx̱ozka' chṉabia' na' beṉ'ka' chli' chsedi leya'. Na' chonan byen witgake' nad', na' ka gak shoṉ lla yiban' ladj beṉ' wetka'.
Na'ch golle' yog'ḻoḻe': ―Shi no cheeni gon nad' txen, chiyaḻ' wsanlall' kwine' na' izanile' yeḻ' mban c̱he'na' yen ile'ile' bittez ni c̱ha', na' gone' ka chazlallaa.
Ḻa' beena' bi chzani yeḻ' mban c̱he'na' yen ile'ile' bittez ni c̱ha', beenan' kwiayi'. San beena' chzani yeḻ' mban c̱he'na' ni c̱ha', beenan' gat' to yeḻ' mban c̱he' zejḻi kaṉi.
Bibi zjanayin gap beṉ' yog'ḻoḻ daa de yell-lioni, shi ḻe' kwiayee.
Nottezə beṉ' chiyii chido'i nad' na' c̱he cho'a xtillaana', ka'kz nad', Beṉ' Bseḻ' Chioza' Yell-lioni, yiyii yido'id' ḻe' kat' yiyed' kon balaaṉ xen c̱ha'na', na' c̱he X̱a' Chioza' na' c̱he anjl c̱he'ka'.
Na' dii ḻi nia' le', baḻ-le lle'le ni, ni mbanle kat' wli' Chioza' yeḻ' wṉabia' c̱he'na'.
Ka gok do to xman wna Jesúza' ka', na'ch wyaje' to lo yaa kwenc̱he jeḻwille' Chioza' na' bc̱hi'e Pédrona', Juanna' na' Jacóbona'.
Na' shlak choe'ḻwille' Chioza', biyak cho'alawe'na' nlla'lə, na' biyak xe'na' xtil ax̱t chey cheeni'n.
Na' gokx̱e c̱hop beṉ' bshaljlengake'ne', toe' dii Moiséza' na' beena' sto Elíaza'.
Na' yeḻ' chey cheeni'na' nec̱hjan ḻegake'. Na' chshaljlengake'ne' c̱he ka nak yeḻ' wita' ile'ile' Jerusalénna'.
Na' Pédrona' len Juanna' na' Jacóbona' ḻe chakxwesgake', per bendiplall'gake' bi wtesgake', na'ch ble'gakile' yeḻ' chey cheeni' c̱he Jesúza' na' c̱he beṉ'ka' zi c̱hop bllin kwite'na'.
Na' ka ba chikwas dii Moiséza' na' Elíaza' kwit Jesúza', Pédrona' golle' Jesúza': ―Maestro, ¡ḻe wen zoacho nizə! Gonnto' shoṉə ransh, to c̱ho', to c̱he dii Moiséza' na' sto c̱he Elíaza'. Na' ni bi gokbe'i Pédrona' bin golle'.
Na' ni choe'tie' dill', ka wze to bej gana' lle'gake' na' bkwashaan ḻegake'. Na' ḻe bllebgake' ka gokbe'gakile' ba yoogake' ḻoo beja'.
Na' ḻoo beja' bengakile' shii Chioza', chi'e ḻegake': ―Beenin xiiṉaa, na' ḻe chakidee. Ḻi wzenag c̱he'.
Na' ka wde goll Chioza' ḻegake' ka', na' ble'gakile' stozə Jesúza' ze. Na' ni to kono gollgake' daa ben ble'gakile'.
Betiyo, ka biyetjgake' lo yaana', beṉ' zan wal jatiḻgake' ḻegake'.
Na'ch ladj beṉ'ka' wṉe to beṉ' byo zillj, chi'e Jesúza': ―Maestro, ben goklen bwiagach bi' c̱ha'ni, ḻa' tlish' tyajchgabaan zoa.
Dii x̱iwaa chox̱a'n ḻeb' na' tokonganz chosyaab', na' chonan ka chazb' shoṉ ax̱t chbia bllin' cho'abaa. Na' chiya dii chonin ḻeb', na' aga cheenin wsanan ḻeb'.
Ba got'yoid' beṉ'ki nakgake' li' txen yibejgachgake' dii x̱iwaa yoob', na' bi gokgake' yibejgake'n.
Na'ch che' Jesúza': ―¡Zi'tegalə c̱helena', le' beṉ' mal na' beṉ' bi chajḻe'! ¿Zi ka'k'tek chiyaḻ' soalen' le'? Na' ¿zi ka'k'tek chiyaḻ' soid' le'? Da diwa' bi' c̱ho'na' ni.
Na' ka zej bi'na' kwit Jesúza' na' wchooṉ dii x̱iwaa ḻeb' lo yona' na' wyazb' shoṉa' sto shii. Na'ch bsheshlen Jesúza' dii x̱iwaa na' bichejan, na' biyakib'. Na' biyone'b' lall' na' x̱abaa.
Na' yog' beṉ'ka' lle' na' bibangakile' daa ble'gakile' yeḻ' wak xen c̱he Chioza'. Na' shlak chibani yog' beṉ'ka' ble'i daa ben Jesúza', na' golle' beṉ'ka' nakgake'ne' txen:
―Ḻi wzeyeṉ' nagle dga iṉia' le': gongake' nad', Beṉ' Bseḻ' Chioza' Yell-lioni, lall' na' beṉ'ka' chakzi' chakzbani nad'.
Na' bi wyajni'gakile' bin golle', ḻa' ni ngashaan lawe'ka' kwenc̱he bi shajni'gakile'n. Na' bllebgake' iṉabgakile'ne' bi zejin daa golle' ḻegake'.
Na' wzolo chakdiḻ-len ljwellgake' nogaken' nak beṉ' zak'chi.
Ka gokbe'i Jesúza' daa chza'lall'gake', na'ch wdoyoe' to bi'do' na' bzie'b' kwite'na'.
Na' chi'e ḻegake': ―Nottezə beṉ' wlebe' ḻaa to bi'do'zə ka bi'do'ni daa chonḻilallee nad', nad'kzan chlebe'. Na' beena' chlebe' nad', ḻekzka' chlebe' Chioza', beena' bseḻ' nad'. Na' beena' chaki bibi zakee lao yog'le, ḻen' nake' beṉ' zak'chi ladjlena'.
Na'ch goll Juanna'ne': ―Maestro, ba ble'into' to beṉ' chzetje' lio'na' kwenc̱he chibeje' dii x̱iw'ka' yoo beṉ'. Na' bllonnto' gone' ka', ḻa' bi nake' cho' txen.
Na' che' Jesúza' ḻegake': ―Bi wllonle gone' ka', ḻa' beena' bi chakile' cho' zi', txenkzan nake' cho'.
Na' ka ba zoa yiyaj Jesúza' yabana', na'ch btoblallee yiyaje' Jerusalénna'.
Na' bseḻee beṉ' wllialozegagake' na' wyajgake' to yell daa mbani Samáriana' jtiljgake' gana' yigaaṉe'.
Na' beṉ' Samáriaka' bi blebgake'ne' daa ṉezgakile' Jerusalénna'lan yiyaje'.
Na' c̱hop beṉ'ka' nakgake'ne' txen, Jacóbona' len Juanna', ka ble'gakile' ka ben beṉ' Samáriaka', na' che'gake' Jesúza': ―X̱an', ¿acheenilo' iṉabinto' Chioza' wseḻee yi'na' kwenc̱he sheytega beṉ'ki?
Na' biyec̱hj Jesúza' bsheshlene' ḻegake', chi'e: ―Aga ṉezile non chṉabia' yic̱hjlall'do'lena' nazle ka'.
Nad', Beṉ' Bseḻ' Chioza' Yell-lioni, aga zaa kwenc̱he wlliayaa yeḻ' mban c̱he beṉ', san zaa kwenc̱he yisla' yeḻ' mban c̱he'kan'. Na'ch biyajgake' yell yoblə.
Na' ka zejgake' tneza', to beṉ' chi'e Jesúza': ―X̱an', cheenid' sa'len' li' gattezə shajo'.
Na' che' Jesúza'ne': ―Zoa yech ga chiyoo bez'ka', na' byiṉdo'ka' non lilldo'gakb, san nad', Beṉ' Bseḻ' Chioza' Yell-lioni, biga de yigaaṉ'.
Na'ch che' Jesúza' sto beṉ': ―Da dino nad'. Na' beena' chi'ene': ―X̱an', ben goklen be' latj zigaate lljakwashaa x̱a'na'.
Na'ch che' Jesúza'ne': ―Bibi gakilo', wikwash'kzə ljwell beṉ' wetka'. San li', jtix̱je'i beṉ' ka nak yeḻ' wṉabia' c̱he Chioza'.
Na'ch sto beṉ' yoblə chizi'e Jesúza': ―X̱an', cheenid' sa'len' li' per zigaate be' latj lljaḻaach' dill' bish' ljwell'ka'.
Na' che' Jesúza'ne': ―To beṉ' chwaaṉe' gooṉ, aga wak wwie' gozkoll'lə. Na' ka'kzan nakan c̱he beena' noe' nad', shi bi nc̱hoglallee aga wak gone' ka cheeni Chioza'.
Na' ka wde dga, Jesúza' wleje' zi guiyon shi beṉ' na' bseḻee c̱hop weje' wllialogake' lawe'na' kwenc̱he llje'gake' cho'a xtilleena' yellka' gana' llia bia' shaje'.
Na' golle' ḻegake': ―Dii ḻi nia' le', dii xen wal daa yizi' yilaple de, na' to c̱hoptgui wen llinka' zoa. Na' ḻi iṉabi Chioza', beena' nak x̱an llinna' wseḻ'stoe' wen llinka' kwenc̱he yizi' yilapgake'n.
Ḻi shajshki ṉaa, nad' chseḻaa le' ka xil'do' ba zej ladj ba zṉia.
Bi wa'le ga koo xshinḻazle, ni mech, ni zi shkwe' xel-le; na' bi shazile wwaple beṉ' chiox tneza'.
Na' ka sho'le to lill beṉ', zigaate wwaplene' chiox, ye'lene': “Soashgale mbalaz, le' zoale yooni.”
Na' shi zoa beṉ' cheenile' soe' mbalaz, na' yeḻ' mbalaza' yigaaṉlenan ḻe'. Na' shi bi cheenile', na' yibiilenan le'.
Na' yoona' gana' illinle na'tezə yigaaṉle na' yeej gaole kon bi goṉgake' le', ḻa' to wen llin chiyaḻ' ikaa laxje'. Na' bi lljsoale to to yoo.
Kat' illinle to yell ga wlebgake' le', yeej gaotezle bittezə dii goṉgake' le'.
Na' yiyonle beṉ'ka' bi shao' yella', na' ye'le ḻegake': “Yeḻ' wṉabia' c̱he Chioza' ba bla'n laoleni.”
Na' shi illinle to yell ga bi wlebgake' le', ḻi yide lyell, ḻi ye'gake':
“Ax̱t bishte c̱he yell c̱heleni wllia ṉi'anto'ni chibibnto'n kwenc̱he gakbe'ile aga wenan chonle bi chleble cho'a xtill' Chioza'. Na' ḻi koosha yic̱hjle dga iṉanto' le', yeḻ' wṉabia' c̱he Chioza'n ba bla'n laoleni.”
Na' nia' le', beṉ'ka' lle' yellka' gana' bi wlebgake' le', dii xench nak yeḻ' zak'zi'na' ile'gakile' aga ka beṉ' yell Sodómaka' llana' wc̱hoglo Chioza' c̱he beṉ'.
’¡Nyesh'laz gak c̱hele, le' beṉ' yell Corazín na' le' beṉ' yell Betsaida! Ḻa' sheḻ' gok yeḻ' wakka' yell Tírona' na' Sidónna' ka diika' ba gok ladjlena', kana'telja biyaj bilengakile' saaxya c̱he'ka', na' ba wche'gake' bwazjgake' dena' yic̱hjlaogake' na' gokwgake' lech' zeshaa, kwenc̱he wli'gake' nan ba biyaj bilengakile' daa chongake', sheḻ'ka'.
Kat' illin lla wc̱hoglo Chioza' c̱he beṉ', yeḻ' zi' xench ile'ile aga ka beṉ' yell Tíroka' na' beṉ' yell Sidonka'.
Na' le' beṉ' yell Capernaúm, bi gonle lez yillinle yabana', ḻa' Chioza' wzaḻee le' gana' sak'zi'le.
Na'ch che' Jesúza' beṉ'ka' bseḻee: ―Beṉ'ka' chzenaggake' c̱hele, c̱ha'kzan chzenaggake'. Na' beṉ'ka' bi chlebgake' le', nad'kzan bi chlebgake'. Na' beena' bi chlebe' nad', ḻekzka' bi chlebe' Chioza', beena' bseḻ' nad'.
Na' beṉ'ka' guiyon shi ḻe chibagakile' ka billingake' kwit Jesúza', na' che'gake'ne': ―X̱an', ax̱t dii x̱iw'ka' chilleshgakan ka chzetjnto' lio'na'.
Na'ch che' Jesúza' ḻegake': ―Ble'id' Satanáza' daa chṉabia' dii x̱iw'ka' bxopan yabana' ka chxop to yi' wziw'.
Nad' ba beṉ' le' yeḻ' waka' kwenc̱he ḻa'kzi gad' no beḻ zṉia wa no bex̱joni' le' aga bi gakile', na' wlej wshoshjtele yog' daa chon dii x̱iwaa.
Per bi yibaile daa chisheshle dii x̱iw'ka', san ḻi yibayi daa ba da' lelena' ḻee libra' de yabana'.
