Na' katena' Espíritu Sántona' bene' ka bibachgayi Jesúza', na' wne': ― X̱a, li' nako' X̱an yabana' na' yell-lioni, na' choe'lawaa li' daa ba bliilo' beṉ'ka' bibi chajnii daa bi bliilo' beṉ' sin'ka' na' beṉ'ka' nteyi. Kan' ba wyazlalloo gono', X̱a.
’X̱a'na' ba none' lall' na' yog'te dii de. Na' ni to kono ṉezi noyeṉ'an' nak' nad' Xiiṉe'; toz X̱a'na' ṉezile'n. Na' ni to kono ṉezi noyeṉ'an' nak X̱a'na'; toz nad' Xiiṉe' ṉezid', na' chon' ka iṉezi beṉ'ka' cheenid' iṉezgakile'n.
Na'ch biyec̱hje' bwie' beṉ'ka' nakgake'ne' txen, chi'e ḻegake': ―Chakomba beṉ'ka' chle'gakile' diika' chle'ile ṉaa.
Nia' le' ka', ḻa' zan beṉ'ka' wdix̱jee daa goll Chioza' ḻegake' na' zan beṉ' wṉabia'ka' goklall'gake' ile'gakile' diiki chle'ile ṉaa, na' bi ble'gakile'n. Goklall'gake' yengakile' dga chenile ṉaa, na' bi bengakile'n.
Na'ch wbig' to beṉ' chli' chsedi leya' wṉabile' Jesúza' kwenc̱hezə iṉezile' shi wak yillii Jesúza' xtilleena', na' wṉabile'ne': ―Maestro, ¿bin chiyaḻ' gon' kwenc̱he gat' to yeḻ' mban c̱ha' zejḻi kaṉi?
Na'ch che' Jesúza'ne': ―¿Bin na leya' chiyaḻ' goncho? ¿Bi na daa chlabo'?
Na'ch beena' chli' chsedi leya' chi'e: ―“Chiyaḻ' gakicho X̱ancho Chioza' do yic̱hj do lall'cho, do ka nak fuerz c̱hechona', na' ax̱t ga zeelo chajniicho; na' gaki bish' ljwellcho ka chaki kwincho.”
Na'ch che' Jesúza'ne': ―Kayeṉ'nan nakan ka ba wno'. Shi gono' ka nan, na' gat' to yeḻ' mban c̱ho' zejḻi kaṉi.
Na' beena' bi goklall' wṉit kwine', na'ch chi'ene': ―¿Noran bish' ljwell'?
Na'ch che' Jesúza'ne': ―To beṉ' ziyo'e nez daa ziza' Jerusalénna' daa ziyaj Jericólə, na' bchej wbanka' tneza' wlangake' yog'te diika' zino'e ax̱t len xe'na' daa nakwe' goljgake', na' bet wdingake'ne', sto chdoaze' bengake', na' bixoṉjgake'.
Na' shintk gok ka' ka wde to bx̱oz lo neza'. Na' ka ble'ile' beena' de na', to wdeze' ka'lə.
Na' ḻekzka' wde to beṉ' nake' xiiṉ dia c̱he dii Levína'. Na' ka ble'ile' chtoḻ beena' na', ḻekzka' to wdeze' ka'lə.
Na' sto beṉ' Samaria ḻekzka' zeje' tneza' ka ble'ile' beena' chtoḻ na', na' biyeshile'ne'.
Na' jabiguee kwite'na', na'ch bllie' lo we'na' set na'ch vino, na' bc̱heje'n. Na' biḻepe'ne' koll' bayix̱' c̱he'na', bic̱hi'ene' to yoo gana' wdape'ne'.
Na' betiyo, ka ba zoa yiza' beṉ' Samáriana', wleje' c̱hop mech plat, na' bi'en x̱an yoona' kwenc̱he gap wwie'ne' zan lla, na' chi'ene': “Wdap bwiagach beeni, na' shi bi gaki mechi chkwaaṉ', na' yiyixja'n kat' zizaa dii yoblə.”
Na' ¿nora beṉ'ki shoṉ chakilo' beni bish' ljwell beena' wlan beṉ' wbanka'?
Na' beena' chli' chsedi leya' chi'ene': ―Beena' biyeshile'ne'. Na' che' Jesúza'ne': ―Ḻekzka' li', kan' chiyaḻ' gono'.
Na' shlak ngoo Jesúza' nez, blline' to yelldo' na' to noolə le Marta blebe'ne' lille'na'.
Na' zoa to beṉ' bil Mártana' lie' María, na' Maríana' wchi'e lao Jesúza' chzenague' dillaa cho'e.
Na' Mártana', dechga daa gone' na' wzeche' wṉeyi c̱heyin, na'ch wyaje' kwit Jesúza', chi'ene': ―X̱an', goll-lat' beṉ' bila'ni gaklene' nad'. Toz' ndakw' yog' mandadka'.
Na' che' Jesúza'ne': ―Marta, Marta, chi'chga yic̱hjo' na' zechgo' wneyi c̱heyi diika' gono'.
Per toz daa de nakan dii llialoch na' Maríani ba wleje'n, na' kono gak yikaan lawe'na'.
Shlin choe'ḻwill Jesúza' Chioza' to latj, na' ka biyoll be'ḻwille'ne', to beena' nake'ne' txen golle'ne': ―X̱an', bli'yi neto' nakan chiyaḻ' we'ḻwillnto' Chioza', ka ben Juanna' bli' bsedile' beṉ'ka' bengake'ne' txen.
Na'ch che' Jesúza' ḻegake': ―Kat' we'ḻwill-le Chioza' kin iṉale: X̱anto' Chios, beṉ' zoa yaba, we'la'oshga yog'ḻoḻ beṉ' li'. Na' iṉabia'gacho' ḻoo yic̱hjlall'do' yog'ḻoḻ beṉ' kwenc̱he gak lo yell-lioni ka chazlalloo, kon ka chak yabana'.
Ka nak daa choṉo' cheej chaonto' yog' lla, beṉgachan ṉaanlla.
Wxi'xen c̱hento', ka chon neto' chzi'xennto' bittezə dii choni beṉ' neto'. Bi we'gacho' latj ibix̱nto' gonnto' daa bi nak wen, san bislagach neto' lo ṉi'a na' dii mala'.
Na'ch che' Jesúza' ḻegake': ―Iṉatezcho shi zoa to beṉ' nllaguile na' do chel shajle lille'na' na' ye'lene': “Beṉ' bish'dawaa, beṉ shloll nad' shoṉ yetxtil,
ḻa' ba bla' lilla'na' to beṉ' nllaguid', zee zit', na' bikzə bi de c̱ha' wshabidee.”
Na'ch beena' yoo ḻoolə lii iṉatie' le': “Bi gonzilo' nad' zed, ba nsejl' lillii na' ba delen' bi' c̱ha'ki. Aga wak c̱has' goṉ' daa chyalljilo'.”
Na' nia' le', ḻa'kzi nllagteile'ne', bi c̱hase' wi'ene' daa chṉabile'ne'. San shi seyide' iṉabe'n, chen ki cheenile' c̱hase' wi'e yog' daa chyalljile.
Daan nia' le': Ḻi iṉabi Chioza' bin cheenile na' goṉe'n. Ḻi yiyiljan na' willelkzilen. Ḻi wtankw ḻee puerta', na' wsaljkze'n.
Ḻa' beena' chṉabile' to bi chṉabile' beṉ', cho'ene'n; na' beena' chiyilje' bi chiyilje', chillelkzile'n; na' beena' chtankwe' to ḻee puert, na' chsaljkzgake'n.
’Ka chak c̱hele le' nakle beṉ' chisgol chischoo bi'do', ka iṉabi xiiṉlena' le' yetxtila', aga we'leb' to yaj. Wa shi iṉabib' le' to beḻ gaob', aga we'leb' to beḻ zṉia.
Wa shi iṉabib' le' to llit gaob', aga we'leb' to bex̱joni'.
Le' naktele beṉ' mal, chak we'le xiiṉleka' daa nak dii wen. ¡Na' X̱acho Chioza' zoa yabana' nakteche' beṉ' wench! Na' wi'e Espíritu Santo c̱he'na' soe' ḻoo yic̱hjlall'do' yog' beṉ' iṉabe'ne'.
Jesúza' chibeje' to dii x̱iw' yoo to beṉ' bi chak iṉie', na' ka bichejan na'ch gok biṉie'. Na' beṉ'ka' lle' na', bibangakile' daa bene'.
Na' baḻe' che'gake': ―Kon yeḻ' wak c̱he Bezlona', daa chṉabia' dii x̱iw'kan', chibeji beeni dii x̱iw'ka'.
Na' zi baḻe' wṉabgakile'ne' gone' to yeḻ' wak dii ile'gakile' kwenc̱he wli'n shi Chioza'kzan bseḻeene'.
Na' ba ṉezli Jesúza' daa chza'lall'gake', na'ch chi'e ḻegake': ―Shi beṉ'ka' lle' to yell gakgake' c̱hoplə na' tiḻ-len ljwellgake', na' kwiayi' yella', shi ṉaa. Na' ḻekzka' shi beṉ'ka' lle' toz yoo tiḻ-len ljwellgake', aga ssha soagake' toz.
Na' ka'kzə Satanáza' na' dii x̱iw'ka' yoo lo na'yin, shi gakgakan c̱hoplə na' kwiayi' yeḻ' wṉabia' c̱heyinna'. Nia' le' ka' daa nale yeḻ' wak c̱he Bezlonan chibejid' dii x̱iw'ka' yoo beṉ'.
Shi chibej' dii x̱iwaa yoo beṉ' kon yeḻ' wak c̱he Bezlona', ¿sheralə beṉ'ka' nakle txen? ¿Aḻekzka' ḻennan' chibejlengake' dii x̱iwaa yoo beṉ'? Daa bi nakan ka', chli'n nakllejilen.
Na' daa chibej' dii x̱iwaa yoo beṉ' kon yeḻ' wak c̱he Chioza', ḻennan' chli'n ba bla' yeḻ' wṉabia' c̱he Chioza' ladjleni.
’Kat' to beṉ' wal nape' dii gonile' zṉia na' chape' lille'na', aga no gak lljtoyo dii de c̱he'.
Per shi illin sto beṉ' walch tiḻ-lene'ne', na' gone'ne' gan, na'ch yigoyoe' yog' daa none' lez wṉiaile', na' kwantie' yog' daa yoo ḻoo lille'na' na' wi'e lat' wej c̱he beṉ'ka' nakgake'ne' txen.
’Beena' bi nake' nad' txen, chakzbanile' nad'. Na' beena' bi chaklen kwenc̱he wzenag beṉ' cho'a xtill' Chioza', ḻen' chsej chllone' wzenaggake'n.
’Kat' chichej to dii x̱iw' dii yoo beṉ', na' chjadan ga bibi dekzə na' chyiljan gana' yizi'lalliin. Na' shi bi chllelin gana' yizi'lalliin na'ch chakin: “Yiyaachkz' dii yoblə gana' bichejkz'.”
Na' ka chillinan gana' bichejan, nakan ka to ḻoo yoo dii nxi nḻoa na' nakan xochi.
Na'ch chza'n chjx̱i'n zi gall dii x̱iw'ka' daa nakch dii malch aga ka ḻen, na' yogaan choogakan beena'. Na' chaktechlə mal c̱he beena' aga ka gok c̱he' dii nech.
Na' shlak che' Jesúza' ka', to noolə zie' ladj beṉ'ka' lle' na' wṉie' zilljə, chi'e: ―¡Chakomba noola' wxane' li' na' bwall bx̱ope' li'!
Na' che' Jesúza'ne': ―¡Mbalazch beṉ'ka' chzenaggake' cho'a xtill' Chioza' na' chongake' ka nan!
Na' bdi'a bllagch beṉ'ka' kwit Jesúza' na' golle' ḻegake': ―Le' zoale ṉaa, nxiṉj yic̱hjlall'do'leka'. Chṉable wliid' le' to yeḻ' wak, na' aga wliid' le' daa cheenile. Ḻete ile'ile to dii nak ka yeḻ' waka' daa ben Chioza' c̱he dii Jonáza'.
Daa gok c̱he Jonáza' bli'n yeḻ' wak c̱he Chioza' lao beṉ' Níniveka'. Kakzə nad', Beṉ' Bseḻ' Chioza' Yell-lioni, wli'a yeḻ' wak c̱he Chioza' laolena', le' zoale ṉaa.
Na' llana' wc̱hoglo Chioza' c̱he beṉ', na' yiban noola' wṉabia' do lli'lə, na' gawe' xya c̱hele lao Chioza', le' zoale ṉaa, iṉe' chiyaḻ' sak'zi'le. Ḻa' noola', zit' wal wzee bidzenague' dill' sin'na' daa be' dii Salomónna', na' nad' zoa' ni, nak' beṉ' zak'chi ka dii Salomónna', na' bi chzenagle c̱ha'.
Na' ḻekzka' llana' wc̱hoglo Chioza' c̱he beṉ', na' yiban beṉ' Níniveka' na' gaogake' xya c̱hele lao Chioza', le' zoale ṉaa, iṉagake' chiyaḻ' sak'zi'le. Ḻa' ḻegake' biyaj bileni saaxya c̱he'ka' ka be'len Jonáza' ḻegake' cho'a xtill' Chioza', na' nad' zoa' ni, nak' beṉ' zak'chi ka dii Jonáza', na' bi chzenagle c̱ha'.
Na' ḻekzka' chi'e ḻegake': ―Biga zoa beṉ' chxene' to kandil na' chzoe'n to ga ngash' wa wdoseen to dii wkwashaan ḻen, san chzoe'n sibə kwenc̱he ile'i beṉ'ka' sho' ḻoo yoona'.
Jalawo'ka' nakan ka to yi' c̱he kwerp c̱ho'na'. Shi jalawo'na' nakan wen, doxen kwerp c̱ho'na' zoan lo beeni'na'. San shi bi chle'i jalawo'na', kwerp c̱ho'na' zoan lo yel c̱hola'.
Na' bsak' wze wṉeyi kwenc̱he ki lwaa to' lo beeni'na', tazo' lo yel c̱hoḻa'lə.
Shi doxen kwerp c̱ho'na' yoon beeni', na' ni to dii shgasj shc̱hoḻ bi yoon, na' ile'ilo' kwasḻoḻ ka chle'ilo' kat' ze to yi' chzeeni'n doxen.
Na' ka biyoll be' Jesúza' dillaa, na' bc̱he' to fariseo ḻe' lljtawe' lille'na'. Na' wyoo Jesúza' lille'na' na' wchi'e cho'a mesa'.
Na' farisewa' bibanile' ka ble'ile' bi bina' Jesúza' ka yoologake' chongake' ka zi' gaogake'.
Na'ch che' X̱ancho Jesúza'ne': ―Le' fariseo nakle ka xig' yeeṉ dii nyib x̱ise' tcho'a tlawin na' ḻo'inna' besjan. Chaki beṉ' ḻe beṉ' wen nakle, len le' chibaile chkaale bi de c̱he beṉ' na' chibaile chonle bichlə dii mal.
¡Le' beṉ' bi nteyi! ¿Abi chakbe'ile Chioza', beena' ben kwerp c̱hechoni, ḻekze'n bene' yic̱hjlall'do'choni?
Ḻi izani bi de c̱hele, ḻi we'n beṉ' bibi de c̱he', na'ch yixi' yiyech yic̱hjlall'do'lena'.
’¡Nyesh'laz gak c̱hele, le' fariseo! Choe'le Chioza' lat' wej no yix̱wej, no kwanirod na' bichlə yix̱' kwan dii mbekle. Na' bi chonle daa nak shḻicha na' bi chakteile' Chioza'. Ḻa' daayeṉ'an llialoch gonle per ḻekzka' bi wsanle kwejle daa chṉab Chioza'.
’¡Nyesh'laz gak c̱hele, le' fariseo! Ḻe chibaile kwe'le gana' chbe' beṉ'ka' zakii gana' chdop chllagcho choe'ḻwillcho Chioza', na' cheenile yog' beṉ' kwee le' balaaṉ ga lle' lla' beṉ'.
’¡Nyesh'laz gak c̱hele, daa nakle beṉ' wxiye'! Nakle ka to ba c̱he beṉ' wet dii bi nla' lawinna' dii bi chle'i beṉ' na' chaj chdegake' lawinna', ni bi chakbe'gakile' bin naki ḻoolə.
Na'ch to beena' chli' chsedi leya' golle' Jesúza': ―Maestro, daa no' ka' len neto' chzoazi'yoo.
Na' goll Jesúza': ―¡Ḻekzka' nyesh'laz gak c̱hele, le' chli' chsedile leya'! Dii zan dii che'le beṉ' chiyaḻ' gongake', na' nakan ka to yoa' xen dii chwa'le ḻegake' dii kono soyi, na' le' bikz bi chda na'le kwenc̱he gaklenle ḻegake'.
’¡Nyesh'laz gak c̱hele! Le' chonshao'zle cho'a ba c̱he dii beṉ'ka' wdix̱jee daa goll Chioza' ḻegake', beṉ'ka' bet dii x̱ozxto'leka'.
Na' daa chonle ka' zejin chonle txen dii x̱ozxto'leka' ka nak daa bengake'. Ḻa' ḻegaken' betgake' beṉ'ka', na' le' chonshao'le cho'a ba c̱he'ka'.
’Na' daan, lo yeḻ' sin' c̱he Chioza' wne': “Wseḻaa beṉ' c̱hix̱jee daa yepee na' len beṉ' wi'e cho'a xtillaana', na' baḻe' witgake' na' zi baḻe' biya dii gongakile'ne'.”
Na' le' zoale ṉaa, lenle ile'ile ka yeḻ' zi'na' ile'i beṉ'ka' blalj xc̱hen dii beṉ'ka' wdix̱jee daa goll Chioza' ḻegake', wzolozan ka wxe wzil yell-lioni.
Le' zoale ṉaa, lenle chidoḻ'le sak'zi'le ni c̱he yeḻ' wit c̱he dii Abela' ax̱t dii Zacaríaza', beena' betgake' cho'a yoodo'na' kwit gana' chzeygake' bayix̱'ka'.
’¡Nyesh'laz gak c̱hele, le' chli' chsedile leya'! Ḻa' nazle chsedile beṉ' c̱he Chioza', per ni le' bi cheenile wzenagle daa nan, na' chllontele shajnii beṉ'ka' chzenagan.
Na' ka goll Jesúza' ka', beṉ'ka' chli' chsedi leya' na' fariseoka' zizikli bllaagake' na' wzologake' chongakile'ne' zed wal wṉabgakile'ne' chiya dii nak lallj,
goklall'gake' we' Jesúza' dill' dii wchix̱a'n ḻe'.
Na'ch bdop bllag beṉ' zan inlleb gana' zoa Jesúza' ax̱t chdakw ljwellgake', na' wzoloe' zigaate be'lene' beṉ'ka' nakgake'ne' txen dill', chi'e: ―Wsak'gale bi shajḻe'le dill' wxiye' c̱he fariseoka' daa zaklebi levadúrana'.
Ḻa' daa kono ṉezi ṉaa, wllin lla iṉezi beṉaan, na' yog'ḻoḻ daa ngash' ṉaa, wllin lla ila' lawin.
Na' yog' daa chakile kono beni daa wnale, wllin lla iṉezgakile'n. Na' daa wnale ka yoole ḻoolə nsejshoshle yoona', ax̱t gosya'i beṉ' wzie'n dill'.
’Le' nllaguid', nia' le' bi illeble beṉ'ka' witgake' le', ḻa' kachokzan zeelo gak gongakile' le'.
Per ni iṉia' le' non chiyaḻ' illeble: ḻi illeb Chioza', ḻa' ka yiyoll yikee yeḻ' mban c̱helena' ḻekzka' nape' yeḻ' wṉabia' wzaḻee le' lo yi' gabiḻa'. Ḻen', ḻi illeb.
’Ṉezicho wak si'cho gay' byiṉdo' kon c̱hop sintabdo'. Ḻa'kzi aga bitek zak'gakb, ni tob bi mbej yic̱hj Chioza'.
Na' ka'kzə le', ax̱t to to yish' yic̱hjlena' mbab. Na' bi illeble, ḻa' zak'chle aga ka zan byiṉdo'ka'.
’Na' nia' le', beena' wc̱heb lao beṉ' nake' nad' txen, ḻekzka' nad', Beṉ' Bseḻ' Chioza' Yell-lioni, wi'a dill' lao yog'ḻoḻ anjl c̱he Chioza', yepgakee beeni nake' nad' txen.
San beena' bi wc̱heb nake' nad' txen, ḻekzka' nad', wi'a dill' lao yog'ḻoḻ anjl c̱he Chioza', yepgakee beeni bi nake' nad' txen.
’Na' beena' biz gon iṉa c̱ha', nad', Beṉ' Bseḻ' Chioza' Yell-lioni, wizi'xen Chioza' c̱he', san beena' iṉe zban c̱he Espíritu Sántona', aga wizi'xen Chioza' c̱he'.
’Kat' lljwa'gake' le' lao beṉ'ka' chṉabia' gana' chdop chllagcho choe'ḻwill-cho Chioza', wa lao beṉ' chc̱hogbia' c̱he beṉ' wa lao josc̱his, bi sele wṉeyi naklə yilliile cho'a xtill' beṉ'ka' wa bin iṉale.
Ḻa' kat' iṉele, Espíritu Sántona'kzan wzajniile' le' daa chiyaḻ' iṉale.
Na' ladj beṉ'ka' ndop nllag wṉe to beṉ', golle' Jesúza': ―Maestro, gollgach beṉ' bishaana' goṉe' daa chidoḻ' ikaa c̱he dii x̱anto'na'.
Na' che' Jesúza'ne': ―¿Nora bzoa nad' ladjleni ka to beṉ' chon yeḻ' josc̱his c̱he beṉ' wa beṉ' chḻaa bi dii de c̱he beṉ'?
Na' ḻekzka' chi'e: ―Ḻi wsak' kwenc̱he bi selall'le gat'ch bi gat' c̱hele, ḻa' aga dii kan' llialo lo yeḻ' mban c̱helena'.
Na'ch bzoe' to jempl, chi'e ḻegake': ―Wzoa to beṉ' wni'a na' dii zan bizi' bilape' lo yell-lio c̱he'na'.
Na'ch chakile': “¿Nakra ka gona'n ṉaa? Biga de kooshawaa dga bizi' bilap'.”
Na'ch wne': “Ba ṉezid' bi gon'. Yic̱hiṉj' yoona' gana' chgooshawaa daa chizi' chilap' na' yiyona'n dii xench, na' kooshawaa daa bizi' bilap' na' bichlə dii de c̱ha'.
Na'ch zan yiz yizia' banez c̱he daa ngooshawaa, na' yizi'lallaa na' yeej gaw', na' soa' mbalaz.”
Na' goll Chioza'ne': “Li', beṉ' bi nteyi, ṉaanlle' gueto' na' daa ngooshawoo, nola c̱heyi gakan.”
Kan' gak c̱he beena' chtop chshag yeḻ' wni'ana', na' bibi zakee lao Chioza'.
Ka wde dga, Jesúza' golle' beṉ'ka' nakgake'ne' txen: ―Ṉaa nia' le': Bi sele wṉeyi c̱he daa yeej gaole, ni bi sele wṉeyi c̱he xalaanlena'.
Ḻa' zak'techlə yeḻ' mban c̱helena' aga ka daa yeej gaole, na' zak'tech xkwerplena' aga ka xalaanlena'.
Ḻi wwiakachi bec̱hjka', ḻa'kzi bi chaz chaaṉgakb na' bibi chizi' chilapgakb, ni bi zoa ga chgooshao'gakb dii gaogakb, len chweej chwaokz Chioza' ḻegakb. Na' le', ṉaa, zak'techle aga ka bado'ka' ze lo llazə.
Ni tole bi gak yisc̱hoochle yeḻ' mban c̱helena' ni zi tgor ḻa'kzi nall inlleb selen wṉeyi.
Shi dga nak diido'zə bi chak gonlen, ¿berac̱he zezle wṉeyi c̱he bichlə dii yoblə?
’Ḻi wwiakachi ka chgol yejdo'ka', len aga bi llin chongakan ni bi choḻgakan do. Na' nia' le', ni Salomónna', beena' wdapchga yeḻ' shao'ka', bi bllin gak xe'na' xochi ka yejdo'ka'.
Shi Chioza' none' xochi yejdo'ka' ze lyix̱aa, ḻa'kzi xtitchgan mbanan na'ch wtop beṉ' ḻen wlli'en lo yi'na', ¿alechlin ki gone' c̱hele, ḻa'kzi bitek chajḻe'le gaklene' le'?
Na' daan bi setekle wṉeyi ga sa' daa yeej gaole.
Ḻa' beṉ'ka' bi nonḻilall'gake' Chioza' to daazə chinogake'. Per le', Chioza' nake' X̱ale, na' ṉezile' chyalljilen.
Ḻi se wṉeyi wzenagle c̱he Chioza' kwenc̱he iṉabi'e le', na' goṉkze' yog' daa chyalljile.
’Bi illeble. Ḻa'kzi bi nyanle, X̱acho Chioza', yeḻ' beṉ' wen c̱he'na', chaklallee yillinle iṉabia'lenlene' gana' chṉabi'e.
Ḻi wit' wde bi de c̱hele, na' ḻi gaklen beṉ' bibi de c̱heyin. Shi ka' gonle, na' gat' yeḻ' shao' c̱hele dii bi te c̱heyin yabana' gana' bi gak kwan wbanna'n, ni bi iteban.
Na' gana' de yeḻ' shao' c̱helena', na'kzan se yic̱hjlall'do'lena' wṉeyi.
Na' ḻekzka' chi'e ḻegake': ―Ḻi gakto ka wen llinka', beṉ'ka' chbezgake' x̱ane'ka' yilline' daa zeje' to ga chak wishagna'. Na' toshiizi chi'gake' chbezgake'ne' na' nox̱'tegake' yi' c̱he'ka' kwenc̱he kate wtankwe' ḻee puerta' lii wsaljtegake'n.
Chakomba wen llinka' chbezgake' kat' yillin x̱ane'ka', ḻa' dii ḻi nia' le', kwine' kweke' ḻegake' cho'a mesa' na' wi'e dii gaogake'.
Chakomba beṉ'ka' chbezgake' yillin x̱ane'ka' ḻa'kzi yilline' do chel wa do zbaḻzə.
Na' chiyaḻ' shajniile dga, sheḻ'ka' to x̱an yoo iṉezile' bi gor illin wbanna' lille'na', wbe'noe'ne' na' bi wi'e latj sho'e lille'na' kwane'.
Ka'kzan le' chiyaḻ' sele wṉeyi toshiizi kwezle nad', Beṉ' Bseḻ' Chioza' Yell-lioni, ḻa' tokonganzə yiyed'.
Na'ch wṉabi Pédrona' Jesúza', chi'ene': ―X̱an', ¿ato neto'zan no' ka', anti c̱he yog' beṉaan no' ka'?
Na'ch goll X̱ancho Jesúza': ―¿Nakra chakile chon to wen llin wen, beṉ' ṉezi nak gone' llinna', shi x̱ane'na' gone' lall' nee yog'te beṉ'ka' zoa ḻoo yoo lille'na' kwenc̱he wweej wwawe' ḻegake' gor c̱heyin?
Chakomba wen llinna' chilaḻile' chone' daa nak lall' nee ka yillin x̱ane'na'.
Dii ḻi nia' le', x̱ane'na' gone' lall' nee yog'ḻoḻ dii de c̱he'.
Na' shi wen llinna' gakile': “Akza ṉaa yila' x̱an'na'”, na'ch soloe' gonile' zban wen llinka' sto, ka nool ka beṉ' byo, na' soloe' yeej gawe' na' sollile'.
Na' tokonganzi yillin x̱ane'na' llana' bi none' lez, na' wdie'ne' to yeḻ' zi' wal kon ka ba nc̱hogloe' gak c̱he beṉ'ka' bi chongake' daa chiyaḻ' gongake'.
’Beṉ' wen llinna' ṉezi bin cheeni x̱ane'na' gone', na' bi chone'n ni bi zie'n wṉeyi, na' wit c̱hinchga x̱ane'na' ḻe'.
Per beena' bi ṉezi bin cheeni x̱ane'na' gone', na' chone' dii chonan ka wsak'zi' x̱ane'na'ne', agalə wsak'zi'teke'ne'. Ḻa' beena' be'lenyeṉee dill' nakan gone', chonan byen gonyeṉee ka bzajniile'ne'. Na' beena' ba bene' lall' nee gone' dii zan dii cheenile' gone', chonan byen gone' yog'ḻoḻte diika' bene' lall' nee.
’Daa bid' yell-lioni nakan ka iṉacho yin' bidxen'. Na' cheenchgaid' sheḻ' ṉaate ba chaḻ'ṉiṉan.
Biya dii yen ile'id', na' ḻe ba chakyeshid' ax̱t ni illini llana'.
¿Achakile bid' yell-lioni kwenc̱he gon' ka soalen ljwell beṉ' mbalaz? Aga kan', san daa bid' illaa ljwellgake' na' gakgake' c̱hoplə.
Ḻa' ṉaa, shi to yoo lle' gayee, na' gakgake' c̱hoplə, shoṉe' tiḻ-lengake' beṉ'ka' c̱hop, na' beṉ'ka' zi c̱hop tiḻ-lengake' beṉ'ka' zi shoṉə.
X̱a bi' byona' tiḻ-lene'b', na' ḻeb' tiḻ-lem' x̱abaa. Na' xṉa' bi' noola' tiḻ'lene'b', na' ḻeb' tiḻ-lem' xṉa'baa. Na' noola' tiḻ-lene' xoolille'na', na' xoolille'na' tiḻ-lene' ḻe'.
Na' ḻekzka' che' Jesúza' beṉ'ka' lle' na': ―Kat' chle'ile ziza' beja' gana' chxoalə wbilla', lii natele: “Wakə yeja'”, na' kayeṉ' chak.
Na' kat' chde be'na' daa za' lli'lə, na' nale: “Ḻe zey'chga yizak”, na' kayeṉ' chak.
¡Le' beṉ' wxiye'! Kat' chle'ile bin chak xan yabana' na' lo yell-lioni ṉezile beran gak. ¿Bic̱he bi chakbe'ile bin zeji daa chon Chioza' llaki zoacho ṉaa?
’¿Bic̱he ki chiyiljle to kwinzle daa nak dii ḻi dii shao'?
Shi no chao xya c̱hele na' wc̱hi'e le' lao josc̱hiska', ḻi gon byen yiyoe'xenlene' tneza'. Ḻa' shi lljwee le' lao beena' chc̱hogbia' c̱he beṉ', na' ḻe' gone' le' lo na' beena' wseje' le' lillyana'.
Na' nia' le', aga wichejle lillyana' ax̱t ki c̱hixjle doxen daa chiyaḻ' c̱hixjle.
Na' lo llana'tezə bllin baḻ beṉ' lao Jesúza' gollgake'ne' ka ben Pilátona' bene' mandad betgake' baḻ beṉ' Galiléaka' ka chitgake' bayix̱'ka' choe'la'ogake' Chioza'. Na' xc̱hene'ka' biyakan toz kon xc̱hen bayix̱'ka' betgake'.
Na' che' Jesúza' ḻegake': ―¿Achakile beṉ' Galiléaka' betgake' nakchgake' beṉ' malch aga ka nochlə beṉ' wlall c̱he'ka'?
Nia' le' bi nakan ka'. Shi le' bi yiyaj yilenile dii malka' chonle, ḻekzka' yog'le kwiayi'.
Shera beṉ' Jerusalénka' shiṉ'shoṉə, beṉ'ka' wit daa bdakwgake' yoo siba' daa zoa Siloéna', ¿achakile' napchgake' doḻ' aga ka beṉ' wlall c̱he'ka'?
Nia' le' bi nakan ka'. Na' shi le' bi yiyaj yilenile dii malka' chonle, ḻekzka' yog'le kwiayi'.
Na'ch bzoa Jesúza' to jempl, chi'e beṉ'ka': ―To beṉ' zoa to yag yix̱wew lo yell-lio c̱he'na' gana' naze' yag uvaka', na' wyaje' jawie' shi llian yix̱wewa', na' ka blline' ni tlish' bi llian.
Na'ch chi'e beena' chap yell-lio c̱he'na': “Ba gok shoṉ yiz chidwia' shi llian yix̱wewa', na' ni to bibi chbian. Bc̱hogchoklan, ḻa' nḻanchokzan yell-lioni.”
Na' beena' chape' yell-lio c̱he'na' chi'e: “X̱an', zi' zoashkin zi twiz na' wc̱heeṉ' xaninna' na' wlla'n ben'na'.
Shera shicholə wbian. Na' shi bi wlliakzan, na' wc̱hogo'n.”
Na' to lla sabd, llana' chombaaṉ beṉ' Israelka', chli' chsedi Jesúza' beṉ'ka' chdop chllag gana' choe'ḻwillgake' Chioza'.
Na' len to noolə ba gok shiṉ'shoṉ yiz nḻew dii x̱iwaa ḻe', na' bichkzə gok yizie' shḻi.
Na' ka ble'i Jesúza'ne' wṉie'ne' na' golle'ne': ―Noolə, ba bikwas yillwe' c̱ho'na'.
Na'ch bx̱oa neena' koll' noola' na' katena' lii bizetie' shḻicha, na' wzoloe' choe'lawee Chioza'.
Na' beena' chgoo xṉezi c̱heyi diika' chongake' gana' chdop chllaggake' bllee daa biyon Jesúza' noola' llana' chombaaṉgake', na'ch chi'e beṉ'ka' lle' na': ―De x̱op lla goncho llinna', na' bittezə llaka' yidle kwenc̱he yiyakile, na' bi gonle lez yiyakile' llani chombaaṉcho.
Na'ch che' X̱ancho Jesúza' ḻegake': ―Le' beṉ' wxiye', ¿abi wsell-le gooṉ c̱heleka' wa burr c̱heleka' lljaweejlegakb nisa' llani chombaaṉcho?
Nooli nake' xiiṉ dia c̱he dii Abrahama', na' ba gok shiṉ'shoṉ yiz Satanáza' daa chṉabia' dii x̱iw'ka' nonan ḻe' ka beṉ' nc̱heje'. ¿Ana' chakile bi nakan wen biyonee llani chombaaṉcho?
Na' ka goll Jesúza' ka', yog' beṉ'ka' chakzbangakile'ne' biyii bido'gakile', na' yog' beṉ'ka' sto bibagakile' daa ble'gakile' yeḻ' wakka' chone'.
Na'ch wna Jesúza': ―¿Nakra ka nak yeḻ' wṉabia' c̱he Chioza', lla? Na' ¿bera ka wsaklebida'n?
Zaklebin sa mostásana' daa goz to beṉ' lo yell-lio c̱he'na', na' ka bla'n na' bgolan gokan to yag xen na' ax̱t byiṉdo'ka' ben lillbka' lo xoziinna'.
Na' ḻekzka' chize' Jesúza': ―Dga sto wsaklebida'n yeḻ' wṉabia' c̱he Chioza'.
Zaklebin levadúrana' daa chc̱hix̱ to noolə shoṉa rob yezj kwenc̱he yisgolan kwa c̱he yetxtila'.
Shlak ziyaj Jesúza' Jerusalénna', bidie' yell yeḻka' na' yelldo'ka' na' bli' bsedile' beṉ'.
Na' bchej to beṉ' wṉabile'ne', chi'ene': ―Maestro, ¿ato c̱hopchga beṉ' yila bi kwiayi'gake'? Na'ch che' Jesúza'ne':
―Ḻi gon byen sho'le cho'a puert daa nak diido'zə kwenc̱he soalenle Chioza'. Ḻa' beṉ' zan gaklall'gake' sho'gake'n, na' bi gak sho'gake'.
Na' ka solla' x̱an yoona' wseje' puerta', na' le', igaaṉle cho'a puerta' wtankwle ḻe'inna' na' ye'lene': “Beṉ'do', bsaljgach kwenc̱he sho'nto'.” Na' x̱an yoona' iṉe' le': “Bi nombi'a le' ni bi ṉezid' ga beṉ' le'.”
Na'ch ye'lene': “Weej wdaolennto' li' txen, na' bli' bsedilo' neto' yell c̱hento'na'.”
Na'ch iṉe' le': “Bi nombi'a le', ni bi ṉezid' ga beṉ' le'. Ḻi lljayaak do na'lə yog'ḻoḻ-le le' beṉ' wen dii mal.”
Na' kwellchgale ax̱t gaox̱ax̱j ḻeylena' daa ḻe gakshejlall'le ka ile'ile dii Abrahama', dii Isaaca', dii Jacoba' na' yog' dii beṉ'ka' wdix̱jee daa goll Chioza' ḻegake' lle'gake' yabana' gana' chṉabia' Chioza', na' le', bi gok yiyoole.
Na' wde wdeli beṉ' lle' zbii zkaaṉ yell-lioni yillingake' yabana' gana' chṉabia' Chioza' na' kwe'gake' gaogake'.
Na' baḻ beṉ' bi nak beṉ' zakii ṉaa gakgake' beṉ' zakii, na' beṉ'ka' nak beṉ' zakii ṉaa bich gakgake' beṉ' zakii.
Na' lo llana'tezə bllin baḻ fariseoka' kwit Jesúza' na' che'gake'ne': ―Biyaj gan yoblə. Cheeni Heródeza' wite' li'.
Na' che' Jesúza' ḻegake': ―Ḻi yiyaj na' ḻi lljayell beṉ' wxiye'na': “Nin soa' to c̱hop shoṉ lla kwenc̱he yibej' dii x̱iw'ka' yoo beṉ' na' yiyon' beṉ' bi shao', na' sheelo diika' chon'.”
Chonan byen kooch' nez ṉaa, wx̱e len willj kwenc̱he yiyaa Jerusalénna' gana' chitgake' beṉ'ka' chyix̱jee daa che' Chioza', ḻa' agagaṉ' witgake' ḻegake' gan yoblə.
’¡Le' beṉ' Jerusalén, chitle beṉ'ka' chidtix̱jee daa che' Chioza' ḻegake', na' yaja' chitile beṉ'ka' chseḻee choe'gake' cho'a xtilleena'! Dii zan shii goklallaa yitop' le' ka chon jeda' chiyellb xiiṉdobka' xan x̱ilba', na' le' bi goonile'.
Ḻi koo yic̱hjle dga iṉia' le', Chioza' kwej yic̱hje' gani zoale. Na' nia' le', aga wle'chile nad' ax̱t kat'ch illin lla iṉale: “¡Gaklenshga X̱ancho Chioza' beeni ba bseḻee!”
To lla sabd, llana' chombaaṉ beṉ' Israelka', wyaj Jesúza' jtawe' lill to fariseo, beṉ' chṉabia', na' fariseoka' sto chinaḻ' chinogake'ne'.
Na' lawe'na' ze to beṉ' yo'e yi.
Na'ch Jesúza' wṉabile' fariseoka' na' beṉ'ka' chli' chsedi leya', chi'e ḻegake': ―¿Ade lsens yiyoncho to beṉ' bi shao' llani chombaaṉcho, anti bi den?
Na' ḻegake' bikzə bi gollgake'ne'. Na'ch Jesúza' bex̱ee beena' yoo yina' na' biyone'ne', na' golle'ne': ―Wak yiyajo'.
Na'ch chi'e fariseoka': ―Shi to burr c̱hele wa to gooṉ c̱hele ixopb to ḻoo yech to lla chombaaṉcho, ¿abi yibejleb katena' ḻa'kzi nakan llana' chombaaṉcho?
Na' bikz bi billel-lall'gake' ye'gake'ne'.
Na' ble'i Jesúza' ka chon beṉ'ka' wdaolene' lill farisewa', wche'gake' gana' chbe' beṉ'ka' zakii. Na'ch bseesee to jempl, chi'e ḻegake':
―Kat' no gax le' to ga chak wishagna', bi kwe'le gana' chbe' beṉ'ka' zakii. Ḻa' shera shi ila' beṉ' zak'chi ka le',
na' beena' goxe' le' iṉe': “Wzolla' kwenc̱he kwe' beeni gani chi'o.” Na'ch do chido'zile yizolla'le na' lljache'le xanteyin.
Na' bi gonle ka'. San kat' no gax le', chiyaḻ' lljc̱he'le xanteyin kwenc̱he kat' ila' beena' goxe' le' na' iṉe': “Bish'dawaa, nilə wda kwi'o gani zak'chi.” Na' ka' sho'le balaaṉ lao beṉ'ka' chi'lenle cho'a mesa'.
Ḻa' beena' chon kwine' beṉ' choo beṉ' xen, Chioza' gone'ne' beṉ' bibi zakii; na' beena' chakile' bibi zakee, Chioza' gone'ne' beṉ' choo beṉ' xen.
Na' ḻekzka' che' Jesúza' beena' goxe'ne' lille'na': ―Kat' cheenilo' wwawo' beṉ', bi gaxo' beṉ' zoalenzo' wen, no beṉ' bishoo, no beṉ' dialla c̱ho', ni no beṉ' wlill c̱ho', beṉ' nake' beṉ' wni'a, ḻa' ḻegake' ḻekzka' wak yigoogake' wzonna' yiwaogake' li' ka beno' c̱hegake'.
Aga kan' gono', san byi beṉ' yesh', beṉ' net ṉi'a nee, beṉ' bi chak sa' wen na' beṉ' lc̱hoḻ. Beṉ'kan' chiyaḻ' gaxo',
na'ch so' mbalaz. Ḻa' beṉ'kan' aga wak yigoogake' wzon c̱ho', san Chiozan' yigwee wzon c̱ho'na' llana' kat' yisbane' beṉ' wenka' ladj beṉ' wetka'.
Na' to beena' chi'lene' Jesúza' cho'a mesa', ka benile' wne' ka', na' chi'ene': ―¡Chakomba beṉ'ka' lljadaogake' gana' chṉabia' Chioza'!
Na'ch che' Jesúza'ne': ―Wzoa to beṉ' bene' to lṉi xen, na' goxe' beṉ' zan kwenc̱he shajgake' lille'na' lljtaogake'.
Na' ka goḻ' gaogake', bseḻee to wen llin c̱he'na' jelle' beṉ'ka' ba bye': “Ḻi dagach, ḻa' ba gok daa gaocho.”
Na' yog' beṉ'ka' jaṉie' wzologake' chc̱he'gake' dill'. Toe' golle'ne': “Zi' bizi'a lat' yell-lio na' chonan byen lljawia'n. Ye'gacho'ne' si'xene' bi gak yid'.”
Na' beena' sto chi'ene': “Zi' bizi'a gay' kwe' gooṉ na' chonan byen wwia' shi wak gaaṉgakb. Ye'gacho'ne' si'xene' bi gak yid'.”
Na' beena' sto chi'ene': “Zi' bshagna', na' bi gak yid'.”
Na'ch biza' wen llinna' jayelle' x̱ane'na' yog' daa goll beṉ'ka' ḻe'. Na'ch bllaa x̱ane'na' na' chi'e wen llin c̱he'na': “Ḻobe' jta lyell na' bc̱he' kon no beṉ' yillago', no beṉ' yesh', no beṉ' net ṉi'a nee, no beṉ' lc̱hoḻ, na' no beṉ' bi chak sa' wen.”
Na' ka jasane' beṉ'ka' jatope', na'ch chi'e x̱ane'na': “X̱an', ba ben' ka wno', na' ni dech latj sho' beṉ'.”
Na'ch che' x̱ane'na': “Wyaj do yawi nezka' na' ben byen yid beṉ'ka' yillago' kwenc̱he yilla' ḻoo lilla'ni.
Na' nia' le', ka nak beṉ'ka' bya' dii nech, ni toe' bi gaogake' daa ba bsini'a.”
Beṉ' zan zjanogake' Jesúza', na'ch biyec̱hje' chi'e ḻegake':
―Shi nole cheeni gakle nad' txen, chiyaḻ' gakchile nad' aga ka x̱axṉa'le, xool-le, xiiṉle, beṉ' bish'le, beṉ' zanle, na' ax̱t yeḻ' mban c̱helena'. Shi bi gakile' nad', aga wak gakle nad' txen.
Na' ḻekzka' beena' bi chzanile' yeḻ' mban c̱he'na', gak bittezə dii gak c̱he', kwenc̱he gone' daa chazlallaa, aga wak gake' nad' txen.
Shi nole cheenile gonle to yoo sib wal, zigaate chiyaḻ' wwiale ka'k' gaki na' shi waki xmechlena' sheeloin.
Ḻa' shi ba wlekwle leninna' na' tena' bich bi de wzeeloilen, na' yog' beṉ'ka' ile'gakile' bi biyollan wxillgakile' le'.
Na' iṉagake': “Kon wdishj beena' len yoona' na' bi goki xmeche'na' wzeeloe'n.”
Na' ka'kz to beṉ' wṉabia', shi cheenile' tiḻ-lene' sto wṉabia' yoblə, na' ḻekzka' chiyaḻ' wsakee shi wzoi shi mil beṉ'ka' nape' tiḻ-lengake' beena' nap gaḻja mil beṉ'.
Na' shi gakbe'ile' bi soi beṉ'ka' nape', na' zi' illinlə beṉ' wṉabia'na' sto, wseḻee to c̱hop beṉ' lljellgake'ne': “Bizə tiḻcho.”
Na' ka' le', shi bi c̱hooṉlall'le yog' dii de c̱hele, aga wakə gakle nad' txen.
’Zedaa nakan dii wen, na' shi bich zxi'n aga wakch yiyonchon zxi' dii yoblə kwenc̱he wc̱hinchon.
Ni bi gak wc̱hinchon lwaa ben', san c̱hooṉchon. Na' le' chenile dga nia', ḻi sen wṉeyi.
Yog' beṉ' wic̱hixjka' na' beṉ' saaxyaka' jabig'gake' kwit Jesúza' kwenc̱he bzenaggake' dillaa cho'e.
Na' fariseoka' na' beṉ'ka' chli' chsedi leya' wzologake' biz chon chnagake' c̱he Jesúza', che'gake': ―Chlebtezə beeni beṉ' saaxyaka' na' chaolenteze' ḻegake'.
Na'ch bzoa Jesúza' to jempl, golle' ḻegake':
―Shi tole naple to guiyoa xil' na' ṉit tob, na' wkwaaṉle baka' taplalj twaḻj lyix̱aa na' lljadiljle bana' wnit, na' ax̱t kon ka yillelb gonle.
Na' ka yillelb, yibaile yix̱oaleb yaaxizlena'.
Na' ka yillinle lill-lena' wtople beṉ'ka' nllaguile na' beṉ' wlill c̱heleka', na' ye'le ḻegake': “Ḻi yibaleni nad', ḻa' ba billel xil' c̱ha'na' bana' wnit.”
Na' nia' le', ka'kzan chibayi Chioza' len anjl c̱he'ka' yabana' kat' to beṉ' wen dii mal chiyajile' saaxya c̱he'na' aga ka taplalj twaḻj beṉ'ka' bi chonan byen yiyajgakile'.
’Wa shi to noolə de shi mech plat c̱he' na' ṉit ton, na' wxene' yi' c̱he'na' na' wḻoe' ḻoo lille'na' na' yiyilje'n ax̱t ki yillelile'n.
Na' ka yillelile'n na' wtope' noolka' nllaguile' na' beṉ' wlill c̱he'ka', na' yee ḻegake': “Ḻi yibaleni nad', ḻa' ba billel mech c̱ha'na' daa wnit.”
Na' nia' le', ka'kzan chibayi Chioza' len anjl c̱he'ka' kat' chiyaj chileni to beṉ' saaxya.
Na' ḻekzka' che' Jesúza' ḻegake': ―To beṉ' wzoa c̱hop xiiṉe',
na' bi' neshaa gollb' x̱abaa: “X̱a, bḻaa daa de c̱ho' na' beṉ nad' daa chiyaḻ' ikaa.” Na'ch bḻaa x̱abaa daa de c̱he' na' bi'en ḻegakb'.
Na' aga wlla, biyit' bide bi' neshaa daa bi'eb', na' mecha' daa bex̱'b' c̱heyin wyajlema'n to yell zit' na' jenditjba'n na' jem' kon daa nazan c̱heb'.
Na' ka biyoll benditj xmechbaa wche' to wbiṉ xen yella' gana' chdab', na'ch wzolo chdeb' wbinna'.
Na' wyajb' jaṉabb' llinna' gom' lao to beṉ' yella' gana' chdab', na' beena' bseḻeeb' lyix̱aa gana' nllee kushka' kwenc̱he jtapb' ḻegakb.
Na' daa ḻe chdom' goklall'b' gaob' daa chao kushka', na' ni ḻen bi be'gake'b'.
Na' gokib': “Beṉ' zan wen llin c̱he x̱a'na' lle' na' chichooṉzan dii cheej chaogake', na' nad', ba chetid' wbinni.
Ba ziyaachoklə kwit x̱a'na' na' yepee: X̱adawaa, ba bx̱iṉj' bḻen' lao Chioza' na' lawo'na'.
Bich chidoḻaa gak' xiiṉo', san beni nad' ka nottezə wen llin c̱ho'ki.”
Na'ch biza'b' ziyajb' lill x̱abaa. ’Na' zi dii xench yillim' lillbaa ble'i x̱abaa ḻeb' na' biyesh'lallile'b'. Na'ch zejdoe' jatiḻe'b' na' wdeḻe'b' na' bnope'b'.
Na'ch che'b' x̱abaa: “X̱adawaa, ba bx̱iṉj bḻen' lao Chioza' na' lawo'na', bich chidoḻaa gak' xiiṉo'.”
Na' x̱abaa chi'e wen llin c̱he'ka': “Ḻobe'zə ḻi lljḻej tgot lech' daa ḻiizelozi nakch na' ḻi wwakwba'n, na' ḻekzka' ḻi wllin to niy xbemaa na' ḻi wllin yel ṉi'abaa.
Na' ḻi lljx̱i' me'do'na' mbejchlawin, ḻi witb kwenc̱he gaochob na' goncho to lṉi,
ḻa' xiiṉdawaani gok c̱heb' ka bi' ba wit, na' ṉaa ba bila'b' mbam'. Gok c̱heb' ka bi' wnit, na' ṉaa ba billelb'.” Na'ch wzologake' bengake' lṉina'.
’Na' ka wzolo lṉina', xiiṉe' bi' necha' chdab' lyix̱aa. Na' ka billim' gaozə lillbaa, benib' chkwell wikwellka' na' chakte wiyaana'.
Na'ch wṉeb' to wen llinka' na' wṉabibee bin chak lillbaa.
Na' wen llinna' chi'e: “Bi' bishoonan' ba bila', na' ben x̱o'na' mandad betgake' me'do'na' mbejchlawin daa bila'b' shi'a shao'.”
Na' xiiṉe' bi' necha' bllaab' na' bi goonib' yiyoob'. Na'ch bchej x̱abaa got'yoile'b' kwenc̱he yiyoob'.
Na'ch che'b' x̱abaa: “Ṉezkzilo' ba gok zan yiz chon' yog' daa no', na' ni shlin biṉ' c̱hishj' cho'a xtilloona'. Na' bigaṉ' goṉo' nad' ḻa'c̱h' to shibdo' kwenc̱he wit'b yeej gaolem' bi'ka' nllaguid'.
Na' ṉaa bila' xiiṉo'ni biyit' bideb' yog' daa bi'ob' na' benditjb' xmecho'na' kon noolə wdaka', na' ba betzo' me'do'na', bana' ḻe nak, ni c̱heb'.”
Na'ch che' x̱abaa: “Xiiṉdawaa, li' zoaleno' nad' toshiizi, na' yog' bi de c̱ha' c̱hekzo' daa.
Per chonan byen ṉaa yibaicho na' goncho lṉini, ḻa' ba bila' bi' bishooni. Ba gok c̱heb' ka bi' ba wit, na' ṉaa ba bila'b' mbam'; gok c̱heb' ka bi' wnit, na' ṉaa ba billelb'.”
Na' ḻekzka' goll Jesúza' beṉ'ka' nakgake'ne' txen: ―Wzoa to beṉ' wni'a nape' to wen llin c̱he', na' bene' lo nee yog' dii de c̱he'. Na' wyaj baḻ beṉ' jellgake'ne': “Ḻe chonditj beena' daa beno' lo nee.”
Na'ch wṉe x̱ane'na' ḻe', chi'ene': “Ba benid' ka nagake' chono', na' chiyaḻ' yidio' kwent diika' ngoo lo no', ḻa' bich goṉ' xshino'na'.”
Na'ch chaki wen llinna': “¿Nakra gona'n ṉaa, bich goṉ x̱an'na' llinna' gon'? Bi soid' gon' llin wal, na' chido'id' yep' beṉ' yiyesh'gakile' nad' goṉgake' lat' wej xmech'.
Ba ṉezid' nak gon' kwenc̱he wleb beṉ' nad' lille'ka' kat' bich gat' llin c̱ha'na'.”
Na'ch goxe' to to beṉ'ka' chaḻ'gake' c̱he x̱ane'na', na' beṉ' necha' wṉabile'ne', chi'ene': “¿Ka'k' chaḻoo c̱he x̱an'na'?”
Na' beena' chi'e: “Chaḻaa to guiyoa medid set.” Na'ch chi'ene': “Ni de yisha', ḻobe'zə wche' na' bda'n shiyonzannan' chaḻoo.”
Na' ka wde, wṉabile' beena' sto, chi'ene': “¿Shera li'? ¿Ka'k' chaḻoo?” Na' beena' chi'ene': “Chaḻaa to guiyoa gush trigo.” Na'ch chi'ene': “Ni de yisha' na' bda'n taplaḻj gushzannan' chaḻoo.”
Na' x̱an wen llinna' be'lawee wen llin mal c̱he'na' daa biyiljlallee naklan gone'n. Ḻa' beṉ'ka' zech wṉeyi c̱he daa chak lo yell-lioni, chiyiljlall'chgake' nak soalen ljwellgake' wen kwenc̱he ile'shii ljwellgake', aga ka beṉ'ka' ba yoo beeni' c̱he Chioza' ḻoo yic̱hjlall'do'eka'.
’Na' nia' le', ḻi wc̱hin yeḻ' shawaa de c̱hele yell-lioni kwenc̱he gaklenle beṉ', na' kat' ba wde c̱he yeḻ' shawaa, Chioza' wlebe' le' soalenlene' zejḻi kaṉi.
’Na' beena' chon ka chiyaḻ' kon lat' daa nak lall' nee, ka'kzan gone' shi bichlə dii xench koo lall' nee. Na' beena' bi chon ka chiyaḻ' kon daa nak lall' nee, ka'kzə gone' shi bitekchlə dii xench koo lall' nee.
Shi bi chonle ka chiyaḻ' kon yeḻ' shawaa de yell-lioni, bi gonzle lez ikaale yeḻ' shawaa de yabana'.
Na' shi bi chonle ka chiyaḻ' kon yeḻ' shawaa nak lall' na'le yell-lioni, ¿nakra gon Chioza' goṉe' le' yeḻ' shawaa daa gaki c̱hele?
’Aga ga zoa to beṉ' wḻane' xshin c̱hop beṉ', ḻa' wakzbanile' beena' to, na' gakchile' beena' sto, wa gone' xshin beena' to do lallee na' xshin beena' sto gone'n nakzi. Aga wak gonle ka cheeni Chioza' shi ḻe chzelall'le yeḻ' wni'ana'.
Na' fariseoka' ḻe chzelall'gake' mecha', na' ka bengakile' dillaa choe' Jesúza', bxillgakile'ne'.
Na'ch che' Jesúza' ḻegake': ―Ḻa'kzi nale nakle beṉ' wen, Chioza' ṉezile' nakan nak yic̱hjlall'do'lena'. Ḻa' daa chaki beṉ' yell-lioni nakan dii llialote, ḻeyeṉ'lannan' chakzbani Chioza'.
Na' ḻekzka' che' Jesúza': ―Leya' na' daa bli' bsedi dii beṉ'ka' wdix̱jee daa goll Chioza' ḻegake', ḻegakannan' wṉabia'gakan ax̱t ka bllin lla bid Juanna'. Na' ka bid Juanna', wzolo chzenag beṉ' dill' wen dill' kob c̱he yeḻ' wṉabia' c̱he Chioza', na' chongake' to dii byen kwenc̱he iṉabi'e ḻoo yic̱hjlall'do'eka'.
’Dii ḻi nia' le', ḻobe'ch te c̱he yabana' len yell-lioni, aga ka daa tegonz shc̱ho'a daa na leya'.
’Shi to beṉ' byo yiḻee xoole'na' na' yikee noolə yoblə, chone' ka chon beena' zoate nool c̱he'na' na' chdalene' noolə yoblə. Na' beena' yikee noola' biḻaa beṉ' c̱he'na' ḻe', ḻekzka' chone' ka chon beena' zoalente nool c̱he'na' na' chdalene' noolə yoblə.
Na' chize' Jesúza' beṉ'ka': ―Wzoa to beṉ' wni'a na' chakwe' shgaḻ' lech' dii wen na' yog' lla chaoshawe'.
Na' ḻekzka' wzoa to beṉ' yesh' wlie' Lázaro, na' llia we'na' doxen kwerp c̱he'na'. Na' tlizi chjc̱hi'e cho'a yoo c̱he beṉ' wni'ana',
gokile' gawe' ḻa'c̱h' bḻaaka' chxop xan mes c̱he'na', na' ax̱t bekw'ka' chḻeegakb we'na' llie'.
Na' bllin lla wit beṉ' yeshaa, na' bic̱he' anjl c̱he Chioza'ne' kwenc̱he jazoalene' dii Abrahama'. Na' ḻekzka' wit beṉ' wni'ana' na' bkwash'gake'ne'.
Na' dii beṉ' wni'ana' chdezi'chgue' gana' lle' beṉ' wetka', na' bḻis jalawe'na' na' zit'lə ble'ile' dii Lázarona' chi'e kwit dii Abrahama'.
Na'ch wṉie' zilljə chi'e: “X̱adawaa Abraham, biyesh'gachi nad' na' bseḻ' Lázarona' kwenc̱he wḻeejlat' xbene'na' ḻoo nisa' na' yidshone'n lo ḻollaani, ḻa' ḻe chllaglochgan' lo yi'ni.”
Na' Abrahama' chi'ene': “Xiiṉ, jadini ka mbalaz gok c̱ho' shlak wbano' yell-liona', na' Lázaroni aga bi dii wen gok c̱he'. Na' ṉaa chizi'e banez ni, na' li' chzak'zi'o.
Na' ziznakan sto, ze to bdiṉj xen gchoḻi, na' aga wak te beṉ'ki yidgake' gana' lle'le, na' beṉ'ka' lle' na' aga wak tegake' yidgake' gani zoanto'.”
Na'ch che' beṉ' wnia'na'ne': “Chṉabid' li' shka', x̱adawaa Abraham, ben goklen bseḻ'gach Lázarona' lill x̱a'na'
gana' zoa zi gay' beṉ' bishaaka', llje'lene' ḻegake' dill' kwenc̱he bi lengake' yiyedgake' gani de yeḻ' zak'zi'ni.”
Na' Abrahama' chi'ene': “Napkzgake' daa bzej dii Moiséza' na' daa bzej dii beṉ'ka' wdix̱jee daa goll Chioza'. ¡Na' chiyaḻ' wzenaggake'n!”
Na' che' beṉ' wnia'na'ne': “Aga wakan, x̱adawaa Abraham, san sheḻ' to beṉ' ba wit yibane' na' yiyaje' lljaye'lene' ḻegake' dill', na' wiyaj wilengakile' saaxya c̱he'ka'.”
Na' che' Abrahama'ne': “Shi bi chzenaggake' daa bzej dii Moiséza' na' daa bzej dii beṉ'ka' wdix̱jee daa goll Chioza', ḻekzka' aga wyajḻe'gake' ḻa'kzi yiban to beṉ' wet.”
Na'ch che' Jesúza' beṉ'ka' nakgake'ne' txen: ―Bia'kzə de dii gon ka ixop beṉ' gone' dii mala', per ¡nyesh'laz gak c̱he beena' wchix̱e' beṉ' yoblə gone' dii mala'!
Wenlan sheḻ' wwaḻ'gake' yene'na' to yaj c̱he molin na' lljazaḻ'gake'ne' ḻoo nisdo'na' aga ka daa wchix̱e' to beṉ'ki chajḻe'gake' c̱ha'.
Daan, ḻi wsak'. ’Shi to bish' ljwell-le gone' mal c̱hele, ḻi wsheshlene', na' shi yiyajile' daa bene' c̱hele, ḻi yizi'xen c̱he'.
Ḻa'kzi ax̱t gall shii shlla gone' bi gone' c̱hele, na' gall shiite iṉe' le': “Chiyajid' daa ben' c̱ho'”, chiyaḻ' yizi'xenle c̱he'.
Na'ch goll postlka' X̱ancho Jesúza': ―Goklen neto' gonḻilall'chnto' Chioza'.
Na'ch che' X̱ancho Jesúza' ḻegake': ―Sheḻ' yeḻ' chajḻe' c̱helena' nakan ḻa'c̱h' ka nak sa mostásana', daa nak diido'zə, wak ye'le yag xen wala': “Blall'shki, na' jsoa ḻoo nisdo' na'lə”, na' gon yaga' daa ye'len, sheḻ'ka'.
’Shi nole zoa to wen llin c̱hele na' zizee lyix̱aa jawaaṉe' gooṉna' wa jtapeeb, aga we'lene': “Biyoo, na' wche' kwenc̱he gawo'.”
Aga we'lene' ka', san ye'l-lene': “Bsini'a daa gaw' xshe'na', na' wze wṉeyi kwenc̱he wdio' daa yeej gaw', na'techlə yeej gawo'.”
Na' ni bi we'lene' yeḻ' chox̱ken daa ba bene' daa che'lene' gone'.
Ḻekzka' le', kat' ba biyoll benle yog' daa non Chioza' mandad gonle, chiyaḻ' iṉale: “Neto' bi chizo chizakinto' gonnto' yog'ḻoḻten, shinchga bizointo' ba bennto' daa chonan byen gonnto'.”
Na' shlak zjada Jesúza' Jerusalénna', wdie' gana' ndiḻ yell-lioka' mbani Samáriana' na' Galileana'.
Na' ka blline' to cho'a yelldo', bllesh shi beṉ' chakgake' yillwe' daa le lepra kwenc̱he lljatiḻgake'ne', na' de zit'lə wzegake'
besyaagake' zilljə, che'gake'ne': ―¡Jesús, Maestro, biyesh'lall'gachi neto'!
Na' ka ble'i Jesúza' ḻegake', na' golle': ―Ḻi shaj lao bx̱ozka' kwenc̱he ile'gakile' le'. Na' shlak zejgake' bigaa yillwe' c̱he'ka'.
Na'ch toe' bibi'e ka gokbe'ile' ba biyakile', na'ch ax̱t chosya'ile' choe'lawee Chioza'.
Na' bc̱hek' xibe'na' lao Jesúza' na' bdose' lo yona' kwenc̱he bi'ene' yeḻ' chox̱ken. Na' beena' ben ka' nake' beṉ' Samaria.
Na'ch che' Jesúza': ―¿Aaga shigaken' biyaki? ¿Garaṉ beṉ'ka' zi ga?
¿Atochga beṉ' zitiin bibi'e choe'lawee Chioza'?
Na'ch che' Jesúza' beena': ―Bizolla' na' biyaj. Ba biyakilo' daa wyajḻi'o c̱ha'.
Na'ch wṉabi fariseoka' Jesúza' batran solo iṉabia' Chioza' lo yell-lioni. Na' chi'e ḻegake': ―Ka nak yeḻ' wṉabia' c̱he Chioza', aga nakan ka to dii ile'tekzicho.
Aga no iṉa: “Ni chṉabia' Chioza'”, wa “Na' chṉabi'e”, ḻa' ladjlenikzan ba bla' yeḻ' wṉabia' c̱he'na'.
Na'ch chi'e beṉ'ka' nakgake'ne' txen: ―Wllin lla kat' gaklall'le ḻa'c̱h' zi shlla ile'chile iṉabi'a, nad', Beṉ' Bseḻ' Chioza' Yell-lioni, na' aga wle'chile nad'.
Na' ichej beṉ' iṉe': “Ni zoe'”, wa “Na' zoe'.” Na' bi shajle, ni bi gonle beṉ'ka' txen.
Ḻa' ka chak kat' chep yes, chzeeni'n doxen xan yabana', ka'kzan gak llana' kat' zizaa, nad', Beṉ' Bseḻ' Chioza' Yell-lioni.
Na' chonan byen zigaate biya daa yen ile'id', na' beṉ'ki zoa ṉaa wzoagake' nad' ka'lə.
Kon ka gok kana' wzoa dii Noéna', ka'kzan gak kat' ba zoa illin lla yiyed' dii yoblə, nad', Beṉ' Bseḻ' Chioza' Yell-lioni.
Kana' wzoa dii Noéna', beṉ' yell-lioka' cheej chaogake', chshagna'gake', na' choe'gake' yeḻ' wishagna' c̱he xiiṉe'ka' bllinte llana' wyoo dii Noéna' ḻoo barkwa'. Na' wzolo chak yejsiwaa yell-lioni ax̱t billa'cha lawinna' nisa', na' blliayi'n yog'ḻoḻe'.
Na' ḻekzka' wizak kana' wzoa dii Lota'. Cheej chaogake', chiya'o chidegake' bi de c̱hegake', na' chaz chaaṉgake', na' chon lillgake'.
Per ka bchej dii Lota' yell Sodómana', Chioza' bḻetje' yi'na' xan yabana' nc̱hix̱an daa ne' azufre na' betan yog' beṉ' yell Sodómaka'.
Na' ka'kzan gak llana' kat' yiyed', nad', Beṉ' Bseḻ' Chioza' Yell-lioni.
’Llana' zizaa, shi to beṉ' llie' yic̱hj lille'na' na' xshinḻaze'na' den ḻoo yoo c̱he'na', bi yiyetjze' kwenc̱he lljaleje'n. Na' shi to beṉ' zeje' lyix̱aa, bi yiyajze' lille'na'.
Ḻi lljadini ka gok c̱he dii xool Lota'.
Beena' bi chsanlall' yeḻ' mban c̱he'na', beenan' kwiayi'; san beena' chsanlall' yeḻ' mban c̱he'na', beenan' gat' to yeḻ' mban c̱he' zejḻi kaṉi.
’Na' nia' le', lle'na' kat' zizaa, c̱hop beṉ' die' toz blag, toe' yic̱hi'a na' stoe' yigaaṉ.
Na' gana' lle' c̱hop noolə chotgake', toe' yic̱hi'a na' stoe' yigaaṉ.
Na' c̱hop beṉ' byo chongake' llin lyix̱aa, toe' yic̱hi'a na' beena' sto yigaaṉe'.
Na'ch wṉabgakile'ne': ―¿Garan gak dga, X̱an'? Na' chi'e ḻegake': ―Gana' de ba weta', nan' chdop chllag llodka'.
Na' bzoa Jesúza' to jempl kwenc̱he bli' bsedile' ḻegake' bi lljshyagakile' we'ḻwillgake' Chioza'.
Chi'e ḻegake': ―Wzoa to beṉ' wen yeḻ' josc̱his to yell, na' bi chall chllebe' Chioza', ni bibi chakile' shi bi chiyoolallii beṉ' ka chone'.
Na' yella' wzoa to noolə wizeb na' chajtezi chaje' lawe'na', chi'ene': “Bensha yeḻ' josc̱his c̱ha'ni.”
Na' ssha ba gok chaje' lawe'na' na' bikzə chone' bin chi'ene', na' bllin lla kat' chakile': “Ḻa'kzi bi chall chlleb' Chioza' na' ni bibi chakid' shi bi chiyoolallii beṉ' ka chon',
gonch' yeḻ' josc̱his c̱he nooli kwenc̱he bich yidyembeguile' nad'.”
Na' X̱ancho Jesúza' chi'e ḻegake': ―Ḻi wzenag ka ben beṉ' wen yeḻ' josc̱hisa', beena' bi chall chlleb Chioza'.
¿Achakile Chioza' bi gaklene' beṉ'ka' ba wleje' nakgake' lall' nee, beṉ'ka' choe'ḻwillgake'ne' ka waḻ ka tella? ¿Awllaile' gaklene' ḻegake'?
Bi nakan ka', san nia' le' katena' gaklene' ḻegake'. Per kat' zizaa, nad', Beṉ' Bseḻ' Chioza' Yell-lioni, ¿alle'ch beṉ' nonḻilall' nad' yell-lioni, lla?
Na' bzoa Jesúza' sto jempl c̱he beṉ'ka' chakgakile' nakgake' beṉ' wen lao Chioza' na' chongakile' beṉ' yoblə nakzi. Na' wne':
―C̱hop beṉ' wyajgake' yoodo'na' kwenc̱he je'ḻwillgake' Chioza'. Toe' nake' fariseo na' beena' sto nake' beṉ' wic̱hixj.
Na' farisewa' zie' chshalj chshon c̱he kwine', chi'e: “Chios c̱ha', chox̱keno' bi chon' ka chon beṉ' yoblə, bi chzi' chban', bi nak' beṉ' wen dii mal, agagaṉ' kwej yic̱hj' nool c̱ha'na' kwenc̱he soalen' nool yoblə, na' ni bi chon' ka chon beṉ' wic̱hixji.
C̱hop shii to xman chzoa' wbas', na' lawi yog' daa chon' gan chbej' daa chidoḻoo ikoo.”
Na' beṉ' wic̱hixja', zit'lə wzie' na' ni bi biyaxjile' wḻis lawe'na' wwie' yabana', san chballee cho'a lc̱ho'ena' chi'e: “¡Chios c̱ha', biyesh'gachi nad' daa nak' beṉ' saaxya!”
Na' nia' le', Chioza' bzenague' c̱he beṉ' wic̱hixja' na' bizee biyaje' lille'na' ba biyakxen saaxya c̱he'na'. San bi bzenague' c̱he farisewa'. Ḻa' beena' chon kwine' beṉ' choo beṉ' xen, Chioza' gone'ne' beṉ' bibi zakii. Na' beena' chakile' bibi zakee, Chioza' gone'ne' beṉ' choo beṉ' xen.
Na' ḻekzka' beṉ' zan jwa' bi'do' c̱he'ka' lao Jesúza' kwenc̱he bx̱oa neena' yic̱hjb'ka' na' wṉabile' Chioza' gaklene'gakb'. Na' ka ble'i beṉ'ka' nakgake'ne' txen, bsheshlengake' ḻegake'.
Na' Jesúza' goxe' bi'do'ka', na' chi'e beṉ'ka' nakgake'ne' txen: ―Ḻi we' latj yid bi'do'ki lawa'ni, bi wllonle, ḻa' Chioza' chṉabi'e ḻoo yic̱hjlall'do' beṉ'ka' nak ka ḻegakb'.
Dii ḻi nia' le', beena' bi yiyak yic̱hjlall'do'ena' ka c̱he bi'do'ki kwenc̱he iṉabia' Chioza' ḻe', bi yilline' gana' zoa Chioza'.
To beṉ' zakii wṉabile' Jesúza', chi'ene': ―Maestro, li' nako' beṉ' wen. Wna nad' beran chiyaḻ' gon' kwenc̱he gat' to yeḻ' mban c̱ha' zejḻi kaṉi.
Na'ch che' Jesúza'ne': ―¿Berac̱he nazo' nad' beṉ' wen? Toz Chioza' nake' beṉ' wen.
Ba ṉezkzilo' daa nllia Chioza' bia' goncho: “Bi soaleno' nool bi nak nool c̱ho', bi wito' beṉ', bi kwano', bi c̱hiljlalloo bizə gon iṉo' c̱he beṉ', na' wdap balaaṉ x̱axṉoo.”
Na'ch che' beena'ne': ― Kana' naktia' bi' xkwid' chon' yog' diika'.
Na'ch ka beni Jesúza' ka goll beena'ne', na' chi'ene': ―Stozə daa chyallj gono': jayet' jade yog' daa de c̱ho' na' be'n beṉ' yesh'ka'. Na' shi gono' ka', na' gat' to yeḻ' shao' c̱ho' yabana'. Na' da, dino' nad'.
Na' ka beni beena' ka goll Jesúza'ne', ḻe gokyeshile', ḻa' beṉ' wni'a nlleban'.
Na' ka ble'i Jesúza' ḻe gokyeshile', na' chi'e: ―¡Lallj inlleb chonan c̱he beṉ' wni'aka' we'gake' latj iṉabia' Chioza' ḻegake'!
Ḻobe'ch te to kamey xan yeshaa aga ka to beṉ' wni'a yiyo'e yabana'.
Na' beṉ'ka' beni, gollgake'ne': ―¿Noran yila shka'?
Na'ch che' Jesúza' ḻegake': ―Daa bi chak gon beṉec̱ha', Chioza' chak gone'n.
Na'ch che' Pédrona' Jesúza': ―X̱an', ba wlej yic̱hjnto' yog' dii de c̱hento' kwenc̱he naknto' li' txen.
Na'ch che' Jesúza' ḻegake': ―Dii ḻi nia' le', nottezə beṉ' ba bzanile' no lille', no x̱axṉee, no beṉ' bishee, no beṉ' zane', no xiiṉ xoole' kwenc̱he cho'e latj chṉabia' Chioza'ne',
Chioza'kzə wi'e dii zak'chi c̱he' yell-lioni aga ka diika' wlej yic̱hje', na' ka yilline' yabana' wi'ene' to yeḻ' mban zejḻi kaṉi.
Na'ch wlej Jesúza' beṉ'ka' shlliṉ ka'lə, beṉ'ka' nakgake'ne' txen, chi'e ḻegake': ―Dga ziyajcho Jerusalénna' ṉaa, yillinin daa bzej dii beṉ'ka' wdix̱jee daa goll Chioza' kani'yi daa gak c̱ha', nad', Beṉ' Bseḻ' Chioza' Yell-lioni.
Ḻa' gongake' nad' lo na' beṉ'ka' bi nombia' Chioza', na' gonḻegake' c̱ha', biya dii iṉagake' nad', na' wlla' x̱eneeka' nad'.
Na' wit c̱hingake' nad' na'tech witgake' nad', na' yiyoṉ lla yiban' ladj beṉ' wetka'.
Na' beṉ'ka' nakgake'ne' txen ni lat' bi wyajni'gakile' daa golle' ḻegake', na' ni bi wṉezgakile' berac̱he chi'e ḻegake' ka', ḻa' daa golle' ḻegake' nakan dii bi gak shajni'gakile'.
Na' ka ba chllin Jesúza' yell Jericóna', na' chi' to beṉ' lc̱hoḻ cho'a neza' chṉabile' beṉ' yiyesh'lall'gakile'ne' we'gake' lat' wej xmeche'.
Na' ka benile' chde beṉ' zan na'ch wṉabe' bin chak.
Na' gollgake'ne': ―Jesús, beṉ' Nazaretan', chda ni.
Na'ch besyee, chi'e: ―¡Jesús, Xiiṉ dia c̱he dii Daví, biyesh'lall'gachi nad'!
Na' beṉ'ka' llialo lao Jesúza' chsheshlengake'ne' kwenc̱he kwi'e llizə, na' zizikchlə chosyee, chi'e: ―¡Xiiṉ dia c̱he dii Daví, biyesh'lall'gachi nad'!
Na'ch wlez Jesúza' na' bene' mandad lljx̱i'gake'ne'. Na' ka bllin beṉ' lc̱hoḻa' lawe'na' na'ch wṉabile'ne':
―¿Beran cheenilo' gon' c̱ho'? Na'ch che' beṉ' lc̱hoḻa'ne': ―X̱an', cheenid' ile'id'.
Na'ch che' Jesúza'ne': ―Daa ba chonḻilalloo nad' na' ile'ilo'.
Na' katena' lii bile'teile', na'ch janoe' Jesúza' choe'lawee Chioza'. Na' yog' beṉ'ka' ble'i daa ben Jesúza' be'la'ogake' Chioza'.
Na'ch bllin Jesúza' yell Jericóna' na' wdie' gchoḻ yella'.
Na' yella' zoa to beṉ' wni'a lie' Zaqueo, na' ngoo lall' nee x̱oṉj wic̱hixjka'.
Na' goklallee ile'ile' Jesúza', per bi gok ile'ile'ne' daa nake' beṉ' bc̱hekwdo' na' daa zejlen Jesúza' beṉ' zan.
Na'ch wllialodoe' lawe'ka' na' wyepe' to lo yag xen kwenc̱he ile'ile'ne' ka tie'.
Na' ka bllin Jesúza' xan yaga', na' bḻis lawe'na' chi'ene': ―Zaqueo, btalalloo biyetj, ḻa' lillo'nan' yigaaṉa' ṉaa.
Na'ch biyetjdo Zaquewa' chibaile' bic̱hi'e Jesúza' lille'na'.
Na' ka ble'i beṉ'ka' lle' na' ka gok, yog'ze' wzolo biz chon chnagake' c̱he', che'gake': ―Yigaaṉxgale' lill beṉ' saaxyani, na.
Na'ch wzolla Zaquewa' na' chi'e X̱ancho Jesúza': ―X̱an', cheenid' wi'a gashjə daa de c̱ha' beṉ' yesh'ka', na' yog' beṉ'ka' ba bc̱hixj' dii xench, yiyoe'gakee taplə ka daa ba wlan' c̱hegake'.
Na'ch che' Jesúza'ne': ―Ṉaanlla ba bisla Chioza' beṉ'ki zoa ḻoo yooni kwenc̱he bi kwiayi'gake', daa len Zaquewi nake' xiiṉ dia c̱he dii Abrahama'.
Ḻa' ka nak' nad', Beṉ' Bseḻ' Chioza' Yell-lioni, bid' kwenc̱he yiyilj' na' yisla' beṉ'ka' yoo nez daa wlliayi'n ḻegake'.
Shlak chzenag beṉ'ka' daa che' Jesúza', bseesile' ḻegake' to jempl, daa ba zoa illine' Jerusalénna' na' ḻegake' gokgakile' daa nake' beṉ' bseḻ' Chioza' lii solotie' iṉabi'e.
Na'ch chi'e ḻegake': ―To beṉ' zakii bcheje' wyaje' to yell zit' wal kwenc̱he lljaḻane' yeḻ' wṉabia' c̱he lalle'na', na' ka yilline' iṉabi'e.
Na' ka zi' see, wṉie' shi wen llin c̱he'ka' na' bi'e ḻegake' twej mech dii zak' dii xen na' chi'e ḻegake': “Ni de mechi, ḻi gonlenan delgens shlak bi soa'.”
Na' beṉ' wlall c̱he'ka' ḻe chakzbangakile'ne', na' ka wde wzee bseḻ'gake' x̱oṉj beṉ' wyajgake' lao beena' we' lsens iṉabi'e kwenc̱he jellgake'ne': “Bi cheeninto' iṉabia' beeni neto'.”
Per bia'kzə gok lo nee iṉabi'e, na' biyaje' lalle'na'. Na' ka billine' goxe' beṉ'ka' bkwaaṉlene' mecha' kwenc̱he iṉezile' ka'k' wej ben mecha' gan daa bkwaaṉlene' to toe'.
Na' ka bllin beṉ' necha' lawe'na' na' chi'ene': “X̱an', xmecho'na' bkwaaṉ'leno' nad' bena'n gan shin.”
Na'ch beṉ' wṉabia'na' chi'ene': “Wenkzan beno'. Daa beno' ka chiyaḻ' kon lat' mecha' bkwaaṉlen' li', wzoa' li' iṉabi'o shi yell.”
Na' ka bllin beena' sto lawe'na' na' chi'ene': “X̱an', xmecho'na' bkwaaṉ'leno' nad' bena'n gan gayaan.”
Na' ḻekzka' chi'e beena': “Wzoa' li' iṉabi'o gay' yell.”
Na'ch bllin stoe' lawe'na' na' chi'ene': “X̱an', ni de xmecho'na' bkwaaṉ'leno' nad'. Blall'tipteza'n to lech' na' wlooshawaan
daa blleb' li', ḻa' ḻe beṉ' zṉia nako'. Chkaatezo' dii bi naki c̱ho', na' chizi' chilaptezo' dii goz gooṉ beṉ' yoblə.”
Na'ch che' beṉ' wṉabia'na' ḻe': “Bikzbi yejni'alallii beno'. Kon ka ba wno' ka'kzan gak c̱ho'. Ṉezilo' nak' beṉ' zṉia, na' chkaatez' dii bi naki c̱ha' na' chizi' chilap' dii goz gooṉ beṉ' yoblə.
Na' daa ṉezilo' ka' chon', ¿berac̱he ki bi'o xmechaa gon yic̱hjin kwenc̱he yikaan ṉaa ba biyed'?”
Na'ch chi'e beṉ'ka' lle' na': “Ḻi yikaa mecha' daa bi'ane' na' ḻi we'n beena' bene' gan shin.”
Na'ch che' beṉ'ka'ne': “X̱an', ba napkzə beena' shin.”
Na' che' beṉ' wṉabia'na' ḻegake': “Nia' le', beena' chonlene' llin daa yoo lo nee, wakch lall' nee dii xench; san beena' bi chonlene' llin daa yoo lo nee, ax̱t daa ngoo lo nee lat' yidoyo.
Na' ka nak beṉ'ka' chakzbangakile' nad', beṉ'ka' bi cheengakile' iṉabi'a, ḻi lljx̱i'gake' ni na' ḻi witgake' ile'teid'.”
Na' ka wde wna Jesúza' ka', na'ch bigoolene' nez beṉ'ka' nakgake'ne' txen ziyajgake' Jerusalénna'.
Na' ka billingake' xṉi'a yaa daa le Yaa Olivos, gaozə yellka' le Betfagé na' Betania, na'ch bseḻee c̱hop beṉ'ka' nakgake'ne' txen,
na' chi'e ḻegake': ―Ḻi shaj yella' llia na', na' ka illinle ile'ile to burr chbando', ba konoṉ' kwia, da'b yag. Na' wsell-leb wc̱he'leb nilə.
Na' shi no iṉaz le': “¿Berac̱he chsellzleb?”, na' ye'lene': “X̱anchonan' chyalljile'b.”
Na'ch wyaj beṉ'ka' bseḻee, na' ka bllingake' ble'gakile' to burr chbando' da'b yag, kon kayeṉ' goll Jesúza' ḻegake'.
Na' ka chsellgake' burra' na'ch che' x̱ama' ḻegake': ―¿Berac̱he chsell-leb?
Na'ch che'gake'ne': ―X̱anchonan' chyalljile'b.
Na'ch bc̱he'gake'b jwa'gake'b lao Jesúza' na' bx̱oagake' xe'ka' koll'ba' na' blliagake' Jesúza' koll'ba'.
Na' shlak zej Jesúza' llie' burra', chshilj xa beṉ'ka' tlo neza'.
Na' ka ba chillingake' gaozə gana' chiyetj nez daa ziza' Yaa Olívoza', yog'ḻoḻ beṉ'ka' nakgake'ne' txen chosyaagake' daa chibagakile' na' choe'la'ogake' Chioza' daa ble'gakile' yog' yeḻ' wakka' bene'.
Na'ch nagake': ―¡Gaklenshga X̱ancho Chioza' beeni ba bseḻee iṉabi'e! ¡Ḻi da, we'la'ocho Chioza' zoa yabana' daa bene' ka zoalenchone' mbalaz!
Na' baḻ fariseoka' len ladj beṉ'ka' no Jesúza', che'gake'ne': ―Maestro, goll beṉ'ki nakgake' li' txen soagake' llizə.
Na' che' Jesúza' ḻegake': ―Nia' le', shi beṉ'ki soagake' llizə, na' yaj kilə solo gosyaagakan we'la'ogakan nad'.
Na' ka billine' gaozə yell Jerusalénna', gokyeshile' ka ble'ile'n na' wchelle' c̱he beṉ'ka' zoa na'.
Na' chi'e: ―¡Sheḻ'ka' ṉaanlla gakbe'ile nakan gonle kwenc̱he soale mbalaz! Per ngashaan laolena' na' aga wakbe'kzile.
Wllin lla ila' beṉ'ka' chakzbangakile' le' na' wzec̱hjgake' yelli leej na' kono gak sho' ichej.
Na' ni sto yaj c̱he lill-leka' bich yikwaaṉgake' koll' ljwellin, na' witgake' le' len xiiṉleka', ḻa' bi gokbe'ile ka bla' Chioza' ladjleni.
Na'ch ka bllin Jesúza' cho'a yoodo'na' na' bisheshe' beṉ'ka' chit' chde.
Na' chi'e ḻegake': ―Cho'a Xtill' Chioza' nan: “Lilla'na' nakan ga choe'ḻwill beṉ' nad'”, na' le' ṉaa ba nonzlen ka to ga chdop chllag wban.
Na' yog' lla bli' bsedi Jesúza' beṉ' gana' zoa yoodo'na', na' bx̱ozka' chṉabia' na' beṉ'ka' chli' chsedi leya' na' nochlə beṉ' wṉabia' c̱he beṉ' Israelka' ḻa'kzi biyiljlall'gake' naklə gongake' kwenc̱he witgake'ne'
bikzə bi gok gongake', ḻa' yog'zə beṉ' chibagakile' chzenaggake' dill'ka' cho'e.
Na' bllin to lla, shlak chli' chsedi Jesúza' beṉ'ka' lesh' chyoodo'na' na' chyix̱je'ile' ḻegake' dill' wen dill' kob c̱he Chioza', bllin bx̱ozka' chṉabia' na' beṉ'ka' chli' chsedi leya' len beṉ' golka' chṉabia'.
Na' che'gake'ne': ―Wnashki neto', ¿bi yeḻ' wṉabia' napo' chono' diiki? Na' ¿nora beṉ li' yeḻ' wṉabia'ni?
Na'ch che' Jesúza' ḻegake': ―Ḻekzka' nad' de to dii iṉabid' le', ḻi iṉashki nad':
¿Noran bseḻ' Juanna' kwenc̱he bidchoe' beṉ' nisa'? ¿AChiozan' bseḻeene'? ¿Anti beṉ' yell-liona'zan bseḻeene', lla?
Na'ch wzologake' choe'len ljwellgake' dill', che'gake': ―¿Nakra ka ye'chone', lla? Shi ye'chone' Chioza' bseḻeene', ḻobe' iṉe' cho': “¿Berac̱he ki wyajḻe'le c̱he', shka'?”
Na' shi yize'chone' nozə beṉ' bseḻeene', yog' beṉ'ki wlliagake' cho' yaj witgake' cho', ḻa' yog'gake' chajḻe'gake' Juanna' bi'e dill' daa goll Chioza'ne'.
Na'ch gollgake' Jesúza': ―Bi ṉezinto' no bseḻ' beena'.
Na'ch che' Jesúza' ḻegake': ―Ḻekzka' nad' aga wnia' le' noran beṉ nad' yeḻ' wṉabia'na' kwenc̱he chon' diiki.
Na' Jesúza' bseesee to jempl lao beṉ'ka' lle' na': ―To beṉ' billee yag uva, na' bene'n lall' na' beṉ'ka' gap wwian, na' wzee wyaje' ssha gan yoblə.
Na' ka bizi' bilap beṉ'ka' uvana', x̱aninna' bseḻee to wen llin c̱he' kwenc̱he lljelle' beṉ'ka' nak lall' na'gake' yag uvaka' we'gake'ne' daa chidoḻee yikee. Na' beṉ'ka' chapgake' yag uvaka' bex̱'gake'ne' bet wdingake'ne', na'tech bilaggake'ne' to ka' che'.
Na'ch bseḻee sto wen llin c̱he'na'. Na' ḻekzka' bet wdingake'ne', na' biya dii bengakile'ne', na' bizlaggake'ne' to ka' che'.
Na'ch de wyoṉ shii, bizseḻee wen llin yoblə, na' ḻekzka' bengake'ne' bido we'zi, na' bizlaggake'ne'.
’Na'ch chaki x̱an yag uvaka': “¿Nakra ka gona'n? Wseḻ'shkid' bi' c̱ha'ni, bi'ni ḻe chakid'. Shera shicholə wzenaggake' c̱heb'.”
Na' ka ble'i beṉ'ka' chap yag uvaka' xiiṉe'na', na'ch che' ljwelle': “Bi'nin yigaaṉlem' yell-lioni. Ḻi da witchob' kwenc̱he yigaaṉlenchon.”
Na' wlejgake'b' gana' lle' yag uvaka' na' betgake'b'. Na'ch wṉabi Jesúza' beṉ'ka' chzenag: ―¿Nakra ka chakile goni x̱an yag uvaka' beṉ'ka', lla?
Ba nakten shaje' na' lljete' beṉ'ka' chap yag uva c̱he'na' na' yiyone' yell-lio c̱he'na' lall' na' beṉ' yoblə. Na' ka beni beṉ'ka' wne' ka', na' wnagake': ―¡Bat we' Chioza' latj gak ka'!
Na' bwia Jesúza' ḻegake', chi'e: ―¿Beran zejin Cho'a Xtill' Chioza' gana' na: Yaja' daa bi wyoolall' wen yooka', ḻeyeṉ'lannan' yaja' daa ba nc̱hejcha yoona'?
Nottezə beṉ' lljc̱haze' lawinna' kwiayee, na' shi idakwan beṉ', ax̱t wshoshjan ḻe'.
Na' bx̱ozka' chṉabia' na' beṉ'ka' chli' chsedi leya' goklall'gake' gox̱'gake' Jesúza' ka biyoll golle' ka', ḻa' gokbe'gakile' c̱hezgaken' wṉie' daa bi chajḻe'gake' c̱he'. Per bllebgake' beṉ'ka' ndop nllag na'.
Na'ch bseḻ'gake' to c̱hop beṉ' wiwia wiyi, na' bentezgake' ka beṉ' cheenchgayi wzenag c̱he'. Per aga do lall'gaken' wyajgake', san kwenc̱hezə kwejyelgakile' Jesúzan' na' lljadaogake' xya c̱he' lao beena' chṉabia' gana' mbani Judeana'.
Na' wṉabgakile'ne': ―Maestro, ṉezinto' daa no' na' daa chli'o nakan dii ḻi, na' aga chwio' nak nak beṉ', shi nake' beṉ' zakii wa shi bi nake'. Ṉezinto' chli'o nez ḻi c̱he Chioza' kon ka nakan.
Wnashki neto': ¿Achiyaḻ' c̱hixjcho daa chṉab Césara', beena' chṉabia', anti bi chiyaḻ' c̱hixjchon?
Na' gokbe'i Jesúza' aga do lall'gaken' wṉabgakile'ne', na'ch chi'e:
―Ḻi wli'shkayi nad' to mech. ¿Nora cho'alawin na' no leyin da'n? Na' che'gake'ne': ―C̱he Césaran', beena' chṉabia' Rómana'.
Na'ch chi'e: ―Na'len, ḻi we' Césara' daa naki c̱he', na' ḻekzka' ḻi we' Chioza' daa naki c̱he'.
Na' ni shcho'a dill' daa bi'e lao beṉ'ka' bi gok wc̱hingake'n kwenc̱he gaogake' xya c̱he'. Na' bibangakile' ka golle' ḻegake' na' bibe'gake' llizə.
Ka wde dga, bllin baḻ saduceoka' lao Jesúza', beṉ'ka' bi chajḻe' daa yiban beṉ' wetka'. Na'ch che'gake' Jesúza':
―Maestro, leya' bzej dii Moiséza' nan: shi to beṉ' byo guete' na' igaaṉ xoole'na' wizeb na' kono xiiṉgake' wzoa, beṉ' bish' beṉ' weta' chiyaḻ' yikee nool wizeba' kwenc̱he soa xiiṉ dia c̱he dii beṉ' bisheena'.
Ki gok to shii, wzoa gall bish' beṉ', na' beṉ' necha' bshagnee, na' wite' na' kono xiiṉe' wzoa.
Na' beṉ' wchopina' bikee noola', na' ḻekzka' wite' na' kono xiiṉe' wzoa.
Na' beṉ' wyoṉina', ḻekzka' bizkee noola', na' wizete' na' kono xiiṉe' wzoa. Na' ḻekzka' beṉ'ka' zi tap bizkaagake' noola' na' witgake', na' ni to beṉ'ka' gall bi wzoa xiiṉgake' kon noola'.
Na' ka bllin lla ḻekzka' wit noola'.
Na' kat' yiban beṉ' wetka', ¿norayeṉ'en' gak beṉ' c̱he', lla?, ḻa' galltien' wzoalene'.
Na'ch che' Jesúza' ḻegake': ―Beṉ'ka' lle' yell-lioni ṉaa chkaa ljwellgake', na' ḻekzka' choe' yeḻ' wishagna' c̱he xiiṉe'ka'.
San beṉ'ka' iṉa Chioza' zak'gake' yiyajgake' gana' zoe' ka yibangake' ladj beṉ' wetka', aga ka'chan gongake'. Ḻa' koch no wshagna' gana' zoa Chioza',
ni koch no guet, san soagake' ka zoa anjlka'. Na' gakgake' xiiṉ Chios daa ba bisbane' ḻegake' ladj beṉ' wetka'.
Kwin dii Moiséza' bzeje' kwenc̱he iṉezicho yiban beṉ' wetka' kana' bzeje' c̱he yag yeshaa daa ble'ile' chaḻ'ṉiṉ. Na' wne' X̱ancho Chioza' nake' Chios c̱he Abrahama', Isaaca' na' Jacoba'.
Na' Chioza' aga nake' Chios c̱he beṉ' wet, san nake' Chios c̱he beṉ' de yeḻ' mban c̱heyin. Ḻa' yog'ḻoḻ beṉ' nx̱enilallii Chioza', dekzə yeḻ' mban c̱hegake'.
Na'ch baḻ beṉ'ka' chli' chsedi leya' gollgake'ne': ―Maestro, ka ba wnayeṉoon nakan.
Na' bich bi biyaxjchgakile' iṉabchgakile'ne'.
Na' che' Jesúza' ḻegake': ―¿Berac̱he nazə beṉ' Crístona' nake' xiiṉ dia c̱he dii Davina'?,
len kwin dii Davinan' bzeje' ḻee libr c̱he Sálmoka' gana' na: X̱ancho Chioza' golle' X̱an'na': “Wche' kwit' de shḻi ni
shlak wzoa' xṉi'ona' beṉ'ka' chakzbani li'.”
¿Berac̱he chakzile Crístona' nake' xiiṉ dia c̱he dii Davina', len kwin Davina' golle'ne': “X̱an'”?
Na' shlak chzenag yog' beṉ'ka' lle' na', Jesúza' golle' beṉ'ka' nakgake'ne' txen:
―Ḻi wsak' bi gonle ka chon beṉ'ki chli' chsedi leya'. Ḻe chibagakile' gon xe'ka' dii toṉ, na' cheengakile' yog'zə beṉ' gapgake' ḻegake' balaaṉ ladj lkwe' beṉ'. Na' gana' chdop chllagcho choe'ḻwillcho Chioza' chbagakile' kwe'gake' gana' chbe' beṉ'ka' zakii, na' ka'kzə chongake' ga de yeḻ' waw.
Na' ḻekzka' chkaatezgake' lill nool wizebka', na' chongake' ka chshaljlen Chioza' ssha nlleb kwenc̱he gaki beṉ' ḻe wen chongake'. Na' daa chongake' ka', ba nakten ile'gakile' yeḻ' zak'zi' wala'.
Na' ble'i Jesúza' ka chgoo beṉ' wni'aka' mecha' gana' chgoo beṉ' mech c̱he yoodo'na'.
Na' ḻekzka' ble'ile' to nool yesh', beṉ' wizeb, wlo'e c̱hop sintabdo'.
Na' goll Jesúza' ḻegake': ―Dii ḻi nia' le', ḻa'kzi nool wizebi nake' beṉ' yesh', ba be'che' dii xench aga ka yog'te beṉ'ka'.
Ḻa' yog'gake' choe'gake' daa chichooṉan c̱he'ka', na' ḻe', naktie' beṉ' yesh', wlo'e doxen daa nape', ḻa'kzi chyalljile'n.
Na' baḻ beṉ'ka' choe'gake' xtill' yoodo'na' ka xochi nak yajka' nongakile'n na' diika' bzani beṉ' be'gake'n yoodo'na'. Na'ch che' Jesúza' ḻegake':
―Ka nak diiki chwiale ṉaa, wllin lla kwiayi' yogaan, ni sto yaj bich kwia koll' ljwellin.
Na'ch wṉabgakile' Jesúza', che'gake'ne': ―Maestro, ¿batran gak dga ba wno'? ¿Bera ka ile'into' gak kwenc̱he iṉezinto' nan ba zoa gaoshosh gakan?
Na'ch che' Jesúza' ḻegake': ―Ḻi wsak' bi we'le latj no siye' le'. Ḻa' beṉ' zan zi ichej gonzgake' ka nad', na' iṉazgake': “Nadaan Crístona'”, na' ḻekzka' iṉazgake': “Ba bllin lla kwiayi' yell-lioni.” Bi gonle ḻegake' txen.
Na' ka yenile chak no wdiḻ wa chtop chshag ljwell beṉ' kwenc̱he soshyi'gake' beṉ' wṉabia'ka', bi illeble. Chonan byen zigaate gak diiki, per aga lii tete c̱he yell-lioni kat' ba chakgakan.
Na'ch golle' ḻegake': ―Ganga kwe' wdiḻa' na' tiḻ yell kon yell.
Na' gak no bedxo' wal, na' gat' wbin, na' biya yillwe' kwe' lo yell-lioni, na' biya dii gak xan yabana' dii wwall wsheban beṉ'.
’Na' ka zi gak diiki, gox̱'gake' le' na' biya dii gongakile' le'. Na' lljwa'gake' le' gana' chdop chllagcho choe'ḻwill-cho Chioza' na' yiya yiyiljgake' le' na' koogake' le' lillya, na' lljwa'gake' le' lao beṉ' wṉabia' xenka' na' lao beṉ' wṉabia'ka' sto ni c̱ha'.
Na' kat' gak c̱hele ka', na'chlə gat' latj we'le cho'a xtillaana' lawe'ka'.
Na' bi sezle wṉeyi naklə iṉale kat' lljsele lao beṉ' wṉabia'ka',
ḻa' nad'kzan wzajniid' le' nakan iṉale na' goṉ' le' yeḻ' sin'na' kwenc̱he ni to beṉ'ka' chakzbangakile' le' bi sogakile' iṉagake' bi nakan ka nale.
Na' no x̱axṉa'tezle, no beṉ' bish'le, no dialla c̱hele, na' no beṉ' zoalenle wen gongake' le' lo na' beṉ' wṉabia'ka', na' witgake' baḻ-le.
Na' ax̱t yog'zə beṉ' gakzbangakile' le' daa nonḻilall'le nad'.
Per ḻi koo yic̱hjle, Chioza' gaklene' le' na' ni tlish' yish' yic̱hjlena' bi kwiayi'.
Na' shi sechale lawi daa yen ile'ile na' bi gakc̱hoplall'le, na'chan gat' to yeḻ' mban c̱hele dii bi te c̱heyin.
’Na' kat' ile'ile nec̱hj soldadka' Jerusalénni, kanan' iṉezile nan ba zoa kwiayi'n.
Na'ch beṉ'ka' lle' gani mbani Judeani, chiyaḻ' wxoṉjgake' lljakwash'gake' do yaa yaoka', na' beṉ'ka' lle' yelli, chiyaḻ' wxoṉjgake', na' beṉ'ka' zej lyix̱aa, bichoklə yiyedgake' yelli.
Ḻa' kanan' gon Chioza' yeḻ' zi' c̱he yog'ze' kwenc̱he yillinin doxen ka na Cho'a Xtilleena'.
¡Nyesh'laz wal gak c̱he noolka' noa' na' noolka' chwall' chx̱op llana' gak diiki! Ḻa' dii xen daa yen ile'i beṉ' Israelki.
Baḻgake' guet lo wdiḻa' na' zi baḻe' wc̱he'gake' pres yell zit'ka'. Na' beṉ' zit'ka' wlej wshoshjgake' yell Jerusalénni ax̱t kat'ch illin lla yiyoll yido ka llia bia' gongake'.
’Na' lo wbilla', lo bewaa na'ch lo beljka' gak dii gonan ka yibani beṉ'. Na' beṉ'ka' lle' yell-lioni gakshejlall'gake' na' illebgake' kat' gon nisdo'na' sshag wal daa so' kwe'n.
Na' ax̱t ic̱hoḻ-lall' beṉ' daa chllebgake' kwiayi'lengake' yell-lioni, ḻa' ax̱t yog' diika' llia xan yabana' iṉibgakan.
Na'ch ile'gakile' nad', Beṉ' Bseḻ' Chioza' Yell-lioni, zizaa to lo bej kon yeḻ' wak xen na' balaaṉ xen.
Na' kat' solo gak diiki, ḻi wtipch lall'le, ḻa' ba zoa gaoshosh yidsla' len'.
Na' ḻekzka' bsees' Jesúza' to jempl chi'e: ―Ḻi wwiakachi yag yix̱wewa' wa bichlə yag.
Kat' chle'ile ba chibia xḻaguiinka', chakbe'ile ba zoa yiyoo la'o linna'.
Ka'kzə, kat' ile'ile ba chak diiki ba wnia', chiyaḻ' iṉezile ba zoa gao wli' Chioza' yeḻ' wṉabia' c̱he'na'.
’Dii ḻi nia' le', aga ba wit beṉ'ka' zoa ṉaa kat' gak yog' diiki.
’Yabana' na' yell-lioni te c̱hegakin, san cho'a xtillaana' aga wde bi gak ka nan.
’Ḻi wsak' bi we'le latj sho' diika' wxiṉjan yic̱hjlall'do'lena'. Bi wḻanzle yeḻ' weezo, na' bi sezle wṉeyi bi chak c̱hele. Ḻi wsak' kwenc̱he aga sha c̱hel-le chon llana' zizaa.
Ḻa' tokonganzan gak diiki yen ile'i yog'te beṉ'ka' lle' doxen yell-lioni.
Na' le', ḻi se wṉeyi, ḻi iṉabi Chioza' toshiizi gaklene' le' kwenc̱he yilale lao yog' diiki llia bia' gak, na' kwenc̱he bi gall illeble sele lawa'na', nad', Beṉ' Bseḻ' Chioza' Yell-lioni.
Na' Jesúza' bli' bsedile' beṉ' yog' lla yoodo'na', na' ka chaḻ, chjagaaṉe' lo Yaa Olívoza'.
Na' yog' zil yog' beṉ' chajgake' yoodo'na' chjazenaggake' daa chli' chsedile'.
Ba zoa gaozə lṉi Paskwa' kat' chaogake' yetxtil daa bi nc̱hix̱ levadúrana'.
Na' bx̱ozka' chṉabia' len beṉ'ka' chli' chsedi leya' chiyiljlall'gake' naklə gongake' witgake' Jesúza' ka kono gakbe'i, ḻa' bllebgake' shi bi goni beṉ' wlall c̱he'ka' ḻegake'.
Na'ch x̱an dii x̱iw'ka' daa le Satanás wyoon ḻoo yic̱hjlall'do' Jud Scariota', beena' nak txen beṉ'ka' shlliṉ.
Na' wyaje' lao bx̱ozka' chṉabia' len lao beṉ'ka' ngoo lall' na' beṉ'ka' chap yoodo'na', na' bi'e dill' nakan gone' Jesúza' lall' na'gake'.
Na' ḻe bibagakile' na' bc̱hebgake' we'gake'ne' mech.
Na'ch bc̱hebe' gone'ne' lall' na'gake'. Na' wzolo chinoe' batan gat' latj kat' kono beṉ' lle' gone' Jesúza' lall' na'gake'.
Na' bllin llana' chsini'agake' c̱he lṉina', llana' chzolo chaogake' yetxtil daa bi' nc̱hix̱ levadúrana' na' chitgake' to xil'do', bana' gaogake' lle' Paskwa'.
Na'ch wlej Jesúza' Pédrona' len Juanna' na' chi'e ḻegake': ―Ḻi lljasini'a daa gaocho lṉi Paskwi.
Na'ch che'gake'ne': ―¿Garan cheenilo' lljasini'anto'n?
Na' che' Jesúza' ḻegake': ―Ka sho'le Jerusalénna', na' ile'ile to beṉ' byo zino'e to chee nis, na' ḻi lljanoe' ax̱t yoona' gana' yilline'.
Na' ye'le x̱an yoona': “Maestrona' chṉabile' li': ¿Garan zoa yoona' wyoone' gana' gaolene' beṉ'ka' nakgake'ne' txen lle' Paskwi?”
Na' wliile' le' to yoo xen dii llia shkwiana' cha'lə ga ba nonshao'tie'. Nan' wsini'ale daa gaocho xshe'na'.
Na' wloogake' nez zejgake', na' kon kayeṉ' golle' ḻegake' gok. Na' bsini'agake' daa wdaogake' lle' lṉi Paskwa'.
Na' ka goḻ' gaogake' xshe'na', Jesúza' wche'lene' postl c̱he'ka' cho'a mesa'.
Na'ch chi'e ḻegake': ―Ba goklall'chga' yeej gaolen' le' lṉi Paskwi ṉaa biṉ' witgake' nad'.
Na' ba nia' le', zeelo ṉaa cheej chaw' dga. Bichga yeej gawa'n ax̱t ki illin llana' wli' Chioza' yeḻ' wṉabia' xen c̱he'na', kana'ch yeej gawa'n dii yoblə.
Na' bex̱ee kopa' na' bi'e Chioza' yeḻ' chox̱ken, na' chi'e: ―Ḻi gox̱' dga, ḻi yeejan lat' wej.
Na' nia' le', bichga yeej' nis uvani ax̱t ki illin lla wli' Chioza' yeḻ' wṉabia' xen c̱he'na'.
Na'ch bex̱ee yetxtila' na' bi'e yeḻ' chox̱ken Chioza'. Na' bxoxje'n bi'en ḻegake' kwenc̱he wdaogake'n, na' chi'e: ―Dgan kwerp c̱ha'ni, chzanlallidaan ni c̱hele. Kin gonle kwenc̱he lljadinile nad'.
Na' ḻekzka' bene' ka wde wdaogake' xshe'na', bex̱ee kopa' sto shii, na'ch chi'e: ―Dga yoll ḻoo kopi zejin xc̱hen'na' daa ḻaljə ni c̱hele daa gonan ka gakḻi dii koba' bc̱heb Chioza' gone'.
’Na' ṉaa, beena' gone' nad' lo na' beṉ'ka' chakzi'gakile' nad' chi'lene' nad' cho'a mesi.
Ḻa' ba bllin lla gak ka nak daa llia bia' gak c̱ha', nad', Beṉ' Bseḻ' Chioza' Yell-lioni, per ¡nyesh'laz gak c̱he beena' gone' nad' lo na' beṉ' malka'!
Na'ch beṉ'ka' nakgake'ne' txen wzologake' chṉabi ljwellgake' noen' gone'ne' lo na' beṉ'ka'.
Na' ḻekzka' chakdiḻ-len ljwellgake' nogaken' nak beṉ' zak'chi.
Na' che' Jesúza' ḻegake': ―Zoa beṉ' wṉabia' to to nación, na' chongake' byen chzenag beṉ' c̱hegake', na' nagake' c̱he kwingake' ḻe chaklengake' beṉ'.
San le', bi chiyaḻ' gonle ka'. Shi nole nakle beṉ' zakii, chiyaḻ' wc̱hek' yic̱hjle ka to bi' xkwid', na' shi nole chṉabia', chiyaḻ' gonle ka nottezə beṉ' wen mandad.
¿Noran nak beṉ' zak'chi?, ¿abeena' chbe' cho'a mesa' chawe'?, ¿anti beena' chon mandadan', lla? Beena' chi' cho'a mesan' nake' beṉ' zak'chi. San nad', ḻa'kzi naktia' x̱anle, zoa' ladjleni ka to beṉ' wen mandad c̱hele.
’Le' ba wzoalenle nad' lao yog'te daa ba gok c̱ha'.
Na' daan, goṉ' le' yeḻ' wṉabia'na' ka daa beṉ X̱a'na' nad'.
Na' yeej gaolenle nad' gana' iṉabi'a. Na' kwe'le gana' iṉabia'le yizi'le kwent c̱he shlliṉ kwen beṉ'ka' nak xiiṉ dia c̱he dii Israela'.
Na' ḻekzka' golle' Simón Pédrona': ―Simón, Simón, Satanáza', daa chṉabia' dii x̱iw'ka', ba wṉaban le' gakle lo na'yin kwenc̱he gondinj gonganin le'.
Na' nad' ba wṉabid' Chioza' gaklene' li', Simón, kwenc̱he gonḻilall'cho nad'. Na' kat' ba biyajilo' c̱heyi daa gono', na' gakleno' beṉ'ki nako' txen kwenc̱he soac̱hec̱hgake' gonḻilall'gake' nad'.
Na' che' Simónna': ―X̱an', ba nc̱hoglallaa ḻaa lillyana' sa'len' li' wa ax̱t guetlen' li' txen.
Na' che' Jesúza': ―Pedro, nia' li', ṉaanlle' shoṉ shii bi wc̱hebo' shi nombi'o nad' ka zi' kwell shikwteza'.
Na'ch che' Jesúza' ḻegake': ―¿Azyalljile bi byalljile kana' bseḻaa le' na' bibi bex̱'le, ni ga koo xalaanle, ni mech na' ni xel-le? Na' che'gake': ―Bibi byalljinto'.
Na'ch golle': ―Per ṉaach nia' le', shi de ga chgoo xalaanle, ḻi gox̱aan, na' shi de xmechle, ḻi wa'n; na' shi nole bi de spad c̱hele, ḻi lljayet' xalena' na' ḻi si' tlisha'n.
Nia' le', chonan byen gak c̱ha' kon ka na Cho'a Xtill' Chioza' gana' na: “Gongakile'ne' ka chongakile' to beṉ' wen dii mal.”
Na' che'gake': ―X̱an', ni napnto' c̱hop spad. Na' chi'e: ―Lliz ḻi soachoklə.
Na'ch biza' Jesúza', na' kon ka yooloe' chone' biyaje' lo Yaa Olívoza', na' zjano beṉ'ka' nakgake'ne' txen.
Na' ka bllingake' latja', na' chi'e ḻegake': ―Ḻi we'ḻwill Chioza' kwenc̱he bi we'zle latj gon beli chenna' le' gan.
Na' bkwase' kwite'ka', ka to ga zeelo chllin to yaj dii chzaḻ'cho, na'ch bc̱hek' xibe'na' be'ḻwille' Chioza'.
Na' golle': ―X̱a, shi li' cheenilo', bislagach nad' lawi dga ba zoa idiḻ illag'; per aga gak ka cheenid', san gak ka cheenilo'.
Na'ch bli'lao to anjl beṉ' za' yabana' ḻe', na' biyo'ene' fuerz.
Na' daa ḻe chakyesh'chgaile', zizikli be'ḻwillche' Chioza' ax̱t biyaklolje'. Na' nis yes c̱he'na' daa chxop lo yona' nakan ka to bllon wej chen.
Biyoll be'ḻwille' Chioza', na' bizollee biyaje' gana' lle' beṉ'ka' nakgake'ne' txen, na' ka billine' kwite'ka' ba chesgake' daa chakyesh'gakile'.
Na' chi'e ḻegake': ―¿Berac̱he cheszle? Ḻi c̱has na' ḻi we'ḻwill Chioza' kwenc̱he bi we'zle latj gon beli chenna' le' gan.
Ni choe'te Jesúza' dill', ka bllin beṉ' zan, na' beena' le Jud, beena' nak txen beṉ'ka' shlliṉ, nc̱hi'e ḻegake'. Na' ka blline' jabiguee kwit Jesúza' na' bnope' x̱agueena'.
Na'ch che' Jesúza'ne': ―Jud, ¿akon dga bnopo' nad' chono' nad', Beṉ' Bseḻ' Chioza' Yell-lioni, lo na' beṉ'ki?
Na' beṉ'ka' lle'len Jesúza', ka ble'gakile' ka ba chak c̱he', na'ch gollgake'ne': ―X̱an', ¿awṉiayinto' spadki?
Na' toe' lii wdintie'n to mos c̱he bx̱oz choo bx̱oz xenna' bc̱hogtie' nague' de shḻina'.
Na' che' Jesúza': ―Bich bi gonile beṉ'ka'. Na'ch bida' Jesúza' nag beena'.
Na' daa bllin bx̱ozka' chṉabia' len beṉ'ka' chap yoodo'na', na' beṉ' golka' chṉabia', kwenc̱he gox̱'gake'ne', chi'e ḻegake': ―¿Berac̱he za'zle nox̱'le yag na' spad kwenc̱he zidṉizle nad' ka to no beṉ' wban?
Yog' lla wzoa' ladjlena' yoodo'na' na' bi bex̱'le nad'. Per ṉaach bllin lla gonle ka cheenile na' ṉaayeṉ' chṉabia' dii mala' daa chṉabia' gana' shgasj shc̱hoḻ.
Na'ch bṉizgake' Jesúza' na' bc̱he'gake'ne' lill bx̱oz choo bx̱oz xenna', na' zit' zit'lə zjano Pédrona'ne'.
Na' bxengake' yi'na' lesh' chyoo c̱he bx̱oz choo bx̱oz xenna' na' wche'gake' cho'a yi'na', na' wlen Pédrona' ḻegake'.
Na' to noolə wen mandad, ka ble'ile' chi' Pédrona' cho'a yi'na', lii wzetie' chwie'ne', na' chi'e: ―Ḻekzka' len beenin nake' Jesúza' txen.
Na' Pédrona' aga bc̱hebe', na' chi'ene': ―Noolə, aga nombi'a beena'.
Na' gokzə xtit bizle'i beṉ' yoblə Pédrona' na' chizi'ene': ―Ḻekzka' lenon' nako' beṉ'ka' txen. Na' Pédrona' chi'ene': ―Bi len' nak' beṉ'ka' txen.
Na' wizak ka do zi' tgor na' wize' sto beṉ' yoblə: ―Dii ḻikzan len beeni nake' txen Jesúza' ḻa' ḻekzka' beṉ' Galilean.
Na'ch che' Pédrona'ne': ―¡Ni bi ṉezid' bi dillaan choo! Na' ni che'telə Pédrona' ka', ka wchell to shikwtez.
Na'ch biyec̱hj X̱ancho Jesúza' bwie' Pédrona', na' Pédrona' jadinile' daa golle'ne', kana' chi'e: “Ṉaanlle' shoṉ shii bi wc̱hebo' shi nombi'o nad' ka zi' kwell shikwteza'.”
Na' bichej Pédrona' gana' lle' beṉ'ka' na' wchellyeshee.
Na'ch beṉ'ka' chapgake' Jesúza' btitjgakile'ne' na' wdap' wlall'gake'ne'.
Na' bsejgake' jalawe'na', na'ch wlall'gake'ne', che'gake'ne': ―¡Wnashki non wlall' li'!
Na' biya dii gollgake'ne' kwenc̱he gakile' zi'.
Na' ka wyeeni', bidop beṉ'ka' chṉabia' beṉ' Israelka', len bx̱ozka' chṉabia' na' beṉ'ka' chli' chsedi leya'. Na' bdegake' Jesúza' lawe'ka'. Na'ch wṉabgakile'ne', che'gake':
―Wnashki neto' shi li'kzan Crístona', beena' chbeznto'. Na' che' Jesúza': ―Shi iṉia' le': “Awe, nadaan”, aga wyajḻe'le c̱ha'.
Na' shi iṉabid' le' bi dii iṉabid' le', aga williilen na' ni bi yisanle nad', shi ṉaa.
Na' ṉaate, nad', Beṉ' Bseḻ' Chioza' Yell-lioni, kwi'a kwit de shḻi c̱he Chioza', beena' nap yeḻ' wak xenna'.
Na'ch yog'ze' wṉabgakile'ne': ―¿Ana' lin' nako' Xiiṉ Chioza'? Na'ch che' Jesúza': ―Awe, shḻikzan ba wnale.
Na'ch che' ljwellgake': ―Kochno chyalljicho gawe' xya c̱he beeni. Kwintekzcho ba benicho ka ba wne'.
Na'ch yog'ḻoḻ beṉ'ka' bizolla'gake' na' jwa'gake' Jesúza' lao Pilátona'.
Na'ch wzologake' chaogake' xya c̱he Jesúza', che'gake': ―Ba bidoḻinto' beeni chta chṉie' beṉ' wlall c̱hento'ka'. Chi'e bi chiyaḻ' c̱hixjcho daa chṉab Césara', beena' chṉabia', na' ḻekzka' naze' nake' Crístona', na' daa ne' ka' zejin nake' to beṉ' wṉabia'.
Na'ch wṉabi Pilátona' Jesúza', chi'ene': ―¿Alin' nako' beṉ' wṉabia' c̱he beṉ' Israelki? Na'ch che' Jesúza'ne': ―Kan' nakan.
Na'ch che' Pilátona' bx̱ozka' chṉabia' na' yog' beṉ'ka' lle' na': ―Ni to dii mal bi chillelid' chon beeni.
Na' zizikchli che'gake': ―Diika' chli' chsedile' chta chṉen yog'ḻoḻ beṉ' lle' doxen lallnto'ni. Wzoloze' Galileana', na' ax̱t Judeani ba bide'.
Ka gollgake' Pilátona' ka', na'ch wṉabile' ḻegake' shi nak Jesúza' beṉ' Galilea.
Na' ka wṉezile' nake' beṉ' Galilea, na'ch bdie'ne' lao Heródeza', beena' nḻane' chṉabi'e Galileana', ḻa' kana'yeṉ' zoa Heródeza' Jerusalénna'.
Na' ḻe bibayi Heródeza' ka ble'ile' Jesúza', ḻa' ba wlla cheenile' ile'ile'ne' daa ba benile' choe' beṉ' xtilleena'. Na' goki Heródeza' ile'ile' gone' to yeḻ' wak.
Na' biya dii wṉabile' Jesúza', na' ni to daa wṉabile'ne' bi billi'e.
Na' ḻekzka' na' lle' bx̱ozka' chṉabia' len beṉ'ka' chli' chsedi leya', na' zizikli chaogake' xya c̱he Jesúza'.
Na'ch Heródeza' len soldad c̱he'ka' biya dii bengakile'ne', na' btitjgakile'ne' bwakwgake'ne' to lech' ka daa chakw to beṉ' wṉabia'. Na'tech bizseḻ' Heródeza'ne' lao Pilátona'.
Na' lo llana' bizoalen Pilátona' Heródeza' wen, ḻa' kana'te chakzbani ljwelle'.
Na'ch biti'a Pilátona' bx̱ozka' chṉabia', na' beṉ'ka' chṉabia'gake' beṉ' Israelka' na'ch beṉ' yell,
na' golle' ḻegake': ―Le' bidwa'le beeni lawii, nale chta chṉie' beṉ', na' nad' ba wṉabidee laoleni, na' bi chillelid' ni to daa nale c̱he' shi ḻi ka chone'n.
Na' ni Heródeza' bi billelile' shi bi doḻ' nap beeni, na' ba bizseḻeene' laochoni. Na' ba ble'teile aga bi bene' iṉacho wc̱hoglozcho guete'.
Na' ṉaa gon' mandad wit c̱hingake'ne' na'tech yisanee.
Na' ka chakz yog' yiz, chiyaḻ' yisane' to beena' nej lillyana' kat' chaḻ' lṉi Paskwa'.
Na' yog' beṉ'ka' ndop nllag na', wzologake' chosyaagake', che'gake': ―¡Guettega beeni! ¡Na' bisan Barrabáza'!
Nyix̱jgake' Barrabáza' lillyana' daa bx̱ie' wdiḻa' yell Jerusalénna', na' bettie' to beṉ'.
Na' daa cheeni Pilátona' yisane' Jesúza', na' stokzə wṉabile' beṉ'ka' shi wisane'ne'.
Na' beṉ'ka' zizikchli chosyaagake', che'gake': ―¡Bdee ḻee yag cruza'! ¡Bdee ḻee yag cruza'!
Na' de wyoṉ shiyi che' Pilátona' ḻegake': ―¿Bera dii malan' ṉezile ba ben beeni, lla? Bi chillelid' ni to dii mal dii ba bene' kwenc̱he guete'. Gonch' mandad wit c̱hingake'ne' na'tech yisanee.
Na' beṉ'ka' wzeyidgake' chosyaagake' chṉabgakile'ne' wdeene' ḻee yag cruza'. Na' daa wzeyidgake' chosyaagake', bengake' gan wzoa xtilleeka'.
Na' bc̱hoglall' Pilátona' gone' ka cheeni beṉ'ka'.
Na' bisane' beena' wṉabgake', beena' de lillyana' daa bx̱ie' wdiḻa' na' daa bettie' to beṉ'. Na' bene' Jesúza' lo na'gake' kwenc̱he gongakile'ne' ka chaklall'gake'.
Na' ka nc̱he'gake' Jesúza' lljada'gake'ne' ḻee yag cruza', billaggake' to beṉ' Cirene lie' Simón zizee lyix̱aa. Na' bex̱'gake'ne' bwa'gake'ne' yag cruz c̱he Jesúza' na'ch janoe'ne'.
Na' beṉ' zan zjanogake'ne', na' zan noolka' chbellgake' na' chosyaagake' ni c̱he Jesúza'.
Na' biyec̱hj Jesúza' bwie' ḻegake' na' golle': ―Le' nool Jerusalén, bi kwellzle c̱ha'; ḻi kwell c̱he kwinle na' c̱he xiiṉleka'.
Ḻa' wllin lla kat' iṉa beṉ': “Chakomba nool willka', beṉ'ka' bi wxan na' bi bwall bx̱opgake'.”
Na'ch beṉ'ka' zoa llana' gak ka', solo iṉagake': “Sheḻ' iyiṉjtega yaa yaoki idakwtegan neto'.”
Shi yag yaa yag banna' chongakile'n kon daa nazan c̱hegake', ¿alechla ki gongakile' yag billa'?
Na' ḻekzka' nc̱he'gake' c̱hop beṉ' wen dii mal kwenc̱he witgake' ḻegake' txen len Jesúza'.
Na' ka bllingake' latja' gana' le Llit Yic̱hj Beṉ' Wet, bda'gake' Jesúza' ḻee yag cruza'. Na' ḻekzka' bda'gake' c̱hopte beṉ' wen dii malka' shḻaa wej kwite'na'.
Na' ka chda'gake' Jesúza' ḻee yag cruza', chi'e: ―X̱a, wxi'xen c̱hegake', ḻa' aga ṉezgakile' bin chongake'. Na' soldadka' bengake' to wyitj kwenc̱he wṉezgakile' nogake' yidoḻ' xe'na'.
Na' lle' beṉ' zan chwiagake', na' ax̱t beṉ'ka' chṉabia'gake' beṉ' Israelka' btitjgakile'ne', nagake': ―Gok bisle' beṉ' yoblə, na' ṉaa yislashki kwine' shi leile' ḻen' Crístona', beena' ba wlej Chioza'.
Na' ḻekzka' soldadka' btitjgakilene', na' jabig'gake' kwit yag cruza' gana' nda'gake'ne' na' bshabgakile'ne' to vino dii nak zic̱hj zḻa'.
Na' che'gake'ne': ―Shi lin' nako' beṉ' wṉabia' c̱he beṉ' Israelki, bislashki kwino'.
Na' yic̱hj yag cruz c̱he'na' bda'gake' to dii cho'en dill' bic̱he nda'gake'ne' ḻee yag cruza', nan: “Beenin beṉ' wṉabia' c̱he beṉ' Israelka'.” Bzejgake'n dill' griego, dill' latín na' dill' hebreo.
Na' to beṉ' wen dii mala', beena' da' kwit Jesúza', biya dii golle'ne', chi'ene': ―Shi lin' Crístona', Beena' Bseḻ' Chioza' iṉabia', bislashki kwino' na' ḻekzka' bisla neto'.
Na' beena' sto bsheshlene'ne', chi'e: ―¿Abikzə chall chlleblatoo Chioza'?, len kon ka chak c̱hen' ba chak c̱ho'.
Cho', ka chiyaḻ'kz gak c̱hechon' kwenc̱he c̱hixjcho c̱he dii mala' daa bencho; san beeni aga bi dii mal bene'.
Na'ch golle' Jesúza': ―Jesús, lljadingachilo' nad' kat'ka' solo iṉabi'o.
Na'ch che' Jesúza'ne': ―Dii ḻi nia' li', ṉaanlla soaleno' nad' latja' gana' nak mbalaz.
Na' do ka gobill bic̱hoḻ doxen yell-liona', bllinte do ka chida shoṉ,
daa bich bzeeni' wbilla'. Na' lechaa ze ḻoo yoodo'na' bllon' gokan c̱hop ḻaalə.
Na'ch besyaa Jesúza' zilljə, chi'e: ―X̱a, chiyon' bishbe c̱ha'ni lall' noo. Na' biyoll golle' ka' na'ch wite'.
Na' ka ble'i beena' chṉabia' soldadka' diika' gok, be'lawee Chioza', chi'e: ―Dii ḻi beeni nake' dowalj beṉ' wen.
Na' yog' beṉ'ka' lle' na', ka ble'gakile' ka gok, ziyajgake' chball'gake' cho'alc̱ho'eka'.
Na' yog' beṉ'ka' nombia'gake' Jesúza', do noolka' za'lengake'ne' ax̱t Galileana', wzegake' zit'lə chwiagake' ka gok.
Wzoa to beṉ' wlie' José, beṉ' yell Arimatea, daa mbani Judéana'. Na' Joséna' nake' txen beṉ'ka' chṉabia' beṉ' Israelka'. Nake' to beṉ' wen na' to beṉ' chon ka cheeni Chioza',
na' zoe' chbeze' wseḻ' Chioza' beena' iṉabia'. Na' Joséna' aga wyoolallee ka ben beṉ'ka' chṉabia'lene' daa betgake' Jesúza', na' bi benlene' ḻegake' txen.
Na'ch wyaje' lao Pilátona' na' wṉabe' lsens yiḻetje' kwerp c̱he Jesúza'.
Na' biḻetje'ne' ḻee yag cruza', na'ch bitobe'ne' to lech' xen na' jḻo'ene' to ḻoo blej daa benshawee, ga biṉ' wkash'gake' ni tlish' beṉ' wet.
Na' llana' gok diiki nakan lla chsini'a beṉ' Israelka' c̱hegake' kwenc̱he bibi llin gongake' lla sabda', llana' chombaaṉgake', na' zi lat'zə chyallj solo llana' chombaaṉgake'.
Na' noolka' za'lengake' Jesúza' ax̱t Galileana', wyajgake' jawiagake' bleja' na' jale'gakile' nak wdix̱jgake' kwerp c̱he'na'.
Na'ch biza'gake', na' ka billingake' gana' zoagake', benshao'gake' daa chḻa' zix̱. Na' bizi'lall'gake' lla sabda' kon ka na leya'.
Na' lla necha' chizolo xmanna', wizaj noolka' ni baḻ cho'a bana', nox̱'gake' diika' chḻa' zix̱ daa benshao'gake', na' wyaj zi baḻ noolə yoblə kon ḻegake'.
Na' ble'gakile' aga chi'ch yaja' cho'a bana'.
Na' wyoogake' ḻoo bleja', na' ble'gakile' aga bich bi kwerp c̱he X̱ancho Jesúza' de na'.
Na' shlak chakgakile' bera zejin dga, kat'kzali ble'gakile' c̱hop beṉ' byo, nakwgake' lech' dii chey cheeni', zegake' kwite'ka'.
Na' noolka' bllebchgagake' na' bc̱hek' yic̱hje'ka' ax̱t lo yona'. Na'ch beṉ'ka' zena' che'gake': ―¿Berac̱he chiyiljzle beena' mban ladj beṉ' wetki?
Kochno de ni. Ba bibane' ladj beṉ' wetki. Ḻi lljadini daa wne' le' kana' zoalene' le' Galileana'.
Wne' chonan byen Beena' Bseḻ' Chioza' Yell-lioni gake' lo na' beṉ' malka', na' witgake'ne' ḻee yag cruza', na' ka yiyoṉ lla yibane' ladj beṉ' wetka'.
Na'ch jadini noolka' daa goll Jesúza' ḻegake'.
Na' biza'gake' biyajgake' gana' lle' postlka' shnej len yog' beṉ'ka' sto gokgake'ne' txen, na' be'gake' dill' yog' daa gok c̱hegake'.
